<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Controls, Tell-tales, Indicators and Sources of Illumination (Standard&#xA0;101)</span>
</h3>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Interpretation</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>101</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(1)ID0EBR0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of this section, <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>control</dfn>
</span> has the same meaning as in <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;101, Controls, Tell-tales, Indicators and Sources of Illumination</cite> (TSD&#xA0;101).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">General</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(2)ID0EBP0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every vehicle that is required by section&#xA0;5 of these Regulations to conform to the standards set out in this section shall, in respect of the controls, tell-tales, indicators and sources of illumination that are fitted in the occupant compartment, conform to the requirements of TSD&#xA0;101, as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;101</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)ID0EMN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S5.2.1 of TSD&#xA0;101,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBKN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if the left turn signal and the right turn signal each have their own control or tell-tale, the arrows in the symbol required for the turn signals control or tell-tale may be disassociated and each arrow may be used separately as a distinct symbol;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBJN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if the left turn signal and the right turn signal each have their own tell-tale and the arrows in the symbol required for the turn signals tell-tale are disassociated so that each arrow is used separately as a distinct symbol, the simultaneous flashing of the left and right turn signal tell-tales may be used as the hazard warning signal tell-tale;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(c)ID0EDIN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(<em>c</em>)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the identification of a control set out below is not required if the control is combined with the master lighting switch:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(c)subp-(i)ID0EBBIN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the control for the tail lamps, parking lamps, licence plate lamps, side marker lamps, identification lamps and clearance lamps, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(c)subp-(ii)ID0EBAIN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the headlamp lower beam control;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(d)ID0EBHN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(<em>d</em>)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if a single tell-tale is used to indicate more than one brake system condition, only the symbol required for the brake system malfunction shall be used;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(e)ID0EDGN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the identification of a control set out below is not required if the control is an integral part of the key-locking system of the vehicle:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(e)subp-(i)ID0EBBGN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the engine start control, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(e)subp-(ii)ID0EBAGN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the engine stop control;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(f)ID0EBFN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(<em>f</em>)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the identification required for the drive position of the automatic transmission control may be replaced by a letter, a number, a combination of letters and numbers, or any symbol that is not set out in column&#xA0;2 of the table to this section;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(g)ID0EBEN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(<em>g</em>)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the symbol required for the engine start control may be replaced by the word &#x201C;start&#x201D;;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(h)ID0EBDN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(h)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the symbol required for the engine stop control may be replaced by the word &#x201C;stop&#x201D;;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(i)ID0EBCN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the symbol required for the electronic stability control system malfunction tell-tale may be replaced by the abbreviation &#x201C;ESC&#x201D;;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(j)ID0EBBN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(j)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the symbol required for the electronic stability control system off control and tell-tale may be replaced by the abbreviation &#x201C;ESC OFF&#x201D;; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(3)p-(k)ID0EBAN0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(k)</span>
</a>&#xA0;until August&#xA0;31, 2018, the symbol required for the passenger air bag deactivated control and tell-tale may be replaced by the words &#x201C;passenger air bag off&#x201D; or &#x201C;pass air bag off&#x201D;.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Speedometers and Odometers</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(4)ID0EBL0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A speedometer shall indicate the speed of the vehicle in kilometres per hour or in kilometres per hour and miles per hour. The unit or units of measurement shall be identified on the speedometer or at a location adjacent to it.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(5)ID0EBK0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A speedometer shall be illuminated whenever the headlamps are activated, unless the headlamps are being flashed for signalling purposes or are being operated as daytime running lamps.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(6)ID0EBJ0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;An odometer or trip odometer shall indicate distances in kilometres or in miles. If the distances are indicated in miles, that unit of measurement shall be identified at a location adjacent to the odometer or trip odometer.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Passenger Air Bag Deactivated Tell-tale</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(7)ID0EDH0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The tell-tale indicating that the passenger air bag has been deactivated shall be fitted in the interior of the vehicle</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(7)p-(a)ID0EBBH0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;forward of and above the seating reference point of each front outboard designated seating position when the seat is in its forwardmost position; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(7)p-(b)ID0EBAH0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in such a manner that the tell-tale, when alight, is visible to the driver and any front passenger when they are restrained by seat belts that are adjusted in accordance with the vehicle manufacturer&#x2019;s instructions.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(8)ID0EDG0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite subsection&#xA0;(7), the tell-tale indicating that the passenger air bag has been deactivated</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(8)p-(a)ID0EBBG0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;shall not be fitted at or adjacent to a location that can serve for storage if an object stored at that location will obstruct the tell-tale from the view of the driver and any front passenger when they are restrained by seat belts that are adjusted in accordance with the vehicle manufacturer&#x2019;s instructions; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(8)p-(b)ID0EBAG0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;shall not be fitted at a location where the tell-tale will not be completely visible to the driver when the driver is restrained by a seat belt that is adjusted in accordance with the vehicle manufacturer&#x2019;s instructions and a rearward-facing child restraint system or an infant restraint system is installed in the forwardmost right outboard designated seating position.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Owner&#x2019;s Manual</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(9)ID0EBE0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The English and French versions of the owner&#x2019;s manual shall contain an explanation of every symbol, word, abbreviation or letter used to identify a control, tell-tale or indicator that is fitted in the vehicle and is required to be identified under this section.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Transitional Provision</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-(10)ID0EBC0LE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Until September&#xA0;1, 2019, a vehicle referred to in subsection&#xA0;(2) may conform to the requirements of this section as it read on the day before the day on which this subsection came into force.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-101ss-ID0ECB0LE0BA">

<th id="t608h63" headers="t608h0 t608h6" class="borderRight borderBottom">Windshield defrosting and defogging system</th>

<div class="imageGroup">

<td headers="t608h0 t608h6 t608h63 t608h2 t608h8" class="borderRight borderBottom">

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Transmission Control Functions (Standard&#xA0;102)</span>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>[SOR/97-421, s. 3]</li>
</ul>
</div>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>102</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(1)ID0EDJ0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Any automatic transmission fitted on a vehicle shall have</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(1)p-(a)ID0EEBJ0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;its control positions in such a sequence that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBCBJ0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;movement between any forward and reverse drive position may be made only through a neutral position,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBBBJ0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a steering-column-mounted control, movement from the neutral position to any forward drive position may be made in a clockwise direction only, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBABJ0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the park position, if included in the sequence, is located at the end of the sequence adjacent to the reverse drive position; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(1)p-(b)ID0EBAJ0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;one forward drive position that, in vehicles having more than one forward transmission gear ratio, provides a greater degree of engine braking than the highest speed transmission ratio at speeds below 40&#xA0;km/h.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(2)ID0EBI0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;On any vehicle equipped with an automatic transmission, a motor used for the vehicle&#x2019;s propulsion must not be started by setting the ignition switch to the position used to start the motor if the transmission control is in a forward or reverse drive position.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(2.1)ID0EBH0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If a passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck or three-wheeled vehicle has a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less and a transmission control sequence that includes a park position, the transmission control must not be capable of shifting from the park position to the forward or reverse drive position &#x2014; while a motor used for the vehicle&#x2019;s propulsion is in use &#x2014; unless the service brake pedal is depressed or the service brakes are otherwise engaged.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(3)ID0EDG0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(5), where the transmission control sequence includes a park position, the identification of the transmission control positions and the position selected shall be displayed in at least a single location in view of the driver when</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBBG0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the ignition switch is set to the position where the transmission can be shifted; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBAG0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the transmission control is not in the park position.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(4)ID0EBF0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(5), if the transmission control sequence does not include a park position, the identification of the transmission control positions and the position selected shall be displayed in at least a single location in view of the driver when the ignition switch is set to the position where the engine is capable of operation.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(5)ID0EBE0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The identification of transmission control positions need not be displayed when the ignition switch is set to the position used to start the vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(6)ID0EBD0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The identification of the transmission control positions and sequence, on vehicles equipped with a manual transmission, shall be permanently displayed in view of the driver.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(7)ID0EBC0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If a passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck or three-wheeled vehicle has a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less and is equipped with a manual transmission, a motor used for the vehicle&#x2019;s propulsion must not be started by setting the ignition switch to the position used to start the motor unless the clutch pedal is depressed or the drive train is otherwise disengaged.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-102ss-(8)ID0EBB0JE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In this section, <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>drive train</dfn>
</span> means the components that transfer motive power from the motor to the drive wheels.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/95-164, s. 4;</li>
<li> SOR/97-421, ss. 4, 22(F);</li>
<li> SOR/2003-189, s. 1;</li>
<li> SOR/2003-272, s. 34;</li>
<li> SOR/2006-94, s. 4(E);</li>
<li> SOR/2007-246, s. 2.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Windshield Defrosting and Defogging</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>103</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(1)ID0EGF0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In this section,</p>
<dl class="Definition">
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>critical area</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>critical area</dfn>
</span> means area C as referred to in section&#xA0;104 of this Schedule; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">zone critique</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>defog</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>defog</dfn>
</span> means to remove moisture from the inside surface of the glass; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">d&#xE9;sembuer</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>defrost</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>defrost</dfn>
</span> means to melt frost or ice on the inside or outside surface of the glass; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">d&#xE9;givrer</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>entire windshield</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>entire windshield</dfn>
</span> means area A as referred to in section&#xA0;104 of this Schedule; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">pare-brise tout entier</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>road load</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>road load</dfn>
</span> means the power output required to move the vehicle at the curb mass plus 180&#xA0;kg on level, clean, dry, smooth portland cement concrete pavement or other surface with an equivalent coefficient of surface friction at a specified speed through still air at 20&#xB0;C and a standard barometric pressure of 101.3&#xA0;kPa, and includes driveline friction, rolling friction and air resistance. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">charge de route</span>) </p>
</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(2)ID0EBE0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(2.1), every vehicle shall be equipped with a windshield defrosting and defogging system.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(2.1)ID0EBD0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A three-wheeled vehicle that is equipped with a windshield shall be equipped with a windshield defrosting and defogging system.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(3)ID0EDC0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In the case of a passenger car or a three-wheeled vehicle, the windshield defrosting and defogging system shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBBC0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;meet the requirements of section&#xA0;3 of SAE Recommended Practice J902 Passenger Car Windshield Defrosting Systems, (August 1964), when tested in accordance with paragraph&#xA0;(<em>b</em>) except that the areas referred to in that section as &#x201C;critical area&#x201D; and &#x201C;entire windshield&#x201D; shall be as referred to in subsection&#xA0;(1) of this section; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBAC0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be tested in accordance with such of the portions of paragraphs&#xA0;4.1 to 4.4.7 of SAE Recommended Practice J902, (August 1964), or SAE Recommended Practice J902<em>a</em>, (March 1967), as are applicable to that system.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(4)ID0EJB0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite the testing requirements set out in subsection&#xA0;(3) for the windshield defrosting and defogging system of a passenger car or three-wheeled vehicle,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EBHB0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a passenger car or three-wheeled vehicle equipped with a heating system other than a heat exchanger type that uses the engine&#x2019;s coolant as a means to supply the heat to the heat exchanger, the procedure specified by the vehicle&#x2019;s manufacturer for cold weather starting shall be followed during the entire test period, except that the use of a power or heat source external to the vehicle is not permitted;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EDGB0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of all other passenger cars and three-wheeled vehicles,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(4)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBGB0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;during the entire test period, the engine speed shall not exceed 1,500&#xA0;revolutions per minute in neutral gear or the engine speed and load shall not exceed the speed and load at 40&#xA0;km/h (25&#xA0;miles per hour) in the manufacturer&#x2019;s recommended gear with road load, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(4)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBAGB0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;during the first 5 minutes of the test period, the warm-up procedure recommended by the vehicle&#x2019;s manufacturer for cold weather starting shall be followed and during the last 35&#xA0;minutes of the test period, the procedure referred to in subparagraph&#xA0;(i) shall be followed;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(4)p-(c)ID0EBFB0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a room air change of 90&#xA0;times per hour is not required;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(4)p-(d)ID0EBEB0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the windshield wipers may be used during the test if they are operated without manual assistance;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(4)p-(e)ID0EBDB0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;one or two windows may be open a total of 25&#xA0;mm;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(4)p-(f)ID0EBCB0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the defroster blower may be turned on at any time;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(4)p-(g)ID0EBBB0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(g)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the wind velocity is at any level from 0 to 3&#xA0;km/h; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-103ss-(4)p-(h)ID0EBAB0HE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(h)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the test chamber temperature and the wind velocity shall be measured after the engine has been started, at the forwardmost point of the vehicle or a point 91.4&#xA0;cm (36&#xA0;inches) from the base of the windshield, whichever is farther forward, at a level halfway between the top and the bottom of the windshield on the vehicle centreline.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/97-264, s. 1;</li>
<li> SOR/2003-272, s. 8;</li>
<li> SOR/2008-104, s. 9.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Windshield Wiping and Washing System</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>104</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(1)ID0EIJ0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In this section,</p>
<dl class="Definition">
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>areas A, B and C</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>areas A, B and C</dfn>
</span> means the areas referred to in Column&#xA0;I of Tables&#xA0;I, II, III and IV to this section when established as shown in Figures&#xA0;1 and 2 of SAE Recommended Practice J903<em>a</em> Passenger Car Windshield Wiper Systems, (May 1966), using the angles specified in Columns&#xA0;III to VI of the above Tables; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">zones&#xA0;A, B et C</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>daylight opening</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>daylight opening</dfn>
</span> means the maximum unobstructed opening through the glazing surface as defined in paragraph&#xA0;2.3.12 of Section&#xA0;E, Ground Vehicle Practice, SAE Aerospace-Automotive Drawing Standards, (September 1963); (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">ouverture de jour</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>glazing surface reference line</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>glazing surface reference line</dfn>
</span> means the intersection of the glazing surface and a horizontal plane 635&#xA0;mm above the seating reference point, as shown in Figure&#xA0;1 of SAE Recommended Practice J903<em>a</em> (May 1966); (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">ligne de r&#xE9;f&#xE9;rence de la surface vitr&#xE9;e</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>overall width</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>overall width</dfn>
</span> means the maximum overall body width dimension W116 as defined in Section&#xA0;E, Ground Vehicle Practice, SAE Aerospace-Automotive Drawing Standards, (September 1963); (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">largeur hors tout</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>plan view reference line</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>plan view reference line</dfn>
</span> means, </p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(1)Definitionp-(a)ID0EBBCJ0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in respect of vehicles with a bench type front seat, a line parallel to the longitudinal centreline of the vehicle and outboard of the centre of the steering wheel by a distance equal to 0.15&#xA0;times the difference between one-half the shoulder room dimension and the steering wheel centre offset, as shown in Figure&#xA0;2 of SAE Recommended Practice J903<em>a</em>, (May 1966); and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(1)Definitionp-(b)ID0EDACJ0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in respect of vehicles with individual front seats,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(1)Definitionp-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBACJ0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a line parallel to the longitudinal centreline of the vehicle which passes through the centre of the driver&#x2019;s designated seating position, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(1)Definitionp-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBAACJ0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a line parallel to the longitudinal centreline of the vehicle located so that the geometric centre of the 95 per cent eye range contour is positioned on the longitudinal centreline of the driver&#x2019;s designated seating position; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">ligne de r&#xE9;f&#xE9;rence longitudinale</span>)</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>shoulder room dimension</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>shoulder room dimension</dfn>
</span> means the front shoulder room dimension W3 as defined in Section&#xA0;E, Ground Vehicle Practice, SAE Aerospace-Automotive Drawing Standards, (September 1963); (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">espace d&#x2019;&#xE9;paules</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>95 per cent eye range contour</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>95 per cent eye range contour</dfn>
</span> means the 95th percentile tangential cut-off specified in SAE Recommended Practice J941<em>a</em> Passenger Car Driver&#x2019;s Eye Range, (August 1967). (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">95 pour cent du contour de port&#xE9;e visuelle</span>) </p>
</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(2)ID0EBI0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of this section, the expressions &#x201C;manikin H-point&#x201D;, &#x201C;manikin H-point with seat in rearmost position&#x201D;, and &#x201C;H-point&#x201D; used in an SAE Standard or SAE Recommended Practice mean &#x201C;seating reference point&#x201D;.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(3)ID0EEH0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(3.1), every vehicle shall have a power-driven windshield wiping system that has at least two frequencies or speeds and that has, irrespective of engine speed and engine load,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBCH0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;one frequency or speed of at least 45&#xA0;cycles per minute;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBBH0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a difference of at least 15&#xA0;cycles per minute between the highest frequency or speed and one of the lower frequencies or speeds; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(3)p-(c)ID0EBAH0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the lower frequency or speed referred to in paragraph&#xA0;(<em>b</em>) equal to at least 20&#xA0;cycles per minute.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(3.1)ID0EBG0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A three-wheeled vehicle that is equipped with a windshield shall have a windshield wiping system that conforms to the requirements of subsection&#xA0;(3).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(4)ID0EBF0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Compliance with subsection&#xA0;(3) shall be demonstrated by testing under the conditions specified in sections&#xA0;4.1.1 and 4.1.2 of SAE Recommended Practice J903<em>a</em>, (May 1966).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(5)ID0EDE0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In the case of a passenger car or a three-wheeled vehicle, the windshield wiping system, when tested wet in accordance with SAE Recommended Practice J903a (May 1966), shall wipe the percentage of areas&#xA0;A, B and C of the windshield that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(5)p-(a)ID0EBBE0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;is specified in Column&#xA0;II of whichever of Tables&#xA0;I, II, III or IV to this section is applicable; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(5)p-(b)ID0EBAE0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;is within the area bounded by a perimeter line on the glazing surface 25&#xA0;mm from the edge of the daylight opening.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(6)ID0EDD0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(7), every vehicle shall have a windshield washing system that meets the requirements of SAE Recommended Practice J942, <cite class="XRefExternal">Passenger Car Windshield Washer Systems</cite> (November 1965), except that the words &#x201C;the effective wipe pattern defined in SAE J903, paragraph&#xA0;3.1.2&#x201D; in paragraph 3.1 of SAE Recommended Practice J942 shall be replaced</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(6)p-(a)ID0EBBD0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a passenger car or a three-wheeled vehicle, by the words &#x201C;the areas established in accordance with the definition of areas&#xA0;A, B and C in subsection&#xA0;(1) of Canada Motor Vehicle Safety Standard No.&#xA0;104&#x201D;; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(6)p-(b)ID0EBAD0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck or bus, by the words &#x201C;the pattern designed by the manufacturer for the windshield wiping system on the exterior surface of the windshield glazing&#x201D;.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-(7)ID0EBC0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A three-wheeled vehicle that is equipped with a windshield shall have a windshield washing system that meets the requirements of subsection&#xA0;(6).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-104ss-ID0EFB0FE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">
</span>
</a>&#xA0;</p>
<figure>

</th>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Hydraulic and Electric Brake Systems (Standard&#xA0;105)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>105</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-105ss-(1)ID0EBE0DE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to section&#xA0;135 of this Schedule, every multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck and bus shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No. 105, Hydraulic and Electric Brake Systems</cite> (TSD&#xA0;105), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-105ss-(2)ID0EBD0DE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;An indicator lamp referred to in S5.3 of TSD 105 shall, when activated due to a condition set out in S5.3.1 of TSD 105, display the identification symbol set out in the table to section 101 of this Schedule that corresponds to that condition, but if the vehicle is fitted with a single common indicator lamp, the lamp shall display the identification symbol for a brake system malfunction set out in the table to section 101 of this Schedule.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-105ss-(3)ID0EBC0DE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The statement set out in S5.4.3 of TSD&#xA0;105 may be replaced by another statement to the same effect.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-105ss-(4)_to_(6)ID0EBB0DE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4) to (6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2015-24, s. 4]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Brake Hoses (Standard&#xA0;106)</span>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>[SOR/93-561, s. 3;</li>
<li> SOR/2011-238, s. 1]</li>
</ul>

</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">

<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>106</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-106ss-(1)ID0EBD0BE0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every brake hose, brake hose assembly and brake hose end fitting with which a passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck, bus, three-wheeled vehicle, motorcycle, trailer, and trailer converter dolly are equipped shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;106, Brake Hoses</cite> (TSD&#xA0;106), as amended from time to time.</p>

<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>108</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(1)ID0EB0MC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck, bus, motorcycle and trailer shall be equipped with the lamps, retroreflective devices and associated equipment required by <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;108, Lamps, Reflective Devices and Associated Equipment</cite> (TSD 108), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(1.1)ID0EB0LC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every three-wheeled vehicle shall be equipped with the lamps, retroreflective devices and associated equipment required by TSD 108 for passenger cars.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(2)ID0EB0KC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every restricted-use motorcycle shall be equipped with the reflex reflectors required for motorcycles by S5.1.1 of TSD 108.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(3)ID0EB0JC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Lamps, retroreflective devices and associated equipment required by this section shall be designed, installed and visible in accordance with the requirements of TSD 108, except Figures&#xA0;11 to 14, 16, 18, 21 and 22.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(4)ID0EB0IC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Lamps, retroreflective devices and associated equipment on a vehicle may conform to the applicable SAE standards and recommended practices contained in the 1994 <cite class="XRefExternal">SAE Handbook</cite> instead of the applicable SAE standards and recommended practices referred to in this section or TSD 108.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(5)ID0ED0HC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;All the information regarding every type of bulb and every type of sealed beam lamp used in lighting equipment required by this section shall be</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(5)p-(a)ID0EEB0HC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;specified for the type of bulb or sealed beam lamp in</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(5)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBCB0HC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a standard or recommended practice issued by the SAE,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(5)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBBB0HC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a regulation issued by the ECE, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(5)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBAB0HC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a standard issued by the International Electrotechnical Commission (IEC); or</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(5)p-(b)ID0EBA0HC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;provided by the vehicle manufacturer to the Minister, at the Minister&#x2019;s request.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(6)ID0EB0GC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Wherever the word &#x201C;filament&#x201D; appears in this section, TSD 108 or an SAE standard or recommended practice, it may be read as &#x201C;arc&#x201D; if the requirement applies to a lamp in which light is produced by a gaseous discharge tube, or as &#x201C;light-emitting diode junction&#x201D; if the requirement applies to a lamp in which light is produced by a light-emitting diode.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(7)ID0EB0FC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of this section, the expression <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>motor driven cycle</dfn>
</span> used in TSD 108 means <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>limited-speed motorcycle</dfn>
</span>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;108</span>
</h3>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Required Motor Vehicle Lighting Equipment &#x2014; S5.1 of TSD 108</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(8)ID0EB0CC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S5.1.1 of TSD 108, lamps and retroreflective devices that are contained within the same physical assembly as a headlamp and conform to the requirements of S7.4(h) of TSD 108 in respect of resistance to corrosion, dust and humidity are not required to be subjected to the corrosion, dust and moisture tests required by any of the SAE standards or recommended practices listed in Tables&#xA0;I and III of TSD 108.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(9)ID0EB0BC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;[Reserved]</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(10)ID0EB0AC004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If reflective material referred to in S5.1.1.4 of TSD 108 is applied to a non-vertical surface, the entrance angle used to demonstrate that the material conforms to the performance standards prescribed by that section shall be the sum of the entrance angle specified in Table&#xA0;1 or Table&#xA0;1A of SAE Standard J594f, <cite class="XRefExternal">Reflex Reflectors</cite> (January 1977), and the angle, measured on the horizontal centreline of the material, by which the material deviates from the vertical.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(11)ID0EB06B004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;S5.1.1.12 and S5.1.1.21 of TSD 108 do not apply.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(12)ID0EB05B004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S5.1.1 and S7.9 of TSD 108, every headlamp assembly on a motorcycle shall conform to S7.8.2, S7.8.2.2, S7.8.3, S7.8.4 and S7.8.5.1(c) of TSD 108.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(13)ID0EB04B004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(13)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every school bus other than a multifunction school activity bus shall be equipped with a flasher that conforms to SAE Recommended Practice J1054, <cite class="XRefExternal">Warning Lamp Alternating Flashers</cite> (October 1989), and that activates the signal lamps referred to in S5.1.4 of TSD&#xA0;108.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Location of Required Equipment &#x2014; S5.3 of TSD 108</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(14)ID0ED02B004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(14)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of S5.3 and Table&#xA0;II of TSD 108, the location of rear identification lamps on a van trailer with side-opening rear doors conforms to that section if the lamps are located as close as practicable to the top of the vehicle</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(14)p-(a)ID0EBB02B004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;above or on the rear doors, if the vertical face of the header rail, measured on the vertical centreline of the vehicle, extends at least 25&#xA0;mm above the rear doors; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(14)p-(b)ID0EBA02B004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;above or below or on the rear doors, if the vertical face of the header rail, measured on the vertical centreline of the vehicle, extends less than 25&#xA0;mm above the rear doors.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(14.1)ID0EB01B004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(14.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S5.3 and Table IV of TSD 108, the tail lamps, stop lamps and parking lamps on a motor tricycle shall be installed in accordance with the requirements of S5.3 and Table&#xA0;IV of TSD 108 for tail lamps, stop lamps and parking lamps installed on a passenger car.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(15)ID0EB0ZB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(15)</span>
</a>&#xA0;[Reserved]</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Special Wiring Requirements &#x2014; S5.5 of TSD 108</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(16)ID0EB0XB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(16)</span>
</a>&#xA0;S5.5.1 and S5.5.2 of TSD 108 do not apply to a motorcycle that is fitted with a single beam headlamp.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(17)ID0EB0WB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(17)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(18), the headlamp, tail lamp and licence plate lamp of a motorcycle shall be continuously activated when the engine is operating.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(18)ID0EB0VB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(18)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The headlamp, tail lamp and licence plate lamp of a motorcycle may remain off after the engine is started until the motorcycle is set in motion by its own power for the first time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(19)ID0ED0UB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(19)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In addition to being activated in accordance with the requirements of S5.5.7 of TSD 108, the lamps referred to in S5.5.7(a) of TSD 108 shall be activated when</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(19)p-(a)ID0EBB0UB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the front fog lamps on the vehicle are activated in a steady-burning state other than as daytime running lamps; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(19)p-(b)ID0EBA0UB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the rear fog lamps on the vehicle are activated in a steady-burning state.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(20)ID0EB0TB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(20)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The requirements of S5.5.11 of TSD 108 are replaced by the daytime running lamp requirements of subsections&#xA0;(44) to (65).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Conspicuity Systems &#x2014; S5.7 of TSD 108</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(21)ID0EB0RB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(21)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S5.7 of TSD 108, the colour of retroreflective sheeting applied in accordance with S5.7.1.4.1(a) and S5.7.1.4.2 of TSD 108 may be white, yellow, white and yellow or white and red, in accordance with S5.7.1.2 of TSD 108 or section&#xA0;3.1.3, 3.1.2 or 3.1.1, respectively, of SAE Standard J578, <cite class="XRefExternal">Color Specification</cite> (May 1988).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(22)ID0EB0QB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(22)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If the retroreflective sheeting referred to in S5.7.1.2 of TSD 108 is applied to a non-vertical surface, the entrance angle used to demonstrate that the sheeting conforms to the photometric requirements prescribed by that section shall be the sum of the entrance angle specified in column&#xA0;1 of Figure&#xA0;29 of TSD 108 and the angle, measured at the horizontal centreline of the sheeting, by which the sheeting deviates from the vertical.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(23)ID0EB0PB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(23)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The retroreflective sheeting applied to the rear of a trailer in accordance with S5.7.1.4.1(c) of TSD 108 shall be located not more than 760&#xA0;mm above the road surface and extend to within 450&#xA0;mm of the extreme outer edges of the trailer.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(24)ID0EC0OB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(24)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If a vehicle is equipped with yellow retroreflective sheeting, the sheeting shall conform to the photometric requirements set out in the table to this subsection:</p>

<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Headlighting Requirements &#x2014; S7 of TSD 108</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(25)ID0EB0MB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(25)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of these Regulations, the DOT symbol marked on the lens of a headlamp or of a beam contributor in accordance with S7.2(a) of TSD 108 indicates that the headlamp or beam contributor conforms to TSD 108.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(26)ID0EB0LB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(26)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S5.1.1 of TSD 108, S7.3.7(a) and S7.3.8(a) of TSD 108 do not apply to the headlamps on a passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck, bus or three-wheeled vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(27)ID0EB0KB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(27)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S7.3.7(e)(8) of TSD 108, the figures to which a deflectometer referred to in section&#xA0;4.5 of SAE Standard J580, <cite class="XRefExternal">Sealed Beam Headlamp Assembly</cite> (December 1986), shall be designed to conform are those specified in a standard or recommended practice issued by the SAE or provided by the vehicle manufacturer to the Minister, at the Minister&#x2019;s request.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(28)ID0EB0JB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(28)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S7.3.8(c)(2) of TSD 108, the figures to which the special adapter and the deflectometer shall be designed to conform are those specified in a standard or recommended practice issued by the SAE or provided by the vehicle manufacturer to the Minister, at the Minister&#x2019;s request.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(29)ID0EB0IB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(29)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The aiming mechanism of every headlamp assembly and front fog lamp assembly shall conform to section&#xA0;5.13.5 of SAE Recommended Practice J1383, <cite class="XRefExternal">Performance Requirements for Motor Vehicle Headlamps</cite> (June 1990).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(30)ID0EB0HB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(30)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Headlamp assemblies and front fog lamp assemblies incorporating retaining rings shall conform to section&#xA0;5.23.2 of SAE Recommended Practice J1383, <cite class="XRefExternal">Performance Requirements for Motor Vehicle Headlamps</cite> (June 1990).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(31)ID0EB0GB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(31)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In addition to conforming to the requirements of S7.3 of TSD 108, sealed beam headlamps with plastic lenses or reflectors shall conform to S7.4(g) and (h) of TSD 108.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(32)ID0EB0FB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(32)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S7.4(a)(3) of TSD 108, a motorcycle headlamp system is not required to be equipped with the Vehicle Headlamp Aiming Device (VHAD) specified in S7.8.5.2 of TSD 108.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(33)ID0EB0EB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(33)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S7.5(g) of TSD 108, if the only replaceable light source in a headlamp is Type HB1, the lens of the headlamp shall bear permanent marking that states the HB Type.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(34)_to_(39)ID0EB0DB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(34) to (39)</span>
</a>&#xA0;[Reserved]</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(40)ID0ED0CB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(40)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every front fog lamp assembly or auxiliary front lamp assembly that may be switched on simultaneously with the lower beam headlamps on a passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck, bus or three-wheeled vehicle shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(40)p-(a)ID0EBB0CB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a lamp assembly that has a mechanism that allows adjustment of the vertical and horizontal aim, conform to S7.8.2, S7.8.2.2, S7.8.3, S7.8.4 and S7.8.5.1(c) of TSD 108; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(40)p-(b)ID0EDA0CB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a lamp assembly that has a mechanism that only allows adjustment of the vertical aim, conform to</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(40)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBA0CB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;S7.8.2 of TSD 108, except that no horizontal aim mechanism need be provided, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(40)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBAA0CB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;S7.8.2.2, S7.8.3 and S7.8.5.1(c) of TSD 108.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(41)ID0EB0BB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(41)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purpose of demonstrating the compliance of a headlamp assembly with the torque deflection test described in S7.8.5.1(a) of TSD 108, the downward torque of 2.25&#xA0;Nm (20&#xA0;lb.-in.) shall be measured at the aiming reference plane, as defined in S4 of TSD 108.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(42)ID0EB0AB004D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(42)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The information contained in a label referred to in S7.8.5.2(b) of TSD 108 shall be in both official languages.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(43)ID0EB604D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(43)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The operator&#x2019;s manual referred to in S7.8.5.2(b) of TSD 108 shall be published by the manufacturer or importer of the vehicle in both official languages.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(43.1)ID0EB504D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(43.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S7.9.6.2 and Table IV of TSD 108, if a headlamp system installed on a motor tricycle consists of two headlamps that are horizontally disposed about the vertical centreline, it may be installed in accordance with the requirements of S.5.3 and Table IV of TSD 108 for headlamp systems installed on passenger cars.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Daytime Running Lamps</span>
</h3>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">General</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(44)ID0EB204D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(44)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck, bus and three-wheeled vehicle shall be equipped with two daytime running lamps or, if the daytime running lamps are optically combined with the upper beams of the headlamps, with two or four daytime running lamps.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(45)ID0EB104D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(45)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A daytime running lamp shall be white, yellow or white to yellow, in accordance with sections&#xA0;3.1.3, 3.1.2 or 3.1.3.1, respectively, of SAE Standard J578, <cite class="XRefExternal">Color Specification</cite> (May 1988).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(46)ID0EBZ04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(46)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A daytime running lamp that is not optically combined with a headlamp shall conform to SAE Recommended Practice J575, <cite class="XRefExternal">Tests for Motor Vehicle Lighting Devices and Components</cite> (December 1988).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(47)ID0EEY04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(47)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(47.1), a daytime running lamp that is not optically combined with another lamp or is optically combined with a lamp, other than a front fog lamp, that is not required by this section shall be designed to conform to SAE Recommended Practice J2087, <cite class="XRefExternal">Daytime Running Lamps for Use on Motor Vehicles</cite> (August 1991), including the photometric values set out in Table&#xA0;2 of that Recommended Practice, except that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(47)p-(a)ID0EBCY04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the maximum luminous intensity at any test point shall be 3 000 cd;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(47)p-(b)ID0EBBY04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the lamp is not required to conform to section&#xA0;6.2 of that Recommended Practice; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(47)p-(c)ID0EBAY04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the effective projected luminous lens area of the lamp may be less than 40&#xA0;cm<sup>2</sup>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(47.1)ID0EBX04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(47.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A daytime running lamp that is not optically combined with another lamp may conform to SAE Standard J583, <cite class="XRefExternal">Front Fog Lamps</cite> (June 1993), or to paragraphs&#xA0;3, 4.2, 4.3, 5 and 6 of ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;19, <cite class="XRefExternalRegulation">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Motor Vehicle Front Fog Lamps</cite>, Revision&#xA0;3 (March&#xA0;2, 1993).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(47.2)ID0EBW04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(47.2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A daytime running lamp that is optically combined with a front turn signal lamp or a parking lamp shall conform to subsection&#xA0;(47).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(48)ID0EEV04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(48)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A daytime running lamp that is optically combined with a headlamp shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(48)p-(a)ID0EECV04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if combined with the lower beam of a headlamp that is designed to conform to the photometric requirements of this section, operate at</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(48)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBCCV04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;normal operating voltage,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(48)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBBCV04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a DC (direct current) system, not less than 75% and not more than 92% of the normal operating voltage, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(48)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBACV04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of an AC (alternating current) system or a modulated voltage system, the equivalent root mean square of not less than 75% and not more than 92% of the normal operating voltage;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(48)p-(b)ID0EEBV04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if combined with the lower beam of a headlamp that is designed to conform to the photometric requirements of section&#xA0;108.1, operate at</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(48)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBCBV04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;normal operating voltage,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(48)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBBBV04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a DC (direct current) system, not less than 86% and not more than 92% of the normal operating voltage, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(48)p-(b)subp-(iii)ID0EBABV04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of an AC (alternating current) system or a modulated voltage system, the equivalent root mean square of not less than 86% and not more than 92% of the normal operating voltage; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(48)p-(c)ID0EBAV04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if combined with the upper beam of a headlamp, be designed to provide a luminous intensity of not less than 2&#xA0;000&#xA0;cd and not more than 7&#xA0;000&#xA0;cd at test point&#xA0;H-V.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(49)ID0EBU04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(49)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purpose of determining if a daytime running lamp conforms to subsection&#xA0;(48), the daytime running lamp shall be tested in accordance with S11 of TSD 108.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(50)ID0EDT04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(50)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A daytime running lamp that is optically combined with a headlamp or headlamps in which two filaments operate together to provide the daytime running lamp function shall conform to the photometric requirements of paragraph&#xA0;(48)(<em>c</em>) when</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(50)p-(a)ID0EEBT04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the daytime running lamp is provided by</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(50)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBCBT04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an upper beam that is provided by two filaments in the headlamp,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(50)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBBBT04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an upper beam and a lower beam of the headlamp, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(50)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBABT04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an upper beam of the headlamp, and a lower beam or upper beam of another headlamp; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(50)p-(b)ID0EBAT04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the luminous intensities at the test point H-V of each headlamp, tested in accordance with S10 of TSD 108, are added together.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(51)ID0EBS04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(51)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If a daytime running lamp is optically combined with a headlamp that is activated in its concealed position, the daytime running lamp shall conform to subsection&#xA0;(47), (48) or (50).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(52)ID0EBR04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(52)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A daytime running lamp may be optically combined with a front fog lamp that conforms to SAE Standard J583, <cite class="XRefExternal">Front Fog Lamps</cite> (June 1993), or to paragraphs&#xA0;3, 4.2, 4.3, 5 and 6 of ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;19, <cite class="XRefExternalRegulation">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Motor Vehicle Front Fog Lamps</cite>, Revision&#xA0;3 (March&#xA0;2, 1993).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(53)ID0EDQ04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(53)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite subsections&#xA0;(45) to (52), a vehicle may be equipped with a daytime running light system that conforms to Canadian Standards Association Standard CAN/CSA-D603-88, <cite class="XRefExternal">Daytime Running Light Systems</cite> (April 1988), other than a Type&#xA0;4 and Type&#xA0;5 system (reduced voltage upper beam headlamps), as indicated in Table&#xA0;1 of the Standard, if</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(53)p-(a)ID0EBBQ04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the daytime running light system is installed in accordance with the instructions referred to in section&#xA0;8.2 of the Standard; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(53)p-(b)ID0EBAQ04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if the vehicle is equipped with gaseous-discharge lower beam headlamps, only a Type&#xA0;1 system (normal voltage lower beam headlamp) or a Type&#xA0;6 or Type&#xA0;7 system (separate lamps other than headlamps), as indicated in Table&#xA0;1 of the Standard, is used.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Switching</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(54)ID0EBO04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(54)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsections&#xA0;(55) and (56), daytime running lamps shall be on continuously when the engine is operating and the master lighting switch is not in the headlamps on position.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(55)ID0EEN04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(55)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Daytime running lamps may switch off</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(55)p-(a)ID0EBCN04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;while the automatic transmission control is in the park or neutral position;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(55)p-(b)ID0EBBN04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;while the parking brake is applied; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(55)p-(c)ID0EBAN04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;after the engine is started but before the vehicle is set in motion for the first time.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(56)ID0EBM04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(56)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A daytime running lamp that is optically combined with a turn signal lamp shall switch off while the turn signal lamp is switched on as a turn signal or as a hazard warning signal.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(57)ID0EDL04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(57)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Daytime running lamps shall switch off</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(57)p-(a)ID0EBBL04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;once the master lighting switch is moved to the headlamps on position; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(57)p-(b)ID0EBAL04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if the lamps are on a vehicle equipped with concealable headlamps and the master lighting switch is moved to the headlamps on position, once the headlamps attain the fully open position.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(58)ID0EEK04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(58)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If the lower beams of the headlamps operating at normal operating voltage are used as daytime running lamps,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(58)p-(a)ID0EBCK04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;it shall not be possible to activate the upper beams of the headlamps except for signalling purposes;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(58)p-(b)ID0EBBK04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if there is a tell-tale that is automatically activated, and visible to the driver, in dark ambient light conditions to indicate that the tail lamps, licence plate lamps, side marker lamps and parking lamps are switched off, those lamps shall not come on automatically; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(58)p-(c)ID0EDAK04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if there is no tell-tale that is automatically activated, and visible to the driver,the lamps referred to in paragraph&#xA0;(<em>b</em>)</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(58)p-(c)subp-(i)ID0EBBAK04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;shall come on automatically and remain on in all ambient light conditions, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(58)p-(c)subp-(ii)ID0EBAAK04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;shall come on automatically in dark ambient light conditions.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(59)ID0EBJ04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(59)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S5.5.1 of TSD 108, the lower beams and upper beams of the headlamps may be activated simultaneously when the headlamps are in use as daytime running lamps.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(60)ID0EBI04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(60)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S5.5.10(d) of TSD 108, daytime running lamps may be wired to flash for signalling purposes.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Visibility</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(61)ID0EBG04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(61)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Daytime running lamps that are not optically combined with another lamp required by this section shall be located at the same height, as far apart as practicable and not less than 380&#xA0;mm and not more than 2&#xA0;110&#xA0;mm above the road surface, measured from the H-V axis of the lamp with the vehicle at curb mass.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(62)ID0EBF04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(62)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A daytime running lamp shall be visible from any point contained within the solid angle bounded by vertical planes 20&#xB0; to the left and right of, and horizontal planes 10&#xB0; above and below, the H-V axis of the lamp.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(63)ID0EEE04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(63)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If the distance, measured on a vertical transverse plane, from the H-V axis of a front turn signal lamp to the exposed edge of the lens of a daytime running lamp that is not optically combined with the turn signal lamp is less than 100&#xA0;mm,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(63)p-(a)ID0EBCE04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the turn signal lamp shall conform to the photometric requirements of Table&#xA0;3 of SAE Standard J588, <cite class="XRefExternal">Turn Signal Lamps for Use on Motor Vehicles Less Than 2032&#xA0;mm in Overall Width</cite> (November 1984), using a luminous intensity multiplier of 2.5;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(63)p-(b)ID0EBBE04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the luminous intensity of the daytime running lamp shall be not more than 2&#xA0;600&#xA0;cd at any point in the beam; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(63)p-(c)ID0EBAE04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the daytime running lamp shall switch off while the turn signal lamp is flashing.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(64)ID0EBD04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(64)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The inner surface of a transparent component, through which light emitted by a daytime running lamp that conforms to subsection&#xA0;(51) passes, shall be accessible for cleaning without the use of any tool designed specifically for vehicles.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(65)ID0EBC04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(65)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A daytime running lamp shall conform to the requirements of S5.1.3 and S5.3 of TSD 108.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108ss-(66)ID0EBB04D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(66)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 2]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
