<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Alternative Requirements for Headlamps</span>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>[SOR/96-366, s. 6]</li>
</ul>
</div>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>108.1</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)ID0EIH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;As an alternative to the headlamps required by section&#xA0;108 of this Schedule, passenger cars, multi-purpose passenger vehicles, buses and trucks may be equipped with headlamps that emit white light and that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(a)ID0EGGH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;comply with</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBEGH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;8, <cite class="XRefExternal">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Motor Vehicle Headlamps Emitting an Asymmetrical Passing Beam or a Driving Beam or Both and Equipped with Halogen Filament Lamps (H<sub>1</sub>, H<sub>2</sub>, H<sub>3</sub>, HB<sub>3</sub>, HB<sub>4</sub>, H<sub>7</sub>, H<sub>8</sub>, H<sub>9</sub>, HIR1, HIR2 and/or H<sub>11</sub>)</cite>, as amended from time to time,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBDGH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;20, <cite class="XRefExternal">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Motor Vehicle Headlamps Emitting an Asymmetrical Passing Beam or a Driving Beam or Both and Equipped with Halogen Filament Lamps (H<sub>4</sub> Lamps)</cite>, as amended from time to time,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBCGH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;31, <cite class="XRefExternal">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Halogen Sealed-beam Unit (HSB Unit) Motor Vehicle Headlamps Emitting an Asymmetrical Passing Beam or a Driving Beam or Both</cite>, as amended from time to time,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(iv)ID0EBBGH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iv)</span>
</a>&#xA0;ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;98, <cite class="XRefExternal">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Motor Vehicle Headlamps Equipped with Gas-discharge Light Sources</cite>, as amended from time to time, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(v)ID0EBAGH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(v)</span>
</a>&#xA0;ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;112, <cite class="XRefExternal">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Motor Vehicle Headlamps Emitting an Asymmetrical Passing Beam or a Driving Beam or Both and Equipped with Filament Lamps</cite>, as amended from time to time;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(b)ID0EBFH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;despite the requirements of the ECE Regulations referred to in this section, are set to be used on vehicles designed to travel on the right-hand side of the road;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(c)ID0EBEH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;provide two upper beams and two lower beams;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(d)ID0EDDH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;conform to</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(d)subp-(i)ID0EBBDH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;paragraphs S5.1.2, S5.5.9, S7.4(g) and (h), S7.8.2, S7.8.2.1(a) and (b), S7.8.2.2, S7.8.3, S7.8.4 and S7.8.5.1(c) of TSD 108, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(d)subp-(ii)ID0EBADH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;subsections&#xA0;108(29) and, if applicable, (30);</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(e)ID0EBCH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;comply with sections&#xA0;5.1.2, 5.1.4 and, if applicable, 5.1.6 of SAE Standard J580, <cite class="XRefExternal">Sealed Beam Headlamp Assembly</cite> (December 1986);</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(f)ID0EDBH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;are fitted with bulbs that conform to</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(f)subp-(i)ID0EBBBH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a document referred to in paragraph&#xA0;108(5)(<em>a</em>) or the information provided pursuant to paragraph&#xA0;108(5)(<em>b</em>), and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(f)subp-(ii)ID0EBABH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;paragraphs S7.7 of TSD 108, except that the &#x201C;DOT&#x201D; symbol referred to in paragraphs S7.7(a) and (e)(7) is not required; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(1)p-(g)ID0EBAH02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(g)</span>
</a>&#xA0;when activated in a steady-burning state, do not have any styling ornament or other feature, such as a translucent cover or grill, in front of the lens.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(2)ID0EEG02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;As an alternative to the headlamps required by section&#xA0;108, motorcycles may be equipped with headlamps that emit white light and that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EBCG02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;provide one upper beam and one lower beam, or two upper beams and two lower beams;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EFBG02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;comply with</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBDBG02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;subparagraphs (1)(<em>a</em>)(i) to (iii) and (v) and paragraphs&#xA0;(1)(<em>b</em>) and (<em>d</em>) to (<em>f</em>),</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBCBG02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;57, <cite class="XRefExternalRegulation">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Headlamps for Motor Cycles and Vehicles Treated as Such</cite>, as amended from time to time,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(iii)ID0EBBBG02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;72, <cite class="XRefExternalRegulation">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Motor Cycle Headlamps Emitting an Asymmetrical Passing Beam and a Driving Beam and Equipped with Halogen Lamps (HS<sub>1</sub> Lamps)</cite>, as amended from time to time, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(iv)ID0EBABG02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iv)</span>
</a>&#xA0;ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;113, <cite class="XRefExternalRegulation">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Motor Vehicle Headlamps Emitting a Symmetrical Passing Beam or a Driving Beam or Both and Equipped with Filament Lamps</cite>, as amended from time to time; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(2)p-(c)ID0EBAG02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;conform to subsections&#xA0;108(12), (29) and, if applicable, (30).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(3)ID0EBF02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;As an alternative to the requirements of the ECE Regulations referred to in this section, headlamps fitted on a vehicle may emit white light as specified in SAE Standard J578, <cite class="XRefExternal">Color Specification</cite> (May 1988).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(4)ID0EEE02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of this section, the following requirements of the ECE Regulations referred to in subsections&#xA0;(1) and (2) do not apply:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EBCE02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;any requirements respecting the approval process;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EBBE02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;any requirements respecting the marking of approved headlamps; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(4)p-(c)ID0EEAE02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;any requirements respecting</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(4)p-(c)subp-(i)ID0EBCAE02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the conformity of headlamp production to the type approved,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(4)p-(c)subp-(ii)ID0EBBAE02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the penalties for non-conformity of production, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(4)p-(c)subp-(iii)ID0EBAAE02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the modification of a headlamp type and extension of approval.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(5)ID0EBD02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The total intensity of the upper beams of the headlamps of a vehicle equipped pursuant to this section shall not exceed 225,000&#xA0;cd at any point in the beam pattern when measured at 12&#xA0;V.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(6)ID0EBC02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Except for headlamps with plastic lenses, wipers may be fitted to the headlamps of a vehicle equipped pursuant to this section, if the headlamps conform to all of the applicable photometric requirements when the wipers are stopped in any position in front of the lenses.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-108.1ss-(7)ID0EBB02D0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/91-692, s. 3]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Tire Selection and Rims for Motor Vehicles With a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;KG or Less (Standard&#xA0;110)</span>
</h3>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">General</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>110</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(1)ID0EBL0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every motor vehicle with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536 kg or less &#x2014; except motorcycles other than motor tricycles equipped with passenger car tires, restricted-use motorcycles, three-wheeled vehicles equipped with tires other than passenger car tires, vehicles imported temporarily for special purposes and low-speed vehicles &#x2014; and every tire rim manufactured for use on those vehicles shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No. 110, Tire Selection and Rims for Motor Vehicles With a GVWR of 4,536 kg or Less</cite> (TSD 110), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;110</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(2)ID0EDJ0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Except as provided in subsections (3) and (4), the information specified in S4.3 and S4.3.5 of TSD 110 shall appear, at the option of the manufacturer, either</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EBBJ0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in both official languages on one vehicle placard, as shown in Figure 3, or, if the manufacturer chooses to use a tire inflation pressure label, on one placard and one label, as shown in Figures 3 and 6; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EBAJ0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in each official language on two vehicle placards, as shown in Figures 1 and 2, or, if the manufacturer chooses to use a tire inflation pressure label, on two placards and two labels, as shown in Figures 1, 2, 4 and 5, affixed at the same location on the vehicle but apart.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(3)ID0EDI0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The information specified in S4.3(f) of TSD 110 that appears on a vehicle placard and, at the manufacturer&#x2019;s option, on a tire inflation pressure label, in accordance with paragraph (2)(<em>a</em>), shall appear either</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBBI0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the form of the symbol number N.03 for Operator&#x2019;s manual, operation instructions, that is included in International Standard ISO 2575, entitled <cite class="XRefExternal">Road vehicles &#x2014; Symbols for controls, indicators and tell-tales</cite>, 7th edition, May 1, 2004; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBAI0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in both official languages on one placard, as shown in Figure 3, or on one placard and one label, as shown in Figures 3 and 6.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(4)ID0EDH0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The information specified in S4.3(f) of TSD 110 that appears on a vehicle placard and, at the manufacturer&#x2019;s option, on a tire inflation pressure label, in accordance with paragraph 2(<em>b</em>), shall appear either</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EBBH0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the form of the symbol number N.03 specified in paragraph (3)(<em>a</em>); or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EBAH0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in each official language on two placards, as shown in Figures 1 and 2, or on two placards and two labels, as shown in Figures 1, 2, 4 and 5, affixed at the same location on the vehicle but apart.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(5)ID0EBG0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The words &#x201C;<span class="otherLang" lang="fr">Voir le manuel de l&#x2019;usager&#xA0;pour plus de renseignements</span>&#x201D;, in the French version of the information specified in S4.3(f) of TSD 110, may, at the option of the manufacturer, be replaced by the words &#x201C;<span class="otherLang" lang="fr">Voir le guide du propri&#xE9;taire&#xA0;pour plus de renseignements</span>&#x201D;, &#x201C;<span class="otherLang" lang="fr">Voir le manuel du propri&#xE9;taire pour plus de renseignements</span>&#x201D; or &#x201C;<span class="otherLang" lang="fr">Voir le guide de l&#x2019;automobiliste&#xA0;pour plus de renseignements</span>&#x201D;.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(6)ID0EBF0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The information specified in S4.3.3 of TSD 110 shall be in both official languages.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(7)ID0EEE0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The following definitions apply for the purposes of TSD 110.</p>
<dl class="Definition">
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>load rating</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>load rating</dfn>
</span> means the maximum load a tire is rated to carry at a given inflation pressure. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">charge nominale</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>maximum load rating</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>maximum load rating</dfn>
</span> means the load rating at the maximum permissible inflation pressure for that tire. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">limite de charge nominale</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>rim base</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>rim base</dfn>
</span> means that portion of a rim remaining after the removal of all split or continuous rim flanges, side rings, and locking rings that can be detached from the rim. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">base de jante</span>) </p>
</dd>
</dl>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Load Range Identification Symbol</span>

<ul class="ProvisionList">

<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-110ss-(8)ID0EBC0XD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Mirrors</span>
</h3>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">General</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>111</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(1)ID0EH0FB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Any mirror referred to in this section that is installed on a vehicle shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(1)p-(a)ID0EBF0FB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;have a stable support;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(1)p-(b)ID0EBE0FB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be adjustable in the horizontal and vertical directions;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(1)p-(c)ID0EBD0FB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be a unit magnification mirror, except in the cases referred to in subsection&#xA0;(6), paragraph&#xA0;(13)(<em>b</em>) and subsection&#xA0;(16);</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(1)p-(d)ID0EBC0FB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be free of sharp points or edges that could cause an injury to an occupant of the vehicle or to a pedestrian;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(1)p-(e)ID0EBB0FB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;except in the case of a System&#xA0;B mirror installed on a school bus that has a forward control configuration, be installed so that the driver&#x2019;s field of view through the mirror is not obscured by the portion of the windshield that is not wiped by the windshield wipers or by any opaque portion of the vehicle structure; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(1)p-(f)ID0EBA0FB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of an outside rearview mirror, have no greater protrusion beyond the perimeter of the vehicle than is necessary to meet the field-of-view requirements for the mirror prescribed in this section.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(2)ID0EB0EB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A rearview mirror referred to in subsection&#xA0;(7) or (11) or paragraph&#xA0;(26)(<em>a</em>) shall be capable of adjustment from within the occupant compartment of the vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(3)ID0EB0DB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The average reflectance of a mirror referred to in this section shall be determined in accordance with SAE Standard J964, <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Procedure for Determining Reflectivity of Rear View Mirrors</cite> (June 1992).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(4)ID0EB0CB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A mirror referred to in this section that is a single reflectance mirror shall have a reflectance level of at least 35 per cent.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(5)ID0EB0BB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A mirror referred to in this section that is a multiple reflectance mirror shall have a daytime reflectance level of at least 35 per cent and a night-time reflectance level of at least 4 per cent. In the event of electrical failure, the mirror shall be adjustable, either manually or automatically, to a reflectance level of at least 35 per cent.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(6)ID0EE0AB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;An outside rearview mirror referred to in paragraph&#xA0;(7)(<em>b</em>) or subsection&#xA0;(26) or (27) that is installed on the side of the vehicle opposite the driver&#x2019;s side may be convex if</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(6)p-(a)ID0EBC0AB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;its reflective surface area is equal to or greater than the reflective surface area that a unit magnification mirror must have in accordance with that paragraph or subsection;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(6)p-(b)ID0EBB0AB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;its average radius of curvature is not less than 890&#xA0;mm (35&#xA0;inches) and not greater than 1&#xA0;800&#xA0;mm (71.5&#xA0;inches); and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(6)p-(c)ID0EBA0AB00UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the radius of curvature at any point does not deviate by more than 12.5 per cent from the average of any five radius-of-curvature measurements made on its reflective surface at least 6&#xA0;mm (0.25&#xA0;inch) from the edge of the image display.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Passenger Cars and Three-wheeled Vehicles</span>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>[SOR/2003-272, s. 13]</li>
</ul>
</div>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(7)ID0ED50UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;An inside rearview mirror shall be installed on every passenger car and three-wheeled vehicle and shall, under the conditions prescribed in subsection&#xA0;(8),</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(7)p-(a)ID0EDB50UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;provide the driver with a field of view to the rear that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(7)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBBB50UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;is not less than 20&#xB0; measured horizontally rearward from the projected eye point, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(7)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBAB50UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;extends to the horizon and includes a point on the road surface not more than 60&#xA0;m (200&#xA0;feet) directly behind the vehicle; or</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(7)p-(b)ID0EBA50UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;where the inside rearview mirror does not provide the field of view to the rear described in paragraph&#xA0;(<em>a</em>), be accompanied, on the side opposite the driver&#x2019;s side, by an outside rearview mirror that has not less than 90 per cent of the reflective surface area of an outside rearview mirror installed pursuant to subsection&#xA0;(11).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(8)ID0ED40UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of subsection&#xA0;(7), the vehicle shall be on a level road surface and loaded with the lighter of the following loads, calculated on the basis of the driver and each occupant weighing 68&#xA0;kg (150&#xA0;pounds):</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(8)p-(a)ID0EBB40UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a driver and four other occupants, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(8)p-(b)ID0EBA40UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an occupant in each designated seating position.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(9)ID0EB30UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A field of view to the rear described in paragraph&#xA0;(7)(<em>a</em>) may be partially obscured by seated occupants or head restraints.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(10)ID0EB20UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;An inside rearview mirror referred to in subsection&#xA0;(7), if situated in the head impact area, shall, when the reflective surface of the mirror is subjected to a force of 400&#xA0;N (90&#xA0;pounds) in any direction that is not more than 45&#xB0; from the forward longitudinal direction, deflect, collapse or break away without leaving sharp edges.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(11)ID0EE10UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;An outside rearview mirror shall be installed on the driver&#x2019;s side of every passenger car and three-wheeled vehicle in such a manner as to provide the driver with a field of view to the rear on a level road surface that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(11)p-(a)ID0EBC10UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;may be partially obscured by the rear body or fender contours;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(11)p-(b)ID0EBB10UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;extends to the horizon; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(11)p-(c)ID0EBA10UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;includes a line measuring 2.5&#xA0;m (8&#xA0;feet) perpendicular to and outboard from the vertical longitudinal plane tangent to the driver&#x2019;s side of the vehicle at its widest part, at a point 10.6&#xA0;m (35&#xA0;feet) behind the eyes of the driver seated with the driver&#x2019;s seat in the rearmost position.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(12)ID0EDZ0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of subsections&#xA0;(7), (9) and (11), the field of view to the rear of the driver shall be evaluated by using</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(12)p-(a)ID0EBBZ0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the location of the driver&#x2019;s eye reference points for the 95th percentile tangential cut-off specified in SAE Recommended Practice J941a, <cite class="XRefExternal">Passenger Car Driver&#x2019;s Eye Range</cite> (August 1967); or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(12)p-(b)ID0EBAZ0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the driver&#x2019;s eye reference points at a nominal location appropriate for any 95th&#xA0;percentile adult male driver.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Motorcycles</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(13)ID0EDX0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(13)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every motorcycle shall have, mounted on each side so that the horizontal centre of each reflective surface of the mirror is at least 280&#xA0;mm (11&#xA0;inches) outward from the longitudinal centreline of the motorcycle,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(13)p-(a)ID0EBBX0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a rearview mirror with not less than 80&#xA0;cm<sup>2</sup> (12.5&#xA0;square inches) of reflective surface area; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(13)p-(b)ID0EBAX0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a convex rearview mirror with not less than 64.5&#xA0;cm<sup>2</sup> (10&#xA0;square inches) of reflective surface area and an average radius of curvature that is not less than 510&#xA0;mm (20&#xA0;inches) and not greater than 1&#xA0;800&#xA0;mm (71.5&#xA0;inches).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">School Buses</span>
</h4>
<h5 class="SchedHeadL4">
<span class="HTitleText4">General</span>
</h5>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(14)ID0EEU0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(14)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of subsections&#xA0;(16) to (25), a driver&#x2019;s eye position shall be represented by the left and right eye points as defined in SAE Recommended Practice J1050, <cite class="XRefExternal">Describing and Measuring the Driver&#x2019;s Field of View</cite> (August 1994), and shall be at any place within the area defined by a 95th&#xA0;percentile eyellipse in accordance with SAE Recommended Practice J941, <cite class="XRefExternal">Motor Vehicle Drivers&#x2019; Eye Locations</cite> (June 1997), with the following adaptations:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(14)p-(a)ID0EBCU0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a 50/50 male-to-female ratio must be used for the male/female mix; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(14)p-(b)ID0EBBU0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>heel point</dfn>
</span> referred to in that Recommended Practice and in other documents referenced in that Recommended Practice means the <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>accelerator heel point (AHP)</dfn>
</span> as defined in section&#xA0;3.16.1 of SAE Recommended Practice J1100, <cite class="XRefExternal">Motor Vehicle Dimensions</cite> (February 2001), and the position of the heel point is that determined by the manufacturer.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(14)p-(c)ID0EBAU0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2008-72, s. 2]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(15)ID0EET0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(15)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of subsections&#xA0;(16) to (25),</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(15)p-(a)ID0EBCT0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cylinders A, D and E shall be 0.305&#xA0;m (1&#xA0;foot) high and 0.305&#xA0;m (1&#xA0;foot) in diameter;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(15)p-(b)ID0EBBT0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cylinders B and C shall be 0.915&#xA0;m (3&#xA0;feet) high and 0.305&#xA0;m (1&#xA0;foot) in diameter; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(15)p-(c)ID0EBAT0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cylinders A, B, C, D and E shall be of a colour that provides a high contrast with the road surface on which the bus is parked.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 class="SchedHeadL4">
<span class="HTitleText4">Requirements</span>
</h5>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(16)ID0EDR0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(16)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every school bus shall have the following two outside mirror systems:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(16)p-(a)ID0EBBR0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;System A, which consists, on each side of the school bus, of one unit magnification mirror that conforms to subsection&#xA0;(18) and one convex mirror that conforms to subsection&#xA0;(19); and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(16)p-(b)ID0EBAR0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;System B, which consists, on each side of the school bus, of one convex mirror that conforms to subsections&#xA0;(20) to (24).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(17)ID0EBQ0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(17)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A System A mirror and System B mirror shall conform to the provisions referred to in subsection&#xA0;(16) at any driver&#x2019;s eye position, when they are adjusted in accordance with the manufacturer&#x2019;s instructions.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(18)ID0EBP0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(18)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Each System A unit magnification mirror shall have a reflective surface area of not less than 325&#xA0;cm<sup>2</sup> (50&#xA0;square inches) that provides, at the driver&#x2019;s eye position, a field of view that includes a continuous view rearward, of the side of the school bus and the road surface, which view shall begin no farther than 60&#xA0;m (200&#xA0;feet) rearward of the mirror&#x2019;s surface and extend to the horizon when measured on a level road, as illustrated in Figure&#xA0;1.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(19)ID0EEO0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(19)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Each System A convex mirror shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(19)p-(a)ID0EGCO0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;provide, at the driver&#x2019;s eye position, a field of view that includes continuous and complete views as illustrated in Figure&#xA0;1,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(19)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBECO0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;rearward,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(19)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBDCO0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;of the ground, which view overlaps the field of view provided by the unit magnification mirror described in subsection&#xA0;(18),</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(19)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBCCO0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;of the side of the bus,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(19)p-(a)subp-(iv)ID0EBBCO0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iv)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the mirror installed on the side opposite the driver&#x2019;s side, of cylinders&#xA0;B and D, placed in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(25), and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(19)p-(a)subp-(v)ID0EBACO0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(v)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the mirror installed on the driver&#x2019;s side, of cylinders&#xA0;C and E, placed in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(25);</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(19)p-(b)ID0EBBO0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;have an average radius of curvature of not less than 482&#xA0;mm (19&#xA0;inches); and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(19)p-(c)ID0EBAO0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;have a radius of curvature that does not deviate at any point by more than 12.5 per cent from the average of any five radius-of-curvature measurements taken at least 6&#xA0;mm (0.25&#xA0;inch) from the edge of the reflective surface.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(20)ID0EDN0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(20)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Each System B mirror shall be installed so that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(20)p-(a)ID0EBBN0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the distance from the driver&#x2019;s eye position to the centre of the mirror is at least 95.25&#xA0;cm (37.5&#xA0;inches); and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(20)p-(b)ID0EBAN0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the slope of the mirror surface has no discontinuities.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(21)ID0EFM0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(21)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Each System B mirror shall provide a field of view that includes continuous and complete views at the driver&#x2019;s eye position, as illustrated in Figure&#xA0;1, of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(21)p-(a)ID0EBDM0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the ground from the front bumper forward to a point where direct observation of the ground is possible;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(21)p-(b)ID0EBCM0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the ground and the side of the bus rearward of the front bumper, extending to and overlapping the field of view provided by the System&#xA0;A convex mirror;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(21)p-(c)ID0EBBM0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a mirror installed on the side opposite the driver&#x2019;s side, of cylinders&#xA0;A and B, placed in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(25), and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(21)p-(d)ID0EBAM0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a mirror installed on the driver&#x2019;s side, of cylinders&#xA0;A and C, placed in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(25).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(22)ID0EDL0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(22)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The images of cylinders&#xA0;A, B and C, placed in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(25), that are reflected in each System B mirror shall meet the following requirements:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(22)p-(a)ID0ECBL0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the shortest angular width of the image shall be no less than 3&#xA0;minutes of arc, measured using the following equation:</p>
<div class="Paragraph">
<p class="Formula">X/D &#x2265; 0,000873</p>
<p class="FormulaGroup">where</p>
<dl class="FormulaDefinitionList">
<dt>
<dfn>X</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the width of the image of the cylinder on the reflective surface,</dd>
<dt>
<dfn>D</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the distance between the centre point of the driver&#x2019;s eye position and the centre of the reflective surface, and</dd>
<dt>
<dfn>0.000873</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the tangent of 3&#xA0;minutes of arc; and</dd>
</dl>
</div>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(22)p-(b)ID0ECAL0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the shortest angular length of the image shall be no less than 9&#xA0;minutes of arc, measured using the following equation:</p>
<div class="Paragraph">
<p class="Formula">Y/D &#x2265; 0,002618</p>
<p class="FormulaGroup">where</p>
<dl class="FormulaDefinitionList">
<dt>
<dfn>Y</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the length of the image of the cylinder on the reflective surface,</dd>
<dt>
<dfn>D</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the distance between the centre point of the driver&#x2019;s eye position and the centre of the reflective surface, and</dd>
<dt>
<dfn>0.002618</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the tangent of 9&#xA0;minutes of arc.</dd>
</dl>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(23)ID0EGK0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(23)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of subsection&#xA0;(22), a comparison chart, such as the one shown in Figure&#xA0;2, may be used to measure the angular width and angular length of an image of a cylinder, where</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(23)p-(a)ID0EBEK0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the comparison chart is placed in a vertical plane that contains the image to be evaluated;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(23)p-(b)ID0EBDK0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the plane of the comparison chart is perpendicular to the line of sight;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(23)p-(c)ID0EBCK0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the image of the cylinder and the comparison chart are visible through the still or video camera&#x2019;s viewfinder;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(23)p-(d)ID0EBBK0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a photograph is taken at the driver&#x2019;s eye position; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(23)p-(e)ID0EBAK0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the image of the cylinder is larger than the references shown on the comparison chart.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(24)ID0EBJ0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(24)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Images reflected in each System B mirror shall be located no less than 3&#xA0;minutes of arc from the edge of the reflective surface, when measured at the driver&#x2019;s eye position.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 class="SchedHeadL4">
<span class="HTitleText4">Testing</span>
</h5>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)ID0EIH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(25)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A System A mirror and a System&#xA0;B mirror shall be tested as follows:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(a)ID0EGGH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cylinders A, B, C, D and E shall be placed at the following locations, as illustrated in Figure&#xA0;1, with measurements taken from the centre of the cylinder, as viewed from above:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBEGH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cylinder A shall be placed in front of the bus so that its centre passes through the bus&#x2019;s longitudinal centreline and its top is directly visible through the portion of the windshield wiped by the windshield wipers at the driver&#x2019;s eye position,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBDGH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cylinder B shall be placed on the side opposite the driver&#x2019;s side at a point where the cylinder is entirely visible through the convex mirrors of both System&#xA0;A and System&#xA0;B on that side so that its centre falls in a vertical plane that is 2&#xA0;m (6.6&#xA0;feet) to the right of, and perpendicular to, a vertical plane tangent to the bus&#x2019;s most outboard surface,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBCGH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cylinder C shall be placed on the driver&#x2019;s side at a point where the cylinder is entirely visible through the convex mirrors of both System&#xA0;A and System&#xA0;B on that side so that its centre falls in a vertical plane that is 2&#xA0;m (6.6&#xA0;feet) to the left of, and perpendicular to, a vertical plane tangent to the bus&#x2019;s most outboard surface,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(a)subp-(iv)ID0EBBGH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iv)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cylinder D shall be placed on the side opposite the driver&#x2019;s side so that its centre falls in the vertical plane that passes through the centreline of the bus&#x2019;s rear-wheel axle and that is 2&#xA0;m (6.6&#xA0;feet) to the right of the bus&#x2019;s most outboard surface, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(a)subp-(v)ID0EBAGH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(v)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cylinder E shall be placed on the driver&#x2019;s side so that its centre falls in the vertical plane that passes through the centreline of the bus&#x2019;s rear-wheel axle and that is 2&#xA0;m (6.6&#xA0;feet) to the left of the bus&#x2019;s most outboard surface;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(b)ID0EBFH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;every mirror shall be adjusted in accordance with the manufacturer&#x2019;s recommendations to the driver&#x2019;s eye position and is not to be moved or readjusted during testing for that eye position but may be readjusted for subsequent tests for different eye positions;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(c)ID0EBEH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a still or video camera shall be positioned so that its image plane is located at the driver&#x2019;s eye point in such a manner that the reflective surface is visible to the camera through the windows of the bus;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(d)ID0EBDH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;for a specific driver&#x2019;s eye position, the requirements of subsections&#xA0;(16) to (25) shall be satisfied with the still or video camera positioned at either the left or right eye point;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(e)ID0EDCH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the still or video camera shall be supported so as to allow pivoting</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(e)subp-(i)ID0EBBCH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the vertical and horizontal planes of its image plane to no greater than the maximum allowable limits of eye rotation specified in SAE Recommended Practice J1050, <cite class="XRefExternal">Describing and Measuring the Driver&#x2019;s Field of View</cite> (August 1994), and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(e)subp-(ii)ID0EBACH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the horizontal plane of its image plane to no greater than the maximum allowable limit of neck rotation specified in SAE Recommended Practice J1050, at a point corresponding to the neck pivot point as specified in that Recommended Practice, only after the maximum limits of eye rotation have been reached;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(f)ID0EBBH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;all of the still or video camera observations shall be done with the service door of the bus closed and the stop signal arm fully retracted; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(25)p-(g)ID0EBAH0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(g)</span>
</a>&#xA0;for the purposes of subsection&#xA0;(21), the front bumper shall be the forwardmost structural contour of the bumper excluding the fasteners, protruding discrete bumper stops, and any attached accessories such as crossing control arms, which shall be removed prior to testing.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Other Vehicles</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(26)ID0EDF0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(26)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck and bus, with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg (10,000&#xA0;pounds) or less, other than a school bus, shall have</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(26)p-(a)ID0EEBF0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the following rearview mirrors, namely,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(26)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBCBF0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an inside rearview mirror that meets the requirements of subsections&#xA0;(7), (9) and (10),</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(26)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBBBF0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;on the driver&#x2019;s side, an outside rearview mirror that meets the field-of-view requirements of subsection&#xA0;(11), and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(26)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBABF0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;on the side opposite the driver&#x2019;s side, an outside rearview mirror that has not less than 90 per cent of the reflective surface area of the outside rearview mirror installed on the driver&#x2019;s side; or</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(26)p-(b)ID0EBAF0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;on each side of the vehicle, an outside rearview mirror of which not less than 125&#xA0;cm<sup>2</sup> (19.5&#xA0;square inches) of reflective surface area is located so as to provide the driver with a view to the rear along both sides of the vehicle.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(27)ID0EBE0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(27)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck and bus with a GVWR of more than 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg (10,000&#xA0;pounds), other than a school bus, shall have on each side of the vehicle an outside rearview mirror of which not less than 325&#xA0;cm<sup>2</sup> (50&#xA0;square inches) of reflective surface area is located so as to provide the driver with a view to the rear along both sides of the vehicle.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Shipment</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-(28)ID0EBC0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(28)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A company may ship a vehicle bearing a compliance label or information label, as the case may be, on which no outside mirrors have been installed, if the applicable outside mirrors and all of the hardware that is necessary for their mounting accompany the vehicle and all of the holes that are necessary for mounting those mirrors have been made in the sheet metal of the vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-111ss-ID0EEB0UD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">
</span>
</a>&#xA0;</p>

</div>

</p>
</figcaption>
</figure>

</li>
</ul>
