</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Hood Latch System</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>113</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-113ss-(1)ID0EBD0QD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In this section, <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>hood</dfn>
</span> means any exterior movable body panel forward of the windshield that is used to cover an engine, luggage, storage or battery compartment.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-113ss-(2)ID0EBC0QD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Each hood with which a vehicle is equipped shall be provided with a hood latch system.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-113ss-(3)ID0EBB0QD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A front-opening hood that, in any position, partially or completely obstructs a driver&#x2019;s forward view through the windshield of the vehicle shall be provided with a second latching position on the hood latch system or with a second hood latch system.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/79-306, s. 4;</li>
<li> SOR/79-940, s. 7;</li>
<li> SOR/2000-182, s. 6.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Theft Protection and Rollaway Prevention (Standard&#xA0;114)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>114</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(1)ID0EBZ0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;With the exception of a walk-in van, every passenger car, every three-wheeled vehicle, and every multi-purpose passenger vehicle and truck with a GVWR of 4 536 kg or less shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No. 114, Theft Protection and Rollaway Prevention</cite> (TSD 114), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(2)ID0EBY0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The term <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>self-mobility</dfn>
</span> in TSD 114 means movement of a vehicle under its own power.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(3)ID0EBX0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 4]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Immobilization System</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(4)ID0EDV0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;With the exception of a walk-in van and an emergency vehicle, every passenger car, every three-wheeled vehicle, and every multi-purpose passenger vehicle and truck with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less shall be equipped with an immobilization system that conforms to</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EEBV0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;one of the following sets of requirements as modified by subsection&#xA0;(22), (23) or (24):</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(4)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBCBV0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the requirements of section&#xA0;3, subsection&#xA0;4.3, sections&#xA0;6 to 10 and subsections&#xA0;12.1, 12.2 and 12.16 of National Standard of Canada CAN/ULC-S338-98, entitled <cite class="XRefExternal">Automobile Theft Deterrent Equipment and Systems: Electronic Immobilization</cite> (May 1998), published by the Underwriters&#x2019; Laboratories of Canada,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(4)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBBBV0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the general and particular specifications that are set out in Part III of ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;97, entitled <cite class="XRefExternal">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Vehicle Alarm Systems (VAS) and of Motor Vehicles with Regard to Their Alarm Systems (AS)</cite>, in the version in effect on August&#xA0;8, 2007, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(4)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBABV0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the general and particular specifications that are set out in Part&#xA0;IV of ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;116, entitled <cite class="XRefExternal">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Protection of Motor Vehicles Against Unauthorized Use</cite>, in the version in effect on February&#xA0;10, 2009; or</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EBAV0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the requirements set out in subsections&#xA0;(8) to (21).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(5)ID0EDU0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A vehicle equipped with an immobilization system shall be accompanied by the following written information:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(5)p-(a)ID0EBBU0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;instructions for operating and maintaining the system; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(5)p-(b)ID0EBAU0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a warning not to leave a disarming device or a combination that disarms the system in the vehicle.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(6)ID0EBT0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The information shall be provided in English, French or both official languages, as requested by the first retail purchaser of the vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(7)ID0EBS0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In this section, <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>disarming device</dfn>
</span> means a physical device that contains or transmits the code that disarms the immobilization system of a vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(8)ID0EBR0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(9), an immobilization system shall arm automatically within a period of not more than 1&#xA0;minute after the disarming device is removed from the vehicle, if the vehicle remains in a mode of operation other than &#x201C;accessory&#x201D; or &#x201C;on&#x201D; throughout that period.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(9)ID0EBQ0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If the disarming device is a keypad or biometric identifier, the immobilization system shall arm automatically within a period of not more than 1 minute after the motors used for the vehicle&#x2019;s propulsion are turned off, if the vehicle remains in a mode of operation other than &#x201C;accessory&#x201D; or &#x201C;on&#x201D; throughout that period.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(10)ID0EEP0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The immobilization system shall arm automatically not later than 2 minutes after the immobilization system is disarmed, unless</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(10)p-(a)ID0EBCP0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;action is taken for starting one or more motors used for the vehicle&#x2019;s propulsion;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(10)p-(b)ID0EEBP0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;disarming requires an action to be taken on</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(10)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBCBP0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the engine start control or electric motor start control,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(10)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBBBP0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the engine stop control or electric motor stop control, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(10)p-(b)subp-(iii)ID0EBABP0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the ignition switch; or</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(10)p-(c)ID0EBAP0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;disarming occurs automatically by the presence of a disarming device and the device is inside the vehicle.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(11)ID0EDO0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If armed, the immobilization system</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(11)p-(a)ID0EBBO0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;shall prevent the vehicle from moving more than 3&#xA0;m under its own power by inhibiting the operation of at least one electronic control unit; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(11)p-(b)ID0EBAO0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;shall not have any impact on the vehicle&#x2019;s brake system except that it may prevent regenerative braking and the release of the parking brake.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(12)ID0EBN0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;During the disarming process, a code shall be sent to the inhibited electronic control unit in order to allow the vehicle to move under its own power.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(13)ID0EBM0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(13)</span>
</a>&#xA0;It shall not be possible to disarm the immobilization system by interrupting its normal operating voltage.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(14)ID0EBL0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(14)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When the normal starting procedure requires that the disarming device mechanically latch into a receptacle and the device is physically separate from the ignition switch key, one or more motors used for the vehicle&#x2019;s propulsion shall start only after the device is removed from that receptacle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(15)ID0EEK0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(15)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The immobilization system shall conform to the following requirements:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(15)p-(a)ID0EBCK0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;it shall have a minimum capacity of 50,000&#xA0;code variants;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(15)p-(b)ID0EBBK0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;it shall not be disarmed by a code that can disarm all other immobilization systems of the same make and model; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(15)p-(c)ID0EBAK0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;subject to subsection&#xA0;(16), it shall not have the capacity to process more than 5,000&#xA0;codes within 24&#xA0;hours;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(16)ID0EDJ0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(16)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If an immobilization system uses rolling or encrypted codes, it may conform to the following requirements, instead of the requirement set out in paragraph&#xA0;(15)(<em>c</em>):</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(16)p-(a)ID0EBBJ0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the probability of obtaining the correct code within 24&#xA0;hours shall not exceed 4 per cent; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(16)p-(b)ID0EBAJ0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;it shall not be possible to disarm the system by re-transmitting in any sequence the previous 5&#xA0;codes generated by the system.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(17)ID0EDI0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(17)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The immobilization system shall be designed so that, when tested as installed in the vehicle,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(17)p-(a)ID0EBBI0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;neither the replacement of an original immobilization system component with a manufacturer&#x2019;s replacement component nor the addition of a manufacturer&#x2019;s component can be completed without the use of software; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(17)p-(b)ID0EBAI0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;it is not possible for the vehicle to move under its own power for at least 5&#xA0;minutes after the beginning of the replacement or addition of a component referred to in paragraph (<em>a</em>).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(18)ID0EBH0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(18)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The immobilization system&#x2019;s conformity to subsection&#xA0;(17) shall be demonstrated by testing that is carried out without damaging the vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(19)ID0EBG0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(19)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Paragraph (17)(<em>b</em>) does not apply to the addition of a disarming device that requires the use of another disarming device that is validated by the immobilization system.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(20)ID0EDF0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(20)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The immobilization system shall be designed so that it can neither be bypassed nor rendered ineffective in a manner that would allow a vehicle to move under its own power, or be disarmed, using one or more of the tools and equipment listed in subsection&#xA0;(21),</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(20)p-(a)ID0EBBF0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;within a period of less than 5&#xA0;minutes, when tested as installed in the vehicle; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(20)p-(b)ID0EBAF0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;within a period of less than 2.5&#xA0;minutes, when bench-tested outside the vehicle.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(21)ID0EIE0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(21)</span>
</a>&#xA0;During a test referred to in subsection&#xA0;(20), only the following tools or equipment may be used:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(21)p-(a)ID0EBGE0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;scissors, wire strippers, wire cutters and electrical wires;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(21)p-(b)ID0EBFE0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a hammer, a slide hammer, a chisel, a punch, a wrench, a screwdriver and pliers;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(21)p-(c)ID0EBEE0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;steel rods and spikes;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(21)p-(d)ID0EBDE0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a hacksaw;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(21)p-(e)ID0EBCE0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a battery operated drill;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(21)p-(f)ID0EBBE0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a battery operated angle grinder; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(21)p-(g)ID0EBAE0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(g)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a battery operated jigsaw.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(22)ID0EED0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(22)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The requirements set out in National Standard of Canada CAN/ULC-S338-98 are modified as follows:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(22)p-(a)ID0EBCD0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the requirements respecting non-OEM systems as defined in section&#xA0;2 of that document and respecting local noise regulations do not apply;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(22)p-(b)ID0EBBD0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a reference to a &#x201C;manufacturer of the electronic immobilization system&#x201D; is to be read as a reference to a &#x201C;manufacturer&#x201D;; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(22)p-(c)ID0EBAD0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;subsection&#xA0;8.1 is to be read as follows: &#x201C;Transponders and remote controls shall be in sealed enclosures that conform to the requirements of Subsections&#xA0;12.1, General, and 12.2, Normal Operation.&#x201D;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(23)ID0EFC0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(23)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The requirements set out in Part III of ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;97 are modified as follows:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(23)p-(a)ID0EBDC0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the aftermarket, type approval and radio transmission requirements do not apply;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(23)p-(b)ID0EBCC0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;all references to paragraph&#xA0;33 do not apply;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(23)p-(c)ID0EBBC0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;for the purposes of paragraph&#xA0;31.7, the word <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>rapidly</dfn>
</span> means less than 5&#xA0;minutes and the words <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>time consuming</dfn>
</span> mean at least 5&#xA0;minutes; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(23)p-(d)ID0EBAC0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;despite any statement to the contrary in paragraphs&#xA0;31.10 and 31.11, the immobilization system shall not have any impact on the vehicle&#x2019;s brake system.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(24)ID0EFB0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(24)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The requirements set out in Part&#xA0;IV of ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;116 are modified as follows:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(24)p-(a)ID0EBDB0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the aftermarket, type approval and radio transmission requirements do not apply;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(24)p-(b)ID0EBCB0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;for the purposes of paragraph&#xA0;8.2.7, the word <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>rapidly</dfn>
</span> means less than 5&#xA0;minutes and the expression <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>time consuming</dfn>
</span> means at least 5 minutes;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(24)p-(c)ID0EBBB0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;despite any statement to the contrary in paragraphs&#xA0;8.2.10 and 8.2.11, the immobilization system shall not have any impact on the vehicle&#x2019;s brake system; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-114ss-(24)p-(d)ID0EBAB0OD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;all references to paragraph&#xA0;8.4 do not apply.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/79-940, s. 7;</li>
<li> SOR/95-164, s. 6;</li>
<li> SOR/97-264, s. 3;</li>
<li> SOR/97-421, s. 6;</li>
<li> SOR/2005-45, s. 4;</li>
<li> SOR/2007-246, s. 3;</li>
<li> SOR/2008-104, s. 13;</li>
<li> SOR/2009-32, s. 2;</li>
<li> SOR/2009-330, s. 3;</li>
<li> SOR/2011-69, s. 1;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-82, s. 2;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-307, s. 4.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Vehicle Identification Number</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>115</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(1)ID0EBT0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every vehicle shall have a vehicle identification number and that vehicle identification number shall not be the same as the vehicle identification number of a vehicle having a model year of 1980 or later manufactured within the preceding 60&#xA0;years.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(1.1)ID0EBS0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A vehicle that is manufactured from an incomplete vehicle shall bear the vehicle identification number assigned by the incomplete vehicle manufacturer.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(1.2)ID0EBR0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1.2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Where a vehicle identification number is stated on a label bearing a statement of compliance affixed to a vehicle and the vehicle is altered, the vehicle identification number shall apply to the altered vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2)ID0EEQ0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(2.1), the vehicle identification number of each vehicle shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EBCQ0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be composed of capital, sanserif characters;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EEBQ0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be sunk into, embossed on or imprinted, clearly and indelibly, and in such a manner that the vehicle identification number cannot be removed without damaging or defacing the plate, label or vehicle, on</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBCBQ0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an integral or structural part of the vehicle other than the dash-board pad or dash-board cover,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBBBQ0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the dash-board or dash-board cover if it is not designed to be replaced following an air bag deployment, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(iii)ID0EBABQ0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a separate plate or label that is permanently affixed in a location referred to in subparagraph&#xA0;(i) or (ii); and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2)p-(c)ID0EEAQ0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a low-speed vehicle, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, passenger car, three-wheeled vehicle or truck having a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less, be</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2)p-(c)subp-(i)ID0EBCAQ0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;composed of characters having a minimum height of 4&#xA0;mm,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2)p-(c)subp-(ii)ID0EBBAQ0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;located inside the occupant compartment, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2)p-(c)subp-(iii)ID0EBAAQ0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;without any part of such vehicle being removed, readable through the vehicle glazing under daylight conditions by an observer having 20/20 vision Snellen whose eyepoint is located outside the vehicle adjacent to the left windshield pillar.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.1)ID0EIP0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The vehicle identification number of a snowmobile shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.1)p-(a)ID0EBGP0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be composed of capital, sans serif characters;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.1)p-(b)ID0EBFP0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be sunk into, embossed on, imprinted on or permanently affixed on the right exterior vertical surface of the track tunnel;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.1)p-(c)ID0EBEP0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be difficult to remove, replace or alter without detection;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.1)p-(d)ID0EBDP0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be composed of characters having a minimum height of 4&#xA0;mm;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.1)p-(e)ID0EBCP0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be legible and indelible;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.1)p-(f)ID0EBBP0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be legible without any part of the vehicle having to be removed; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.1)p-(g)ID0EBAP0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(g)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be protected from corrosion.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.2)ID0EBO0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2.2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;At the option of the manufacturer, the vehicle identification number may also be displayed in a bar code format that shall meet the requirements of section&#xA0;5.6 of guideline AIAG B-10, <cite class="XRefExternal">Trading Partner Labels Implementation Guideline</cite> (February, 2000), except for the specifications respecting code density and dimensions, which shall meet the requirements of section&#xA0;4.1 of standard AIAG B-2, <cite class="XRefExternal">Vehicle Identification Number Label Standard</cite> (June, 1988).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.3)ID0EDN0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2.3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every bar coded vehicle identification number shall be displayed on</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.3)p-(a)ID0EBBN0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the vehicle&#x2019;s compliance or information label; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.3)p-(b)ID0EBAN0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a separate label that is applied beside the compliance or information label in accordance with paragraphs&#xA0;7(<em>a</em>) and (<em>b</em>) of these Regulations.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.4)ID0EDM0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2.4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If the vehicle identification number is displayed on a label in a bar code format, it need not, until September&#xA0;1, 2012, also be applied to the vehicle in accordance with paragraph&#xA0;115(2)(<em>b</em>), but may, at the option of the manufacturer, be sunk into, embossed on or imprinted, clearly and indelibly, on</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.4)p-(a)ID0EBBM0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;any part of the vehicle that is not designed to be removed except for repair, other than glazing; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(2.4)p-(b)ID0EBAM0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a separate plate or label that is permanently affixed to a part referred to in paragraph (<em>a</em>).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(3)ID0EKL0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The vehicle identification number of any vehicle shall be alphanumeric and shall be composed of 17&#xA0;characters as follows:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBIL0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the first three characters, the third of which shall not be &#x201C;9&#x201D;, shall uniquely identify the manufacturer and the class of vehicle, if the manufacturer manufactures 1,000 or more vehicles of a prescribed class annually;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(3)p-(a.1)ID0EBHL0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the first three characters, the third of which shall be &#x201C;9&#x201D;, and the twelfth to fourteenth characters shall uniquely identify the manufacturer and the class of vehicle, if the manufacturer manufactures less than 1,000 vehicles of a prescribed class annually;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EEGL0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the fourth to eighth characters, inclusive, shall uniquely identify the decipherable information for the vehicle as set out in Column&#xA0;II of Table&#xA0;I, except that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(3)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBCGL0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seventh character shall be alphabetic for a multi-purpose passenger vehicle, passenger car, three-wheeled vehicle or truck having a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(3)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBBGL0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;subject to subparagraph&#xA0;(i), the characters and their positioning may be determined by the manufacturer, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(3)p-(b)subp-(iii)ID0EBAGL0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of an incomplete vehicle to be completed as a trailer, the decipherable information required for an incomplete vehicle in column&#xA0;II of Table&#xA0;I shall be that for a trailer;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(3)p-(c)ID0EBFL0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the ninth character shall be the check digit determined in accordance with subsections&#xA0;(7) and (8) after all other characters have been determined by the manufacturer;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(3)p-(d)ID0EBEL0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the tenth character shall be the code that corresponds to the vehicle model year as set out in Table&#xA0;II;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(3)p-(e)ID0EBDL0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the eleventh character shall identify the plant of manufacture of the vehicle;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(3)p-(f)ID0EBCL0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the twelfth to seventeenth characters shall be sequentially assigned by the manufacturer during the manufacturing process, if the manufacturer manufactures 1,000 or more vehicles of a prescribed class annually;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(3)p-(g)ID0EBBL0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(g)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the fifteenth to seventeenth characters shall be sequentially assigned by the manufacturer during the manufacturing process, if the manufacturer manufactures less than 1,000 vehicles of a prescribed class annually; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(3)p-(h)ID0EBAL0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(h)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the fourteenth to seventeenth characters shall be numeric for all vehicles and the thirteenth character shall be numeric if the vehicle is a multi-purpose passenger vehicle, passenger car, three-wheeled vehicle or truck having a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(4)ID0EBK0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2004-250, s. 3]</span>
</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(5)ID0EBJ0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Each character used in a vehicle identification number shall be one of the Arabic numerals or Roman letters specified in Table&#xA0;III.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(6)ID0EBI0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/88-535, s. 1]</span>
</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(7)ID0EFH0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The check digit referred to in paragraph&#xA0;(3)(<em>c</em>) shall be determined by</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(7)p-(a)ID0EBDH0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;assigning to each numeral of the vehicle identification number the actual mathematical value of that numeral;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(7)p-(b)ID0EBCH0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;assigning to each letter the mathematical value for that letter specified in Table&#xA0;IV;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(7)p-(c)ID0EBBH0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;multiplying the assigned value for each character of the vehicle identification number by the weight factor set out opposite that character in Table&#xA0;V; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(7)p-(d)ID0EBAH0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;adding together the numbers obtained under paragraph&#xA0;(<em>c</em>) and dividing the total by 11.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(8)ID0EBG0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The fractional portion of the quotient obtained by paragraph&#xA0;(7)(<em>d</em>), multiplied by 11, shall be the check digit, except that if that product is 10, the check digit shall be X.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(9)ID0EBF0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The Minister may require manufacturers of vehicles in respect of which this section applies to submit to the Minister those characters that uniquely identify a vehicle including, where applicable, the twelfth to fourteenth characters, inclusive, that constitute part of the identifier, for each make and class of vehicle manufactured and, in all cases, the information necessary to decipher the characters in vehicle identification numbers.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(10)ID0EBE0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If a character in a vehicle identification number identifies engine net power, the engine net power represented by that character shall not differ by more than 10 per cent from the actual engine net power.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(11)ID0EBD0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Manufacturers of vehicles in respect of which this section applies shall apply to the Canadian Vehicle Manufacturers&#x2019; Association for the characters referred to in paragraphs&#xA0;3(<em>a</em>) and (<em>a.1</em>) that uniquely identify the manufacturer and class of vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-(12)ID0EBC0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite subsections&#xA0;(1) to (11), every vehicle having a model year of 2009 or earlier shall comply with the requirements of this section as it read on the day before the day on which this subsection came into force.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-115ss-ID0EGB0MD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">
</span>
</a>&#xA0;</p>
<figure>

<tr>
<td headers="t615h0" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">2.</td>
<td headers="t615h1 t615h3" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">Multi-purpose passenger vehicle</td>
<td headers="t615h2 t615h4" class="noBorderBottom">Make, line, series, body type, engine type and gross vehicle weight rating. In addition, for multipurpose passenger vehicles with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less, all restraint system types and their location in the vehicle.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td headers="t615h0" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">3.</td>
<td headers="t615h1 t615h3" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">Truck</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td headers="t615h0" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">4.</td>
<td headers="t615h1 t615h3" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">Bus</td>
<td headers="t615h2 t615h4" class="noBorderBottom">Make, model or line, series, body type, engine type and brake system</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td headers="t615h0" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">5.</td>
<td headers="t615h1 t615h3" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">Trailer</td>
<td headers="t615h2 t615h4" class="noBorderBottom">Make, type of trailer, body type, length and axle configuration</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td headers="t615h0" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">6.</td>
<td headers="t615h1 t615h3" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">Motorcycle or restricted-use motorcycle</td>
<td headers="t615h2 t615h4" class="noBorderBottom">Make, type of cycle, line, engine type and engine net power</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td headers="t615h0" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">7.</td>
<td headers="t615h1 t615h3" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">Incomplete vehicle</td>
<td headers="t615h2 t615h4" class="noBorderBottom">Make, model or line, series, cab type, engine type and brake system</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td headers="t615h0" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">8.</td>
<td headers="t615h1 t615h3" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">Trailer converter dolly</td>
<td headers="t615h2 t615h4" class="noBorderBottom">Make, series and axle configuration</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td headers="t615h0" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">9.</td>
<td headers="t615h1 t615h3" class="noBorderRight noBorderBottom">Snowmobile</td>
<td headers="t615h2 t615h4" class="noBorderBottom">Make, type of snowmobile, line, engine type and engine net power</td>
</tr>
<tr>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Motor Vehicle Brake Fluids (Standard&#xA0;116)</span>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>[SOR/93-561, s. 5;</li>
<li> SOR/97-421, s. 7(F);</li>
<li> SOR/2011-238, s. 2]</li>
</ul>
</div>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>116</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-116ss-(1)ID0EBD0KD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The hydraulic brake system of a every passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck, bus, three-wheeled vehicle, motorcycle, trailer, and trailer converter dolly shall contain brake fluid that conforms to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;116, Motor Vehicle Brake Fluids</cite> (TSD&#xA0;116), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-116ss-(2)ID0ECC0KD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A reference in TSD&#xA0;116 to a standard published by ASTM that is set out in column&#xA0;1 of the table to this subsection may be read as a reference to the standard set out opposite that standard in column&#xA0;2 of the table.</p>
<figure>
<figcaption>
<p class="caption ">TABLE</p>
</figcaption>

<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-116ss-(3)ID0EBB0KD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 5]</span>
</p>

<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/79-940, s. 7;</li>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Power-Operated Window, Partition and Roof Panel Systems (Standard&#xA0;118)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>118</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-118ss-(1)ID0EBD0ID0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every power-operated window system, power-operated partition system and power-operated roof panel system fitted on a passenger car, a three-wheeled vehicle, an enclosed motorcycle or on a multi-purpose passenger vehicle or a truck with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;118, Power-Operated Window, Partition, and Roof Panel Systems</cite> (TSD&#xA0;118), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-118ss-(2)ID0EBC0ID0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;However, vehicles manufactured before October&#xA0;1, 2010, need not comply with the requirements of S6 of TSD&#xA0;118.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-118ss-(3)ID0EBB0ID0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 6]</span>
</p>
</li>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Tire Selection and Rims for Motor Vehicles With a GVWR of More Than 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;KG (Standard&#xA0;120)</span>
</h3>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">General</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>120</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-120ss-(1)ID0EBI0FD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every motor vehicle with a GVWR of more than 4 536 kg, except vehicles imported temporarily for special purposes, every three-wheeled vehicle equipped with tires other than passenger car tires, every motorcycle except motor tricycles equipped with passenger car tires, and every tire rim manufactured for use on those vehicles shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No. 120, Tire Selection and Rims for Motor Vehicles With a GVWR of More Than 4,536 kg</cite> (TSD 120), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;120</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-120ss-(2)ID0EEG0FD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In addition to conforming to the requirements of S5.1.3 of TSD 120, used or retreaded tires installed on a bus, trailer, trailer converter dolly or truck shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-120ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EBCG0FD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;not have been the subject of a notice of defect;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-120ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EBBG0FD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;have a tread depth greater than 1.5 mm; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-120ss-(2)p-(c)ID0EDAG0FD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;have been originally manufactured to conform to the requirements of any of the following that applied at the time of manufacture:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-120ss-(2)p-(c)subp-(i)ID0EBBAG0FD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of used tires, the <cite class="XRefExternalRegulation">
<a href="http://laws-lois.justice.gc.ca/eng/regulations/SOR-2013-198">Motor Vehicle Tire Safety Regulations</a>
</cite> or the <cite class="XRefExternalRegulation">
<a href="http://laws-lois.justice.gc.ca/eng/regulations/SOR-95-148">Motor Vehicle Tire Safety Regulations, 1995</a>
</cite>, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-120ss-(2)p-(c)subp-(ii)ID0EBAAG0FD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of retreaded tires, section 4 of the <cite class="XRefExternalRegulation">
<a href="http://laws-lois.justice.gc.ca/eng/regulations/SOR-2013-198">Motor Vehicle Tire Safety Regulations</a>
</cite>, Schedule V to the <cite class="XRefExternalRegulation">
<a href="http://laws-lois.justice.gc.ca/eng/regulations/SOR-95-148">Motor Vehicle Tire Safety Regulations, 1995</a>
</cite>, the United States <cite class="XRefExternal">Federal Motor Vehicle Safety Standard No. 119</cite> or the <cite class="XRefExternal">Japanese Industrial Standard JIS D4230</cite>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-120ss-(3)ID0EBF0FD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The information specified in S5.3 of TSD 120 shall be in both official languages.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-120ss-(4)ID0EDE0FD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The following definitions apply for the purposes of TSD 120.</p>
<dl class="Definition">
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>load rating</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>load rating</dfn>
</span> means the maximum load a tire is rated to carry at a given inflation pressure. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">charge nominale</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>maximum load rating</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>maximum load rating</dfn>
</span> means the load rating at the maximum permissible inflation pressure for that tire. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">limite de charge nominale</span>) </p>
</dd>
</dl>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Load Range Identification Symbol</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-120ss-(5)ID0EBC0FD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In the case of vehicles equipped with light-truck tires, the load range identification symbol shall appear either on the compliance label required by section 6 of these Regulations or on the tire information label.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-120ss-(6)ID0EBB0FD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 7]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Air Brake Systems (Standard&#xA0;121)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>121</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(1)ID0EBH0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(2), this section applies in respect of every truck, bus and trailer that is equipped with an air brake system.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(2)ID0EIG0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;This section does not apply in respect of the following trucks, buses and trailers:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EBGG0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a trailer that has a width of more than 2.6&#xA0;m with extendable equipment in the fully retracted position and that is equipped with two short-track axles in a line across the width of the trailer;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EBFG0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a truck, bus or trailer that is equipped with an axle that has a gross axle weight rating of 13&#xA0;154&#xA0;kg or more;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(2)p-(c)ID0EBEG0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a truck or bus that has a speed attainable in 3.2&#xA0;km (2 miles) of not more than 53.1&#xA0;km/h;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(2)p-(d)ID0EBDG0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a truck that has a speed attainable in 3.2&#xA0;km (2 miles) of not more than 72.3&#xA0;km/h, an unloaded vehicle mass of not less than 95% of its GVWR, and no capacity to carry occupants other than the driver and the operating crew;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(2)p-(e)ID0EBCG0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a trailer that has a GVWR of more than 54&#xA0;432&#xA0;kg and whose body conforms to that described in the definition <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>heavy hauler trailer</dfn>
</span> in subsection&#xA0;2(1) of these Regulations;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(2)p-(f)ID0EBBG0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a trailer that has an unloaded vehicle mass of not less than 95% of its GVWR; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(2)p-(g)ID0EBAG0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(g)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a load divider dolly.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(3)ID0EBF0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every truck, bus and trailer shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;121, Air Brake Systems</cite> (TSD&#xA0;121), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(4)ID0EBE0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If a truck or bus is equipped with a front brake pressure limiting valve, that valve shall be automatic and shall operate while the service brakes are applied.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(5)ID0EBD0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Any antilock brake system malfunction indicator referred to in S5.1.6.2 of TSD&#xA0;121 shall be the antilock brake system tell-tale set out in section&#xA0;101.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(6)ID0EBC0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The parking brake static retardation force test that is referred to in S5.6.1 of TSD&#xA0;121 shall be conducted in both a forward and a rearward direction.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-121ss-(7)ID0EBB0DD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 8]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">

<li> SOR/79-547, s. 1;</li>
<li> SOR/79-940, s. 7;</li>
<li> SOR/80-638, s. 2;</li>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Motorcycle Brake Systems (Standard&#xA0;122)</span>
</h3>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">General</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>122</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(1)ID0EDS0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every motorcycle shall conform to</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(1)p-(a)ID0EBBS0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No. 122, Motorcycle Brake Systems</cite> (TSD 122), as amended from time to time; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(1)p-(b)ID0EBAS0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the requirements set out in paragraphs 5 and 6 and Annex 3 of ECE Regulation No. 78, Revision 1, <cite class="XRefExternal">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Vehicles of Categories L<sub>1</sub>, L<sub>2</sub>, L<sub>3</sub>, L<sub>4</sub> and L<sub>5</sub> with Regard to Braking</cite>, in the version in effect on June 24, 2008, as amended by any subsequent amendments in the 03 series of amendments (ECE Regulation No. 78).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(2)ID0EBR0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If a motorcycle is designed to operate with or without a sidecar, it shall conform to the requirements of subsection (1) in each of those configurations.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(3)ID0EBQ0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every motorcycle shall have a mark containing the symbol &#x201C;DOT&#x201D; followed by a reference to the type of brake fluid recommended by the manufacturer.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(4)ID0EEP0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The mark shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EBCP0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be permanently affixed and of a colour that contrasts with its background, or be engraved or embossed;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EBBP0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be located, so as to be visible without obstruction, either on or within 101.6 mm of the brake-fluid reservoir filler plug or cap; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(4)p-(c)ID0EBAP0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;have letters and numbers at least 2.38 mm in height.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(5)ID0EDO0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The English and French versions of the owner&#x2019;s manual shall include, respectively, the English or French version of the following warning about brake fluid:</p>
<p class="ContinuedSectionSubsection">&#x201C;WARNING: Clean filler cap before removing. Use only [here insert the information contained on the mark referred to in subsection (3)] fluid from a sealed container.&#x201D;</p>
<p class="ContinuedSectionSubsection">
<span class="otherLang" lang="fr"> AVERTISSEMENT&#xA0;: Nettoyer le bouchon de remplissage avant de l&#x2019;enlever. Utiliser seulement du liquide [ins&#xE9;rer ici les renseignements figurant sur la marque vis&#xE9;e au paragraphe (3)] provenant d&#x2019;un contenant scell&#xE9;. </span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Technical Standards Document No. 122</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(6)ID0EBM0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of TSD&#xA0;122, the definitions <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>antilock brake system</dfn>
</span> or <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>ABS</dfn>
</span>, <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>control</dfn>
</span>, <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>split service brake system</dfn>
</span> and <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>stopping distance</dfn>
</span> in subsection 2(1) of these Regulations, and section 5.3 of these Regulations, do not apply.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(7)_to_(11)ID0EBL0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7) to (11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2015-111, s. 2]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">ECE Regulation No. 78</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(12)ID0EGJ0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of this section,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(12)p-(a)ID0EBEJ0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a reference to vehicle category &#x201C;L<sub>1</sub>&#x201D; in ECE Regulation No. 78 is a reference to a limited-speed motorcycle that is designed to travel on two wheels in contact with the ground and that has a maximum speed of 50 km/h or less;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(12)p-(b)ID0EBDJ0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a reference to vehicle category &#x201C;L<sub>2</sub>&#x201D; in ECE Regulation No. 78 is a reference to a limited-speed motorcycle that is designed to travel on three wheels in contact with the ground and that has a maximum speed of 50 km/h or less;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(12)p-(c)ID0EBCJ0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a reference to vehicle category &#x201C;L<sub>3</sub>&#x201D; in ECE Regulation No. 78 is a reference to a motorcycle that is designed to travel on two wheels in contact with the ground, that has a maximum speed of more than 50 km/h and that is not equipped with a sidecar;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(12)p-(d)ID0EBBJ0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a reference to vehicle category &#x201C;L<sub>4</sub>&#x201D; in ECE Regulation No. 78 is a reference to a motorcycle that is designed to travel on two wheels in contact with the ground and that is equipped with a sidecar, and to a motorcycle that is designed to travel on three wheels in contact with the ground that are asymmetrically arranged in relation to the longitudinal median plane; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(12)p-(e)ID0EBAJ0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a reference to vehicle category &#x201C;L<sub>5</sub>&#x201D; in ECE Regulation No. 78 is a reference to a motorcycle that has a maximum speed of more than 50 km/h and that is designed to travel on three wheels in contact with the ground that are symmetrically arranged in relation to the longitudinal median plane.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(13)ID0EBI0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(13)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of this section and despite the definition <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>three-wheeled vehicle</dfn>
</span> in subsection 2(1) of these Regulations, the term <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>three-wheeled vehicle</dfn>
</span> used in ECE Regulation No. 78 means a motorcycle that is designed to travel on two wheels in contact with the ground and that is equipped with a sidecar, and a motorcycle that is designed to travel on three wheels in contact with the ground.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(14)ID0EBH0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(14)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of paragraph 1.1.3 of Annex 3 of ECE Regulation No. 78, the peak braking coefficient shall be measured in accordance with paragraph 1.1.3(a) of that Regulation.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(15)ID0EBG0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(15)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of paragraph 2.4 of Annex 3 of ECE Regulation No. 78, the brake temperature shall be measured in accordance with paragraph 2.4(b) of that Regulation.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(16)ID0EBF0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(16)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite the second sentence of paragraph 5.1.6 of ECE Regulation No. 78, sidecar wheels are never required to be equipped with a brake.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(17)ID0EBE0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(17)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A reference to a warning lamp in paragraph&#xA0;5.1.12 of ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;78 shall be read as a reference to the tell-tale for a brake system malfunction set out in the table to section&#xA0;101 of this Schedule.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(18)ID0EBD0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(18)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A reference to a warning lamp in paragraph&#xA0;5.1.13 of ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;78 shall be read as a reference to the tell-tale for an antilock brake system malfunction set out in the table to section&#xA0;101 of this Schedule.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Transitional Provision</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-122ss-(19)ID0EBB0AD0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(19)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite subsections (1) to (18), a motorcycle may, until September 1, 2016, conform to the requirements of this section as it read immediately before the day on which this subsection comes into force.</p>
</li>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Motorcycle Controls and Displays (Standard&#xA0;123)</span>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>[SOR/93-31, s. 4;</li>
<li> SOR/2007-180, s. 9;</li>
<li> SOR/2011-238, s. 3]</li>
</ul>
</div>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>123</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(1)ID0EBQ05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every motorcycle, except those designed and sold exclusively for use by law enforcement agencies, shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;123, Motorcycle Controls and Displays</cite> (TSD&#xA0;123), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(2)ID0EHP05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every motorcycle shall be equipped with the following controls:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EBFP05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a horn;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EBEP05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a fuel tank shutoff valve;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(2)p-(c)ID0EBDP05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a twist-grip throttle;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(2)p-(d)ID0EBCP05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a front wheel brake;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(2)p-(e)ID0EBBP05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a rear wheel brake; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(2)p-(f)ID0EBAP05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an ignition switch.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(3)ID0EBO05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The ignition switch is optional in the case of a limited-speed motorcycle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(4)ID0EBN05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Item&#xA0;12 of Table&#xA0;3 to TSD&#xA0;123 applies to manual fuel tank shutoff valves only.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(5)ID0EBM05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Any control or display that is not listed in Table&#xA0;3 to TSD&#xA0;123 and for which no other identification requirements are specified in these Regulations shall, if identified, be identified by the corresponding symbol set out in International Standard ISO&#xA0;6727, <cite class="XRefExternal">Road vehicles &#x2014; Motorcycles &#x2014; Symbols for controls, indicators and telltales</cite>, as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(6)ID0EBL05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Any control or display for which a symbol is not specified in Table&#xA0;3 to TSD&#xA0;123 or in International Standard ISO&#xA0;6727, <cite class="XRefExternal">Road vehicles &#x2014; Motorcycles &#x2014; Symbols for controls, indicators and telltales</cite>, as amended from time to time, may be identified by a symbol designed by the manufacturer in compliance with the principles specified in that Standard.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(7)ID0EBK05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Wherever the term &#x201C;motorcycle&#x201D; is used in International Standard ISO&#xA0;6727, <cite class="XRefExternal">Road vehicles &#x2014; Motorcycles &#x2014; Symbols for controls, indicators and telltales</cite>, as amended from time to time, it shall have the same meaning as &#x201C;motorcycle&#x201D; in subsection&#xA0;2(1) of these Regulations.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(8)ID0EBJ05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The words and abbreviations that must be displayed under this section shall be displayed in both official languages. However, if there is insufficient space to display the words or abbreviations identifying the ignition, tachometer or fuel tank shutoff valve in both official languages in a readily visible manner, they may be displayed in one official language only.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(9)ID0EBI05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The symbols and abbreviations used to identify the controls and displays of a motorcycle shall be provided in writing in the English and French versions of the owner&#x2019;s manual, accompanied by a full explanation.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(10)ID0EBH05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite the requirements of item&#xA0;8 of Table&#xA0;3 to TSD&#xA0;123, a speedometer fitted on a motorcycle shall be calibrated in kilometres per hour or in kilometres per hour and miles per hour. Digital speedometers that switch between kilometres per hour and miles per hour are permitted if the unit of measure is identified.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(11)ID0EBG05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In the case of analogue speedometer displays, the kilometre-per-hour scale on the speedometer shall increase in a clockwise direction. Major graduations and numerals shall appear at 10- or 20-kilometre-per-hour intervals and minor graduations at 5- or 10-kilometre-per-hour intervals.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(12)ID0EBF05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;An odometer or trip odometer installed on a motorcycle adjacent to the speedometer shall display distances in the same unit of measure as that of the predominant speedometer scale. If the odometer or trip odometer is not adjacent to the speedometer or switches between kilometres and miles independently of the speedometer, the odometer or trip odometer shall display distances in kilometres or miles and shall identify the unit of measure used.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(13)ID0EBE05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(13)</span>
</a>&#xA0;S5.2.4 of TSD&#xA0;123 does not apply to motor tricycles.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(14)ID0EBD05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(14)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S5.2.5 of TSD&#xA0;123, it is not necessary for a footrest for a passenger on a motorcycle to fold rearward and upward when not in use.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(15)ID0EBC05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(15)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A turn signal lamp display fitted on a motorcycle shall be green or yellow.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-123ss-(16)ID0EBB05C0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(16)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 9]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/79-306, s. 5;</li>
<li> SOR/79-940, s. 7;</li>
<li> SOR/82-656, s. 3;</li>
<li> SOR/88-268, s. 10;</li>
<li> SOR/93-31, s. 5;</li>
<li> SOR/94-374, s. 5(F);</li>

<li> SOR/96-366, s. 8;</li>

<li> SOR/98-524, s. 4(F);</li>
<li> SOR/2003-272, s. 19;</li>
<li> SOR/2007-180, s. 10;</li>
<li> SOR/2009-318, s. 11;</li>
<li> SOR/2011-238, s. 3;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-307, s. 9.</li>
</ul>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Light Vehicle Brake Systems (Standard&#xA0;135)</span>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>[SOR/2001-35, s. 5;</li>
<li> SOR/2011-238, s. 3]</li>
</ul>
</div>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>135</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-135ss-(1)ID0EBF0WC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every passenger car, every three-wheeled vehicle and every multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck and bus with a GVWR of 3&#xA0;500&#xA0;kg or less shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;135, Light Vehicle Brake Systems</cite> (TSD&#xA0;135), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-135ss-(2)ID0EBE0WC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The statement set out in&#xA0;S5.4.3 of TSD&#xA0;135 may be replaced by another statement to the same effect.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-135ss-(3)ID0EBD0WC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A brake warning indicator referred to in S5.5.5 of TSD 135 shall, when activated due to a condition set out in S5.5.1 of TSD 135, display the identification symbol set out in the table to section 101 of this Schedule that corresponds to that condition, but if the vehicle is fitted with a single common brake warning indicator, the indicator shall display the identification symbol for a brake system malfunction set out in the table to section 101 of this Schedule.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-135ss-(4)ID0EBC0WC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The word &#x201C;car&#x201D; used in S6.3.6 and S6.3.7 of the English version of TSD 135 shall be read as &#x201C;vehicle&#x201D;.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-135ss-(5)_to_(7)ID0EBB0WC0BA">

</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2015-24, s. 6]</span>
