<h2 class="SchedHeadL1">
<span class="HLabel1">PART III</span>
</h2>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Section">
<strong>200</strong>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/83-138, s. 2]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Occupant Protection</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>201</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(1)ID0EFN0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In this section,</p>
<dl class="Definition">
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>head impact area</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>head impact area</dfn>
</span> means the non-glazed surfaces of the interior of the vehicle that are capable of being contacted statically by the head form of a measuring device in accordance with the following procedure or its graphic equivalent: </p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(1)Definitionp-(a)ID0EDCDN0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at each designated seating position, by placing the pivot point of the measuring device,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(1)Definitionp-(a)subp-(i)ID0EDBCDN0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;for seats that are adjustable fore and aft, at</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(1)Definitionp-(a)subp-(i)Clause(A)ID0EBBBCDN0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(A)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seating reference point, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(1)Definitionp-(a)subp-(i)Clause(B)ID0EBABCDN0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(B)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a point 130&#xA0;mm (five inches) horizontally forward of the seating reference point displaced vertically 20&#xA0;mm (0.75&#xA0;inches) or a distance equal to the rise that results from a 130&#xA0;mm (five inches) forward adjustment of the seat, and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(1)Definitionp-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBACDN0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;for seats that are not adjustable fore and aft, at the seating reference point,</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(1)Definitionp-(b)ID0EBBDN0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;with the pivot point to top-of-head dimension at each adjustment allowed for the measuring device by the interior dimension of the vehicle, by determining all contact points above the lower windshield glass line and forward of the seating reference point, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(1)Definitionp-(c)ID0EBADN0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;beginning with the head form of the measuring device at each contact point referred to in paragraph&#xA0;(<em>b</em>) and with the measuring device in a vertical position if no contact point exists for a particular adjusted length, by pivoting the measuring device forward and downward through all arcs in vertical planes to 90&#xB0; each side of the longitudinal plane through the seating reference point until the head form contacts an interior surface or until it is tangent to a horizontal plane 25&#xA0;mm (1&#xA0;inch) above the seating reference point, whichever occurs first; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">zone d&#x2019;impact de la tte</span>)</p>
</li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>interior compartment door</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>interior compartment door</dfn>
</span> means any door in the interior of a vehicle installed by the manufacturer as a cover for storage space normally used for personal effects; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">porte de compartiment int&#xE9;rieur</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>measuring device</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>measuring device</dfn>
</span> means a device having a spherical head form with a diameter of 165&#xA0;mm (6.5&#xA0;inches) attached to a pivot, with the distance between the pivot point and the top of the head form being adjustable at any point between 740&#xA0;mm (29&#xA0;inches) and 840&#xA0;mm (33&#xA0;inches); (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">appareil de mesure</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>pelvic impact area</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>pelvic impact area</dfn>
</span> means that area of the door or body side panel adjacent to any outboard designated seating position that is bounded by: </p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(1)Definitionp-(a)ID0EBBAN0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;horizontal planes 180&#xA0;mm (seven inches) above and 100&#xA0;mm (four inches) below the seating reference point, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(1)Definitionp-(b)ID0EBAAN0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;vertical transverse planes 200&#xA0;mm (eight inches) forward and 50&#xA0;mm (two inches) rearward of the seating reference point. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">zone d&#x2019;impact pelvienne</span>)</p>
</li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(2)ID0EBM0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;This section applies to passenger cars and to multi-purpose passenger vehicles, trucks and buses with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg (10,000&#xA0;pounds) or less.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(3)ID0EDL0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(3.2), the instrument panel of a vehicle shall be constructed so that the deceleration of a spherical head form with a weight of 6,8&#xA0;kg (15&#xA0;pounds) and a diameter of 165&#xA0;mm (6.5&#xA0;inches) does not exceed 80&#xA0;<em>g</em> continuously for more than 3&#xA0;ms when the area of the instrument panel that is within the head impact area is impacted in accordance with the test procedure referred to in subsection&#xA0;(3.1) at a relative velocity of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBBL0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;19.3&#xA0;km/h, in the case of a vehicle that is equipped, at the right front outboard designated seating position, with an air bag and a Type&#xA0;2 manual seat belt assembly that conform to section&#xA0;208; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBAL0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;24&#xA0;km/h (15&#xA0;mph), in the case of any other vehicle.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(3.1)ID0EDK0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The test of the instrument panel shall be performed in accordance with SAE Recommended Practice, &#x201C;Motor Vehicle Instrument Panel Laboratory Impact Test Procedure &#x2014; Head Area &#x2014; SAE J921b&#x201D; (November 1971) and using the instrumentation whose performance is specified in SAE Recommended Practice, &#x201C;Instrumentation For Impact Tests &#x2014; SAE J211&#x201D; (October 1988) except that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(3.1)p-(a)ID0EBBK0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the origin of the line tangent to the surface of the instrument panel shall be a point on a transverse horizontal line through a point 130&#xA0;mm (5&#xA0;inches) horizontally forward of the seating reference point of the front outboard designated seating position, displaced vertically 19&#xA0;mm (0.75&#xA0;inches) or a distance equal to the rise in the seating reference point that results from a 130&#xA0;mm (5&#xA0;inch) forward adjustment of the seat; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(3.1)p-(b)ID0EBAK0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the impact shall be directed in a vertical plane parallel to the longitudinal axis of the vehicle or in a plane normal to the surface at the point of contact.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(3.2)ID0EGJ0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3.2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subsection&#xA0;(3) does not apply to</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(3.2)p-(a)ID0EBEJ0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;console assemblies;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(3.2)p-(b)ID0EBDJ0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;areas less than 130&#xA0;mm (5&#xA0;inches) from the junction of the instrument panel and the inside of the side structure of the body;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(3.2)p-(c)ID0EBCJ0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;areas closer to the junction of the windshield and the instrument panel than those areas that are capable of being contacted by the head form with the windshield in place;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(3.2)p-(d)ID0EBBJ0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;areas outboard of all points on the line of contact of the head form with the instrument panel when the head form is moved along the inboard side of a vertical longitudinal plane tangent to the inboard edge of the steering wheel; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(3.2)p-(e)ID0EBAJ0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;areas below any point at which a vertical line is tangent to the rearmost surface of the instrument panel.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4)ID0EFI0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(4.1), the seats of a vehicle shall be constructed so that the deceleration of a spherical head form with a weight of 6,8&#xA0;kg (15&#xA0;pounds) and a diameter of 165&#xA0;mm (6.5&#xA0;inches) does not exceed 80&#xA0;<em>g</em> continuously for more than 3&#xA0;ms when the area of a seatback that is within the head impact area is impacted, at a relative velocity of 24&#xA0;km/h (15&#xA0;miles per hour), in accordance with SAE Recommended Practice, &#x201C;Motor Vehicle Seatback Assembly Laboratory Impact Test Procedure &#x2014; Head Area &#x2014; SAE J346&#x201D; (June 1971) using the instrumentation whose performance is specified in SAE Recommended Practice, &#x201C;Instrumentation For Impact Tests &#x2014; SAE J211&#x201D; (October 1988), except that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EBDI0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the origin of the line tangent to the uppermost component of the seatback frame shall be a point on a transverse horizontal line through the seating reference point of the appropriate rear outboard designated seating position, with adjustable forward seats in their rearmost design driving position and reclinable forward seatbacks in their normal design position;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EBCI0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the impact shall be directed in a vertical plane parallel to the longitudinal axis of the vehicle or in a plane normal to the surface at the point of contact;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4)p-(c)ID0EDBI0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4)p-(c)subp-(i)ID0EDBBI0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a seat without head restraints, each test shall be performed</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4)p-(c)subp-(i)Clause(A)ID0EBBBBI0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(A)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in respect of each individual split seatback or bucket seat seatback, between two points each situated 100&#xA0;mm (4&#xA0;inches) outboard of its centreline, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4)p-(c)subp-(i)Clause(B)ID0EBABBI0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(B)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in respect of each bench seat seatback, between two points each situated 100&#xA0;mm (4&#xA0;inches) outboard of the centreline of each outboard designated seating position, and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4)p-(c)subp-(ii)ID0EBABI0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a seat with head restraints, each test shall be conducted at a point on the centreline of each head restraint with the head restraint in place at its lowest adjusted position; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4)p-(d)ID0EBAI0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a type of seat that is installed in more than one body style, tests conducted at the foremost and rearmost positions identified by the application of paragraph&#xA0;(<em>a</em>) shall be deemed to be conclusive for all intermediate positions.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4.1)ID0EHH0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subsection&#xA0;(4) does not apply in respect of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4.1)p-(a)ID0EBFH0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;seats installed in a school bus that complies with section&#xA0;222 when tested in accordance with <cite class="XRefExternal">Motor Vehicle Safety Test Methods</cite>, section&#xA0;222, &#x201C;School Bus Passenger Seating and Crash Protection&#x201D; (December&#xA0;19, 1983);</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4.1)p-(b)ID0EBEH0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the rearmost seats;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4.1)p-(c)ID0EBDH0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;side-facing seats;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4.1)p-(d)ID0EBCH0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;back-to-back seats;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4.1)p-(e)ID0EBBH0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;folding auxiliary jump seats; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(4.1)p-(f)ID0EBAH0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;temporary seats.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(5)ID0EEG0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(7), every interior compartment door located in an instrument panel, console, seatback or side panel adjacent to an outboard designated seating position shall remain closed when</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(5)p-(a)ID0EBCG0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the interior compartment door latch system is tested by being subjected to a force equal to an inertia load of 10&#xA0;<em>g</em> in a horizontal transverse direction and an inertia load of 10&#xA0;<em>g</em> in a vertical direction, in accordance with SAE Recommended Practice, &#x201C;Passenger Car Side Door Latch Systems &#x2014; SAE J839&#x201D; (July 1982);</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(5)p-(b)ID0EDBG0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;one of the following tests is conducted, namely,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(5)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBBG0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the vehicle is tested by being impacted perpendicularly into a fixed collision barrier at a forward longitudinal velocity of 48&#xA0;km/h (30&#xA0;miles per hour), or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(5)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBABG0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the interior compartment door latch system is tested by being subjected to a force equal to a horizontal inertia load of 30&#xA0;<em>g</em> in a longitudinal direction, in accordance with SAE Recommended Practice, &#x201C;Passenger Car Side Door Latch Systems &#x2014; SAE J839&#x201D; (July 1982); and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(5)p-(c)ID0EBAG0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the instrument panel or seatback is tested in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(3) or (4), as the case may be.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(6)ID0EBF0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/92-689, s. 1]</span>
</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(7)ID0EBE0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;All interior compartment door assemblies that have a locking device shall be tested with the locking device in an unlocked position.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(8)ID0EBD0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A sun visor shall be provided at each front outboard designated seating position on every vehicle and shall be constructed of, or covered with, energy absorbing material and so mounted that each mounting shall not have a rigid material edge with a radius of less than 3&#xA0;mm (0.125&#xA0;inch) that is statically contactable by a spherical head form with a diameter of 165&#xA0;mm (6.5&#xA0;inches).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(9)ID0EEC0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Each arm-rest installed on a vehicle, other than an arm-rest referred to in subsection&#xA0;(10), shall meet at least one of the following performance requirements:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(9)p-(a)ID0EBCC0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be constructed of energy absorbing material that collapses laterally at least 50&#xA0;mm (2&#xA0;inches) without permitting contact with any underlying rigid material;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(9)p-(b)ID0EDBC0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be constructed</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(9)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBBC0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;of energy absorbing material that collapses to within 32&#xA0;mm (1.25&#xA0;inches) of a rigid test panel surface without permitting contact with any rigid material, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(9)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBABC0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;so that the vertical height of any rigid material between 13&#xA0;mm (0.5&#xA0;inches) and 32&#xA0;mm (1.25&#xA0;inches) from the panel surface is not less than 25&#xA0;mm (1&#xA0;inch); and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(9)p-(c)ID0EBAC0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;when measured vertically in side elevation, provide at least 50&#xA0;mm (2&#xA0;inches) of coverage within the pelvic impact area along not less than 50&#xA0;mm (2&#xA0;inches) of its length.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(10)ID0EDB0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Each arm-rest that folds into the seat back or between two seat backs of a vehicle shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(10)p-(a)ID0EBBB0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;comply with subsection&#xA0;(9); or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-201ss-(10)p-(b)ID0EBAB0SC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be constructed of or covered with energy absorbing material.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/83-138, s. 2;</li>
<li> SOR/86-453, s. 2;</li>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Head Restraints</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Section">
<strong>202</strong>&#xA0;Every multi-purpose passenger vehicle, bus or truck with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less, every passenger car and every three-wheeled vehicle shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No. 202, Head Restraints</cite> (TSD 202), as amended from time to time.</p>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/95-60, s. 2;</li>
<li> SOR/2003-272, s. 21;</li>
<li> SOR/2006-94, s. 4(E);</li>
<li> SOR/2007-180, s. 11;</li>
<li> SOR/2008-72, s. 4(F);</li>
<li> SOR/2009-122, s. 1;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-82, s. 5;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-307, s. 13.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Driver Impact Protection and Steering Control System</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>203</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-203ss-(1)ID0EBF0OC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The steering control system of a vehicle shall be constructed in such a manner that no component or attachment &#x2014; including any horn actuating mechanism &#x2014; is capable, during normal driving manoeuvres, of catching the driver&#x2019;s clothing or the driver&#x2019;s jewellery, such as a watch, a ring or a bracelet other than a bracelet with loosely attached or dangling members.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-203ss-(2)ID0EBE0OC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(4), the steering control system of every passenger car and three-wheeled vehicle and every multi-purpose passenger vehicle, bus and truck &#x2014; other than a walk-in van &#x2014; with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less shall be tested in accordance with SAE Recommended Practice J944, <cite class="XRefExternal">Steering Control System &#x2014; Passenger Car &#x2014; Laboratory Test Procedure</cite> (June 1980).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-203ss-(3)ID0EDD0OC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The following requirements with respect to the steering control system shall be met during the test referred to in subsection&#xA0;(2):</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-203ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBBD0OC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the system shall be impacted by a body block at a relative velocity of 24&#xA0;km/h;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-203ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBAD0OC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the impact force developed on the chest of the body block and transmitted to the system shall not exceed 11&#xA0;120&#xA0;N, except for intervals with a cumulative duration of not more than 3&#xA0;ms.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-203ss-(4)ID0EBC0OC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subsections (2) and (3) do not apply to a vehicle that conforms to the requirements of S5 and S14 of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No. 208, Occupant Crash Protection</cite> (TSD 208), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-203ss-(5)ID0EBB0OC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 14]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Glazing Materials</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>205</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(1)ID0EBO0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of this section, <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>bus</dfn>
</span>, <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>motorhome</dfn>
</span>, <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>multi-purpose passenger vehicle</dfn>
</span>, <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>passenger car</dfn>
</span>, <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>readily removable windows</dfn>
</span>, <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>trailer</dfn>
</span>, and <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>truck</dfn>
</span> in the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996 shall have the same meaning as in subsection&#xA0;2(1) of these Regulations.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(2)ID0EBN0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of this section, the definition <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>motor vehicle</dfn>
</span> in the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996 does not apply.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(3)ID0EBM0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsections&#xA0;(4) to (13), each piece of glazing material for use in a vehicle, except a trailer other than a bus trailer, shall meet the requirements of the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(4)ID0EBL0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In the event of any inconsistency or conflict between the requirements for items&#xA0;1 to 16B listed in section&#xA0;4.2 of the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996 and the requirements shown in Table&#xA0;1 of that Standard, the latter shall prevail.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(5)ID0EBK0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Any glazing material for use in a multi-purpose passenger vehicle shall meet the requirements specified in the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996 for glazing material for use in trucks.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(5.1)ID0EBJ0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Any glazing material for use in a three-wheeled vehicle shall meet the requirements specified in the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996 for glazing materials for use in passenger cars.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(6)ID0EBI0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite section&#xA0;6 of the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996, the exposed edges of tempered glazing material installed in school buses need not be banded.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(7)ID0EBH0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Instead of using the procedures described in the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996 for tests 1 and 16 described in that Standard, those tests may be conducted using the procedures described for tests&#xA0;1 and 16 in the ANSI Z26 Safety Code &#x2014; 1990.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(8)ID0EBG0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Instead of using the steel frame made in accordance with Figure&#xA0;1 in the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996 required for tests&#xA0;6, 8 to 14, 26 and 29 described in that Standard, those tests may be conducted using a maple or similar hardwood frame made in accordance with Figure&#xA0;1 in the ANSI Z26 Safety Code &#x2014; 1990.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(9)ID0EEF0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Instead of conducting the fracture test using the procedure for test&#xA0;7 described in the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996 and testing the specimens specified in that test, the fracture test may be conducted using the following procedure:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(9)p-(a)ID0EBCF0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;test the uncracked and unbroken specimens remaining from test 6 described in the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(9)p-(b)ID0EBBF0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;continue the procedure for test 6 by increasing the height from which the sphere is dropped by increments of 305&#xA0;mm starting from a height of 3.35&#xA0;m until each specimen is broken; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(9)p-(c)ID0EBAF0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;interpret the results in accordance with test&#xA0;7.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(10)ID0EBE0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When conducting tests&#xA0;9 and 12 described in the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996, the specimens of the glazing materials listed in item&#xA0;14 of section&#xA0;4 of the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996 may be clamped in the frame of the holding fixture.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(11)ID0EBD0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When conducting test&#xA0;26 described in the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996, the specimens of the glazing materials listed in item&#xA0;14 of section&#xA0;4 of the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996 shall be clamped in the frame of the holding fixture.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(12)ID0EBC0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Any plastic glazing material that meets the requirements of item&#xA0;7 of section&#xA0;4 of the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996 may be used in that portion of a motorcycle windshield that is below an imaginary horizontal plane located 380&#xA0;mm vertically above the lowest seating position.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(13)ID0EDB0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(13)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Each piece of glazing material installed in a vehicle shall be legibly and permanently marked with</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(13)p-(a)ID0EBBB0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the appropriate marking required by section&#xA0;7 of the ANSI Z26 Safety Standard &#x2014; 1996; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-205ss-(13)p-(b)ID0EBAB0KC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an approved code mark, assigned by the Minister to the glazing material manufacturer, in letters and numbers not less than 1.8&#xA0;mm in height.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/82-656, s. 4;</li>
<li> SOR/84-336, s. 1;</li>
<li> SOR/86-161, s. 2;</li>
<li> SOR/88-268, s. 11;</li>
<li> SOR/93-5, s. 3(F);</li>
<li> SOR/94-670, s. 2(F);</li>
<li> SOR/94-717, s. 2;</li>
<li> SOR/2002-55, s. 16;</li>
<li> SOR/2002-187, s. 2;</li>
<li> SOR/2003-272, s. 22;</li>

<li> SOR/2006-94, s. 4(E).</li>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Door Locks and Door Retention Components (Standard&#xA0;206)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">

</a>&#xA0;Every bus with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less, enclosed motorcycle, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, three-wheeled vehicle, passenger car and truck that is equipped with side doors or back doors shall be so equipped in accordance with either</p>

</a>&#xA0;the general requirements, performance requirements and test procedures set out in ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;11, entitled <cite class="XRefExternal">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Vehicles with regard to Door Latches and Door Retention Components</cite>, in the version dated June 11, 2007, as amended from time to time after that date by any amendment in the 03 series of amendments.</p>
</li>

</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">

</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of paragraph&#xA0;6.3.2 of ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;11, the locking device shall be the device referred to in paragraph&#xA0;6.3.2.1(a) or (b) of that Regulation.</p>

<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In the case of a truck or multi-purpose passenger vehicle with a GVWR greater than 4&#xA0;563&#xA0;kg or a motor home, a seat that is labelled in accordance with S4.4 of TSD 207 is not considered to be a designated seating position.</p>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Occupant Protection In Frontal Impacts (Standard 208)</span>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>[SOR/2013-9, s. 5]</li>
</ul>
</div>
</h3>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Seat Belt Installation Requirements</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>208</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(1)ID0EE50DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every enclosed motorcycle shall be equipped at each designated seating position with a Type 2 manual seat belt assembly that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(1)p-(a)ID0EBC50DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;has an upper torso restraint that cannot be detached from the pelvic restraint;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(1)p-(b)ID0EBB50DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;can be adjusted by means of an emergency-locking retractor; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(1)p-(c)ID0EBA50DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cannot be detached from any anchorage point.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)ID0EG40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every passenger car and three-wheeled vehicle, and every truck and multi-purpose passenger vehicle with a GVWR of 4 536 kg or less, shall be equipped</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EEE40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at each front outboard designated seating position except the one referred to in paragraph (<em>b</em>), and at each rear designated seating position except those referred to in paragraphs (<em>c</em>) and (<em>d</em>), with a Type 2 manual seat belt assembly that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBCE40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;has an upper torso restraint that cannot be detached from the pelvic restraint,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBBE40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;can be adjusted by means of an emergency-locking retractor, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBAE40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cannot be detached from any anchorage point;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EBD40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at each front outboard designated seating position that is designed for a disabled person, with a Type 2 seat belt assembly;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(c)ID0EEC40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at each rear designated seating position that has a seat designed to be easily removed and replaced by means of equipment installed by a manufacturer for that purpose, or that is adjacent to a walkway located between the seat and the side of the vehicle and designed to allow access to more rearward seating positions, or that is an inboard designated seating position that has a seat whose back can be folded so that no part of the back extends above a horizontal plane located 250 mm above the highest seating reference point on the seat, with a Type 2 manual seat belt assembly that conforms to the requirements of paragraph (<em>a</em>) or with a Type 2 manual seat belt assembly that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(c)subp-(i)ID0EBCC40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;can be detached from the upper or lower anchorage point, but not from both, by means of a key or key-like object,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(c)subp-(ii)ID0EBBC40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;can be adjusted by means of an emergency-locking retractor, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(c)subp-(iii)ID0EBAC40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;has an upper torso restraint that cannot be detached from the pelvic restraint;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(d)ID0EDB40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at each rear designated seating position that has a seat that can be adjusted to change the direction it is facing, with a Type 2 manual seat belt assembly that conforms to the requirements of paragraph (<em>a</em>) and can function regardless of the direction the seat is adjusted to face, or with a Type 2 manual seat belt assembly that cannot be detached from any anchorage point and that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(d)subp-(i)ID0EBBB40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;has a pelvic restraint that restrains the movement of the pelvis regardless of the direction the seat is adjusted to face and is equipped with an emergency-locking retractor, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(d)subp-(ii)ID0EFAB40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a seat that can be placed in a forward-facing or rear-facing position or within &#xB1;30&#xB0; of either position, has an upper torso restraint that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(d)subp-(ii)Clause(A)ID0EBDAB40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(A)</span>
</a>&#xA0;can be detached from the pelvic restraint,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(d)subp-(ii)Clause(B)ID0EBCAB40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(B)</span>
</a>&#xA0;can be adjusted by means of an emergency-locking retractor,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(d)subp-(ii)Clause(C)ID0EBBAB40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(C)</span>
</a>&#xA0;is for use only in conjunction with the pelvic restraint, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(d)subp-(ii)Clause(D)ID0EBAAB40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(D)</span>
</a>&#xA0;can function when the seat is in any position in which it can be placed within that range; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(e)ID0EEA40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at each rear designated seating position that has a side-facing seat, and at each front inboard designated seating position,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(e)subp-(i)ID0EBCA40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;with a Type 2 manual seat belt assembly that conforms to the requirements of paragraph (<em>a</em>),</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(e)subp-(ii)ID0EEBA40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;with a Type 2 manual seat belt assembly that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(e)subp-(ii)Clause(A)ID0EBCBA40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(A)</span>
</a>&#xA0;has a pelvic restraint that can be adjusted by means of an emergency-locking retractor, an automatic-locking retractor or a manual adjusting device,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(e)subp-(ii)Clause(B)ID0EBBBA40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(B)</span>
</a>&#xA0;has an upper torso restraint that can be adjusted by means of an emergency-locking retractor or a manual adjusting device, and</p>
</li>
<li>

<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(e)subp-(ii)Clause(C)ID0EBABA40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(C)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cannot be detached from any anchorage point, or</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(e)subp-(iii)ID0EDAA40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;with a Type 1 manual seat belt assembly that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(2)p-(e)subp-(iii)Clause(A)ID0EBBAA40DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(A)</span>

<p class="Clause">

</a>&#xA0;can be detached from the upper or lower anchorage point, but not from both, by means of a key or key-like object,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(5)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBBC10DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;can be adjusted by means of an emergency-locking retractor, and</p>
</li>

</a>&#xA0;has an upper torso restraint that cannot be detached from the pelvic restraint;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>

<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>

<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(5)p-(c)subp-(i)ID0EBBB10DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;has a pelvic restraint that restrains the movement of the pelvis regardless of the direction the seat is adjusted to face and is equipped with an emergency-locking retractor, and</p>
</li>

<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a seat that can be placed in a forward-facing or rear-facing position or within &#xB1;30&#xB0; of either position, an upper torso restraint that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">

<span class="lawlabel">(A)</span>
</a>&#xA0;can be detached from the pelvic restraint,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(5)p-(c)subp-(ii)Clause(B)ID0EBCAB10DC0BA">

</a>&#xA0;can be adjusted by means of an emergency-locking retractor,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(5)p-(c)subp-(ii)Clause(C)ID0EBBAB10DC0BA">

</a>&#xA0;is for use only in conjunction with the pelvic restraint, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(5)p-(c)subp-(ii)Clause(D)ID0EBAAB10DC0BA">

</a>&#xA0;can function when the seat is in any position in which it can be placed within that range; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(5)p-(d)ID0EEA10DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at each rear designated seating position that has a side-facing seat,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(5)p-(d)subp-(i)ID0EBCA10DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;with a Type 2 manual seat belt assembly that conforms to the requirements of paragraph (<em>a</em>),</p>
</li>

<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(5)p-(d)subp-(ii)ID0EDBA10DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;with a Type 2 manual seat belt assembly that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">

</a>&#xA0;cannot be detached from the pelvic restraint or from any anchorage point, or</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>

<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(5)p-(d)subp-(iii)ID0EDAA10DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;with a Type 1 manual seat belt assembly that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(5)p-(d)subp-(iii)Clause(A)ID0EBBAA10DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(A)</span>
</a>&#xA0;can be adjusted by means of an emergency-locking retractor, an automatic-locking retractor or a manual adjusting device, and</p>
</li>
<li>

<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(5)p-(d)subp-(iii)Clause(B)ID0EBAAA10DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(B)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cannot be detached from any anchorage point.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>

</li>

<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(6)ID0EDZ0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every bus with a GVWR greater than 4 536 kg shall be equipped, at the driver&#x2019;s designated seating position,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">

<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(6)p-(a)ID0EEBZ0DC0BA">

</a>&#xA0;with a Type 2 manual seat belt assembly that</p>

</a>&#xA0;has an upper torso restraint that cannot be detached from the pelvic restraint,</p>
</li>

</a>&#xA0;cannot be detached from any anchorage point; or</p>
</li>

<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;with a Type 1 manual seat belt assembly that</p>

</a>&#xA0;can be adjusted by means of an emergency-locking retractor or an automatic-locking retractor, and</p>
</li>

<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cannot be detached from any anchorage point.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(7)ID0EEY0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every school bus with a GVWR of 4 536 kg or less shall be equipped, at the driver&#x2019;s designated seating position, with a Type 2 manual seat belt assembly that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(7)p-(a)ID0EBCY0DC0BA">

</li>

</a>&#xA0;cannot be detached from any anchorage point.</p>
</li>

<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(8)ID0EBX0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;[Reserved]</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(9)ID0EDW0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;An automatic-locking retractor that is installed in order for a seat belt assembly to conform to the requirements of paragraph (2)(<em>e</em>), (3)(<em>a</em>) or (<em>b</em>) or (5)(<em>d</em>) or subsection (6) shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(9)p-(a)ID0EBBW0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;engage the next locking position when a length of seat belt webbing between 19 mm and 77 mm has moved into the retractor, as measured from an initial position determined by extending the seat belt webbing to 75 per cent of its total length from the retractor; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(9)p-(b)ID0EBAW0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if used on a vehicle seat that has a suspension system, be attached to the suspended portion of the seat.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Seat Belt Fit</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(10)ID0EEU0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A Type 2 manual seat belt assembly shall be constructed so that when a 50th percentile adult male occupant is secured in place by the seat belt assembly, the intersection of the upper torso restraint and the pelvic restraint shall be at least 150 mm from the front vertical centreline of the occupant, measured along the centreline of the pelvic restraint, with</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(10)p-(a)ID0EBCU0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;any upper torso restraint manual adjusting device adjusted in accordance with the manufacturer&#x2019;s instructions;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(10)p-(b)ID0EBBU0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the vehicle seat adjusted to its rearmost and lowest position; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(10)p-(c)ID0EBAU0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat back adjusted to the manufacturer&#x2019;s nominal design riding position.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(11)ID0EDT0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When the vehicle seat is placed in any position, and the seat back is placed in the manufacturer&#x2019;s nominal design riding position and any adjustable seat belt anchorage is placed in the manufacturer&#x2019;s nominal design position for a 50th percentile adult male occupant, every pelvic restraint shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(11)p-(a)ID0EBBT0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at the driver&#x2019;s designated seating position, be adjustable to fit any occupant whose dimensions range from those of a 5th percentile adult female to those of a 95th percentile adult male; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(11)p-(b)ID0EBAT0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at all of the other designated seating positions, be adjustable to fit any occupant whose dimensions range from those of a 50th percentile six-year-old child to those of a 95th percentile adult male.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(12)ID0EBS0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When the vehicle seat is placed in any position, and the seat back is placed in the manufacturer&#x2019;s nominal design riding position and any adjustable seat belt anchorage is placed in the manufacturer&#x2019;s nominal design position for a 50th percentile adult male occupant, every upper torso restraint shall be adjustable to fit any occupant whose dimensions range from those of a 5th percentile adult female to those of a 95th percentile adult male.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Technical Standards Document No. 208</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(13)ID0EBQ0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(13)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck, bus and three-wheeled vehicle, and their owner&#x2019;s manuals, shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No. 208, Occupant Crash Protection</cite> (TSD 208), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(14)ID0EDP0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(14)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of this section,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(14)p-(a)ID0EBBP0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the words <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>passenger car</dfn>
</span> used in TSD 208 mean <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>passenger car and three-wheeled vehicle</dfn>
</span>; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(14)p-(b)ID0EBAP0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the word <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>dummy</dfn>
</span> used in the English version of TSD 208 means <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>anthropomorphic test device</dfn>
</span>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(15)ID0EBO0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(15)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite subsection (13), every vehicle with a front outboard designated seating position that is designed for a disabled person may, instead of conforming to the requirements of S5, S7.1, S7.2, S7.4 and S14 to S27 of TSD 208, display the following statement on one or more labels, permanently affixed in view of the occupants of the front designated seating positions, in letters of not less than six points in height: &#x201C;The [here refer to the outboard designated seating position in the front row of designated seating positions that does not conform to the requirements set out in CMVSS 208] does not conform to all of the requirements set out in CMVSS 208. / <span class="otherLang" lang="fr">La [ins&#xE9;rer ici la place assise d&#xE9;sign&#xE9;e ext&#xE9;rieure de la premire rang&#xE9;e de places assises design&#xE9;es qui n&#x2019;est pas conforme aux exigences pr&#xE9;vues par la NSVAC 208] n&#x2019;est pas conforme &#x00E0; toutes les exigences pr&#xE9;vues par la NSVAC 208</span>.&#x201D;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(16)ID0EBN0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(16)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite subsection (13), every three-wheeled vehicle shall, at the option of the manufacturer, either conform to the requirements of S5 and S14 to S27 of TSD 208 or display the following statement on one or more labels, permanently affixed in view of the occupants of the front designated seating positions, in letters of not less than six points in height: &#x201C;This vehicle does not conform to the requirements of the dynamic or static tests set out in CMVSS 208. / <span class="otherLang" lang="fr">Ce v&#xE9;hicule n&#x2019;est pas conforme aux exigences des essais dynamiques ou statiques pr&#xE9;vues par la NSVAC 208</span>.&#x201D;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(17)ID0EBM0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(17)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If a label referred to in subsection (15) or (16) is displayed in a vehicle, the English and French versions of the owner&#x2019;s manual shall include the statement contained on the label.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(18)ID0EBL0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(18)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The information contained on the label referred to in S4.5.1(a) of TSD 208 shall be in both official languages.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(19)ID0EBK0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(19)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S4.5.4 of TSD 208, a passenger car, three-wheeled vehicle, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck and bus manufactured on or after September 1, 2012 may be equipped with a device that deactivates the air bag installed at the right front outboard designated seating position in the vehicle if all of the conditions in S4.5.4.1 to S4.5.4.4 of that TSD are satisfied.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(20)ID0EBJ0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(20)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S6.4(b) of TSD 208, the compression deflection of the sternum relative to the spine of the upper thorax of each anthropomorphic test device shall not exceed 55 mm.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(21)ID0EBI0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(21)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The information referred to in S4.5, S7.1.1.5 and S7.4.2 of TSD 208 shall be provided in the English and French versions of the owner&#x2019;s manual.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(22)ID0EBH0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(22)</span>
</a>&#xA0;S14 of TSD 208 applies to every passenger car, and to every truck, bus and multi-purpose passenger vehicle &#x2014; other than a walk-in van &#x2014; with a GVWR of 3 856 kg or less and an unloaded vehicle weight of 2 495 kg or less.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(23)ID0EBG0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(23)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite S15.3.4 of TSD 208, the compression deflection of the sternum relative to the spine of the upper thorax of each anthropomorphic test device shall not exceed 45 mm, when the vehicle is tested in accordance with S16.1(a)(2) or S18 of TSD 208.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(24)ID0EBF0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(24)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 18]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Air Bag Warning Labels</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(25)ID0EDD0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(25)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If a vehicle is equipped with an air bag at a front outboard designated seating position, the vehicle shall have a label or labels permanently affixed to the sun visor at that designated seating position or permanently affixed in a readily visible area adjacent to the sun visor stating, in letters of not less than six points in height, in both official languages, the following warnings:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(25)p-(a)ID0EDBD0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a right front outboard designated seating position with an air bag that can be deactivated by means of a manual cut-off switch,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(25)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBBBD0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a warning not to install an infant restraint system or a rear-facing child restraint system in that designated seating position unless the air bag is deactivated, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(25)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBABD0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a warning about the safety of children around air bags; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(25)p-(b)ID0EBAD0DC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in all other cases, a warning about the safety of children around air bags.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">

</h4>

<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-208ss-(26)ID0EBB0DC0BA">

</li>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Seat Belt Assemblies (Standard&#xA0;209)</span>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>[SOR/95-536, s. 7(F);</li>
<li> SOR/2011-238, s. 4]</li>
</ul>
</div>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>209</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-209ss-(1)ID0EBK0BC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck, bus, low-speed vehicle, three-wheeled vehicle and enclosed motorcycle shall be equipped with seat belt assemblies that conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;209, Seat Belt Assemblies</cite> (TSD&#xA0;209), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-209ss-(2)ID0EBJ0BC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The pelvic restraint of a Type&#xA0;2 manual seat belt assembly that is equipped with a detachable upper torso restraint shall meet all requirements for a Type&#xA0;1 seat belt assembly set out in these Regulations.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-209ss-(3)_to_(6)ID0EBI0BC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3) to (6)</span>

<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-209ss-(8)ID0EBG0BC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of S4.1(e) of TSD&#xA0;209, the first sentence of the section shall be read without reference to the words &#x201C;readily accessible to the occupant to permit his easy and rapid removal from the assembly&#x201D;.</p>

<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-209ss-(9)ID0EBF0BC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Sections S4.1(g) and (m), S4.5(b) and S4.6 of TSD&#xA0;209 do not apply.</p>

<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-209ss-(10)ID0EBE0BC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The instructions referred to in S4.1(l) of TSD&#xA0;209 shall be provided in the English and French versions of the owner&#x2019;s manual.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-209ss-(11)ID0EBD0BC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The requirements relating to non-locking retractors provided in S4.1(l), S4.3(h) and S5.2(h) and (k) of TSD 209 do not apply.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-209ss-(12)ID0EBC0BC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A Type&#xA0;1 or Type&#xA0;2 seat belt assembly that includes a load-limiter and that does not meet the elongation requirements of S4.2(c), S4.4(a)(2) or S4.4(b)(4) or (5) of TSD&#xA0;209 may be installed only at a front outboard seating position that is equipped with a frontal air bag.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-209ss-(13)ID0EBB0BC0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(13)</span>
</a>&#xA0;This section expires on January&#xA0;31, 2016.</p>
</li>
</ul>
