<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Seat Belt Anchorages (Standard&#xA0;210)</span>
</h3>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">General</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>210</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(1)ID0EDP05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The following seat belt anchorages shall be installed in a designated seating position in respect of which a seat belt assembly has been installed under section&#xA0;208:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(1)p-(a)ID0EBBP05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if a Type 1 seat belt assembly has been installed, seat belt anchorages for a pelvic restraint; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(1)p-(b)ID0EBAP05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if a Type 2 seat belt assembly has been installed, seat belt anchorages for a combination pelvic and upper torso restraint.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(2)ID0EBO05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Only the strength test requirements set out in subsections&#xA0;(7) to (10) apply to enclosed motorcycles.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(2.1)ID0EBN05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2008-72, s. 7]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Anchorage Positioning Requirements</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(3)ID0EBL05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A seat belt anchorage for the pelvic portion of a seat belt assembly shall be located at least 165&#xA0;mm laterally from the other seat belt anchorage of that seat belt, as measured between the vertical centrelines of the bolt holes or, in designs using another means of attachment to the vehicle structure, the centroids of such means.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(4)ID0EEK05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In the case of a seat belt assembly in which</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EFCK05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat belt passes outside the seat or between the seat cushions without bearing on the seat structure, as illustrated in Figure&#xA0;1 of SAE Recommended Practice J383 (June 1995), a line from</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(4)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBDCK05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a seat that has no travel, the seating reference point,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(4)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBCCK05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a seat with a travel of not more than 70&#xA0;mm, where the travel is intended for use by an occupant, the H-point with the seat in its rearmost position within that range of travel, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(4)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBBCK05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a seat with a travel of more than 70&#xA0;mm, a point 64&#xA0;mm to the fore of, and 10&#xA0;mm above, the seating reference point</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="ContinuedParagraph">to the nearest contact point of the belt with the seat belt anchorage shall extend to the fore from that contact point at an angle to the horizontal of not less than 30&#xB0; and not more than 75&#xB0;;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EDBK05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat belt bears on the seat structure, as illustrated in Figure&#xA0;3 of SAE Recommended Practice J383 (June 1995),</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(4)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBBK05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat belt anchorage shall be aft of the rearmost contact point of the belt on the seat frame with the seat in its rearmost position, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(4)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBABK05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the line from the seating reference point to the nearest contact point of the seat belt with the seat frame shall extend to the fore from that contact point at an angle to the horizontal of not less than 30&#xB0; and not more than 75&#xB0;; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(4)p-(c)ID0EBAK05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat belt anchorage is on the seat structure, the line from the seating reference point to the nearest contact point of the belt with the anchorage shall extend to the fore from that contact point at an angle to the horizontal of not less than 30&#xB0; and not more than 75&#xB0;.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(5)ID0EDJ05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In the case of each non-adjustable seat belt anchorage for the upper end of an upper torso restraint, the intersection of the longitudinal centreline of the bolt hole and the surface of the mounting structure or, in designs using another means of attachment to the vehicle structure, the centroid of the means shall be located within the range indicated in section&#xA0;6.1 of SAE Recommended Practice J383, <cite class="XRefExternal">Motor Vehicle Seat Belt Anchorages &#x2014; Design Recommendations</cite> (June 1995), with reference to an H-point template described in section&#xA0;4.1 of SAE Standard J826, <cite class="XRefExternal">Devices for Use in Defining and Measuring Vehicle Seating Accommodation</cite> (July 1995), where</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(5)p-(a)ID0EBBJ05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the H-Point of the template is located at the unique Design H-Point of the seat, as defined in section&#xA0;3.11.1 of SAE Recommended Practice J1100, <cite class="XRefExternal">Motor Vehicle Dimensions</cite> (February 2001), at the full rearward and full downward position of the seat; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(5)p-(b)ID0EBAJ05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the torso line of the template is at the same angle to the vertical plane as the seat back with the seat adjusted to its full rearward and full downward position and the seat back in its most upright position.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(6)ID0EBI05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In the case of each adjustable seat belt anchorage for the upper end of an upper torso restraint, the mid-point of the range of adjustment of the anchorage or the position that is suitable for a 50th&#xA0;percentile adult male, if that position is specified in the owner&#x2019;s manual, shall be located within the range referred to in subsection&#xA0;(5).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Strength Requirements</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(7)ID0EBG05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When the seat belt anchorages for a Type&#xA0;1 seat belt assembly or for the pelvic portion of a Type&#xA0;2 seat belt assembly that is equipped with a detachable upper torso restraint are tested for strength in accordance with <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 210 &#x2014; Seat Belt Anchorages</cite> (January 2010) by applying a force of 22&#xA0;241&#xA0;N, none of the seat belt anchorages shall separate completely from the vehicle structure or seat structure.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(8)ID0EBF05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When the seat belt anchorages for the pelvic portion and for the upper torso portion of a Type&#xA0;2 seat belt assembly are tested for strength in accordance with <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 210 &#x2014; Seat Belt Anchorages</cite> (January 2010) by simultaneously applying a force of 13&#xA0;345&#xA0;N, none of the seat belt anchorages shall separate completely from the vehicle structure or seat structure.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(9)ID0EBE05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2003-57, s. 1]</span>
</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(10)ID0EDD05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Seat belt anchorages for designated seating positions that face in the same direction shall be tested by simultaneously loading the seat belt assemblies attached to the anchorages, where the anchorages are</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(10)p-(a)ID0EBBD05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;common to the same seat; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(10)p-(b)ID0EBAD05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;laterally adjacent but not common to the same seat and at least one of the anchorages is located within 305&#xA0;mm of the anchorage for the adjacent seating position, as measured between the vertical centrelines of the bolt holes or, in designs using another means of attachment to the vehicle structure, the centroids of those means.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Information Respecting Restraint Systems</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210ss-(11)ID0EBB05B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The English and French versions of the owner&#x2019;s manual for a three-wheeled vehicle, passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, bus or truck with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less and rear designated seating positions, other than a school bus, shall contain a statement indicating that children and infants are safer when properly restrained in a child restraint system or infant restraint system secured in a rear seating position.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/90-588, s. 3;</li>
<li> SOR/93-5, s. 5;</li>
<li> SOR/97-447, s. 7;</li>
<li> SOR/2003-57, ss. 1, 3(F), 4(F);</li>
<li> SOR/2003-272, s. 25;</li>
<li> SOR/2006-94, s. 4(E);</li>
<li> SOR/2007-180, s. 14;</li>
<li> SOR/2008-72, s. 7;</li>
<li> SOR/2011-264, s. 6.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">User-ready Tether Anchorages for Restraint Systems and Booster Seats (Standard&#xA0;210.1)</span>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>[SOR/2013-117, s. 7]</li>
</ul>
</div>
</h3>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Application</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>210.1</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(1)ID0EGV02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(2), this section applies to every</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(1)p-(a)ID0EBEV02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;passenger car;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(1)p-(b)ID0EBDV02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;three-wheeled vehicle;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(1)p-(c)ID0EBCV02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;multi-purpose passenger vehicle and truck with a GVWR of 3&#xA0;856&#xA0;kg or less and an unloaded vehicle weight of 2&#xA0;495&#xA0;kg or less;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(1)p-(d)ID0EBBV02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;school bus; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(1)p-(e)ID0EBAV02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;bus, other than a school bus, with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(2)ID0EDU02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;This section does not apply to</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EBBU02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a designated seating position at which a built-in restraint system is provided that is not part of a removable vehicle seat; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EBAU02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a hearse.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">General</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3)ID0EKS02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsections (3.2) and (3.3), a user-ready tether anchorage shall be installed in a vehicle, other than a convertible or an open-body type vehicle,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBIS02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a vehicle, other than a school bus, that has only one row of forward-facing designated seating positions, at all forward-facing designated seating positions other than that of the driver;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBHS02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a vehicle, other than a school bus, that has two or more rows of designated seating positions, and not more than three forward-facing designated seating positions located to the rear of the first row of designated seating positions, at all forward-facing designated seating positions located to the rear of the first row of designated seating positions;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3)p-(c)ID0EBGS02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a vehicle, other than a school bus, that has two or more rows of designated seating positions, and four or more forward-facing designated seating positions located to the rear of the first row of designated seating positions, at three forward-facing designated seating positions located to the rear of the first row of designated seating positions, with at least one user-ready tether anchorage being installed at a forward-facing designated seating position in the second row of designated seating positions, and at least one user-ready tether anchorage being installed at a forward-facing inboard designated seating position, if such a designated seating position exists;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3)p-(d)ID0EBFS02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a school bus that has not more than 24&#xA0;passenger designated seating positions, and only one forward-facing designated seating position other than that of the driver and those of a bench seat that is next to an emergency exit and contains an adjacent seat, at that forward-facing designated seating position;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3)p-(e)ID0EBES02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a school bus that has not more than 24&#xA0;passenger designated seating positions, and two or more forward-facing designated seating positions other than that of the driver and those of a bench seat that is next to an emergency exit and contains an adjacent seat, at two of those forward-facing designated seating positions;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3)p-(f)ID0EBDS02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a school bus that has 25 or more, but not more than 65, passenger designated seating positions, and not more than three forward-facing designated seating positions other than that of the driver and those of a bench seat that is next to an emergency exit and contains an adjacent seat, at all of those forward-facing designated seating positions;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3)p-(g)ID0EBCS02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(g)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a school bus that has 25 or more, but not more than 65, passenger designated seating positions, and four or more forward-facing designated seating positions other than that of the driver and those of a bench seat that is next to an emergency exit and contains an adjacent seat, at four of those forward-facing designated seating positions;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3)p-(h)ID0EBBS02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(h)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a school bus that has 66 or more passenger designated seating positions, and not more than seven forward-facing designated seating positions other than that of the driver and those of a bench seat that is next to an emergency exit and contains an adjacent seat, at all of those forward-facing designated seating positions; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3)p-(i)ID0EBAS02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a school bus that has 66 or more passenger designated seating positions, and eight or more forward-facing designated seating positions other than that of the driver and those of a bench seat that is next to an emergency exit and contains an adjacent seat, at eight of those forward-facing designated seating positions.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3.1)ID0EBR02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A user-ready tether anchorage shall be available for use at all times, except when the designated seating position at which it is installed is not available for use because the vehicle seat has been removed or converted to an alternate use, such as the carrying of cargo.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3.2)ID0EBQ02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3.2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If a lower universal anchorage system is installed at a passenger designated seating position in the first row of designated seating positions in accordance with subsection&#xA0;210.2(8), one user-ready tether anchorage shall be installed at that designated seating position.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3.3)ID0EBP02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3.3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The number of user-ready tether anchorages required under paragraphs&#xA0;(3)(<em>b</em>) and (<em>c</em>) may be reduced by one if a user-ready tether anchorage is installed in the first row of designated seatings positions in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(3.2).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(3.4)ID0EBO02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3.4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2013-117, s. 8]</span>
</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(4)ID0EBN02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The portion of a user-ready tether anchorage that is designed to bind with the tether strap hook shall be readily accessible and, if under a cover, the cover shall be identified by one of the symbols or the mirror image of one of the symbols set out in Figure&#xA0;2 and shall be removable without the use of tools.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Tether Anchorage Positioning</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(5)ID0EEL02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsections&#xA0;(5.1) and (7), the portion of each user-ready tether anchorage that is designed to bind with a tether strap hook shall be located within the shaded zone, as shown in Figures 3 to 7, of the designated seating position for which it is installed, with reference to the H-point of a template described in section&#xA0;4.1 of SAE Standard J826, <cite class="XRefExternal">Devices for Use in Defining and Measuring Vehicle Seating Accommodation</cite> (July 1995), if</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(5)p-(a)ID0EDCL02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the H-Point of the template is located</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(5)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBBCL02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at the unique Design H-Point of the designated seating position, as defined in section&#xA0;3.11.1 of SAE Recommended Practice J1100, <cite class="XRefExternal">Motor Vehicle Dimensions</cite> (February 2001), at the full downward and full rearward position of the seat, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(5)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBACL02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a designated seating position that is equipped with a lower universal anchorage system, midway between the two lower universal anchorage system bars;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(5)p-(b)ID0EBBL02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the torso line of the template is at the same angle to the vertical plane as the vehicle seat back with the seat adjusted to its full rearward and full downward position and the seat back in its most upright position; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(5)p-(c)ID0EBAL02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the template is positioned in the vertical longitudinal plane that contains the H-point of the template.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(5.1)ID0EBK02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In the case of a bus, no portion of the user-ready tether anchorage shall be located on the bus floor.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(6)ID0EBJ02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2008-72, s. 8]</span>
</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(7)ID0EEI02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The portion of a user-ready tether anchorage in a vehicle that is designed to bind with the tether strap hook may be located outside the shaded zone referred to in subsection&#xA0;(5), if no part of the shaded zone is accessible without removing a seating component of the vehicle and the vehicle is equipped with a routing device that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(7)p-(a)ID0EBCI02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;ensures that the tether strap functions as if the portion of the anchorage designed to bind with the tether strap hook were located within the shaded zone;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(7)p-(b)ID0EBBI02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;is at least 65&#xA0;mm behind the torso line, in the case of a non-rigid-webbing-type routing device or a deployable routing device, or at least 100&#xA0;mm behind the torso line, in the case of a fixed rigid routing device; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(7)p-(c)ID0EBAI02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;when tested after being installed as it is intended to be used, is of sufficient strength to withstand, with the user-ready tether anchorage, the force referred to in subsection&#xA0;(8).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Strength Requirements</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(8)ID0EFG02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(10), every user-ready tether anchorage in a row of designated seating positions shall, when tested, withstand the application of a force of 10&#xA0;000&#xA0;N</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(8)p-(a)ID0EDDG02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;applied by means of one of the following types of test devices, installed as a child restraint system would be in accordance with the vehicle manufacturer&#x2019;s installation instructions, namely,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(8)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBBDG02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a test device shown in Figures&#xA0;12 to 16, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(8)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBADG02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a test device shown in Figures&#xA0;7 and 8 of section&#xA0;210.2, in the case of a designated seating position having a lower universal anchorage system;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(8)p-(b)ID0EDCG02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;applied</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(8)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBCG02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in a forward direction parallel to the vehicle&#x2019;s vertical longitudinal plane through the X&#xA0;point on the test device, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(8)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBACG02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;initially, along a line above the horizontal line, at an angle of 10&#xB0; &#xB1; 5&#xB0; to it.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(8)p-(c)ID0EBBG02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;attained within 30&#xA0;seconds, at any onset force rate of not more than 135&#xA0;000&#xA0;N/s; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(8)p-(d)ID0EBAG02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;maintained at a 10&#xA0;000-N level for a minimum of one second.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(9)ID0EBF02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2008-72, s. 8]</span>
</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(10)ID0EBE02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If the zones in which user-ready tether anchorages are located overlap and if, in the overlap area, a user-ready tether anchorage is installed that is designed to accept the tether strap hooks of two restraint systems or booster seats simultaneously, each portion of the user-ready tether anchorage that is designed to bind with a tether strap hook shall withstand the force referred to in subsection&#xA0;(8) when it is applied to both portions simultaneously.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(11)ID0EBD02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If a bench seat in a bus or a row of designated seating positions in another vehicle has more than one user-ready tether anchorage and a distance of 400&#xA0;mm or more, measured in accordance with Figure&#xA0;20, separates the midpoints of adjacent designated seating positions, the force referred to in subsection&#xA0;(8) or (10), as the case may be, shall be applied simultaneously to each user-ready tether anchorage in the manner specified in that subsection.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-(12)ID0EBC02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The strength requirement tests shall be conducted with the vehicle seat adjusted to its full rearward and full downward position and the seat back in its most upright position.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-ID0ERB02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">
</span>
</a>&#xA0;</p>

</p>

<h6>
<span class="HTitleText5">Notes</span>
</h6>
<figure>
<ul class="noBullet">
<li>
<div class="listItemBlock0">
<div class="listItemLabel">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.1ss-TableGrouptabletgrouptbodyrowentryProvisionListItem1ID0EBDAAAAAAAGB02B0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">1</span>
</a>&#xA0;</div>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Lower Universal Anchorage Systems for Restraint Systems and Booster Seats (Standard&#xA0;210.2)</span>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>[SOR/2013-117, s. 9]</li>
</ul>
</div>
</h3>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Application</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>210.2</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(1)ID0EG40YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(2), this section applies to every</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(1)p-(a)ID0EBE40YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;passenger car;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(1)p-(a.1)ID0EBD40YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;three-wheeled vehicle;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(1)p-(b)ID0EBC40YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;multi-purpose passenger vehicle and truck with a GVWR of 3&#xA0;856&#xA0;kg or less and an unloaded vehicle weight of 2&#xA0;495&#xA0;kg or less;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(1)p-(c)ID0EBB40YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;bus, other than a school bus, with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(1)p-(d)ID0EBA40YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;school bus.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(2)ID0EF30YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;This section does not apply to</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EBD30YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a walk-in van;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EBC30YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a bus that has only one row of forward-facing designated seating positions rearward of the driver&#x2019;s seat;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(2)p-(c)ID0EEB30YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a vehicle that is not equipped with a manual cut-off switch to deactivate the frontal air bag installed at the right front outboard designated seating position when any restraint system or booster seat is installed, and that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(2)p-(c)subp-(i)ID0EBCB30YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;has only one row of forward-facing designated seating positions,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(2)p-(c)subp-(ii)ID0EBBB30YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cannot accommodate, because of the location of transmission or suspension components, the installation of the bars of a lower universal anchorage system to permit the attachment to them of a child restraint fixture as shown in Figure&#xA0;1 in a seating position located to the rear of the first row of seating positions, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(2)p-(c)subp-(iii)ID0EBAB30YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;has no seating position located to the rear of the first row of seating positions that is able to accommodate a child restraint fixture shown in Figures&#xA0;2 to 4; or</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(2)p-(d)ID0EBA30YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a hearse.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">General</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(3)ID0EH10YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A lower universal anchorage system consists of two straight horizontal bars that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBF10YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;are transverse to the longitudinal axis of the vehicle;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBE10YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;have a diameter of 6&#xA0;mm &#xB1; 0.1&#xA0;mm and a length, measured in accordance with Figure&#xA0;12, of not less than 25&#xA0;mm;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(3)p-(c)ID0EBD10YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;are parallel, with collinear centroidal longitudinal axes, and are spaced laterally so that they permit the lower connectors on a child restraint fixture, shown in Figures&#xA0;2 to 4, to be attached to them over the entire length of the lower connectors;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(3)p-(d)ID0EBC10YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;are an integral and permanent part of a vehicle seat or seat anchorage or the structure of the vehicle such that they can be removed only with the use of tools;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(3)p-(e)ID0EBB10YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;are rigidly attached to a vehicle seat or seat anchorage or the structure of the vehicle so that they will not deform more than 5&#xA0;mm when subjected to a force of 100&#xA0;N in any direction with the vehicle seat adjusted in the vehicle to its full rearward and full downward position and the seat back adjusted in the nominal design riding position; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(3)p-(f)ID0EBA10YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;permit a checking device to be attached to them over the entire width of the checking device, with a gap of less than 1&#xA0;mm between the surface of the bars and line M, shown in Figure&#xA0;5.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(4)ID0EKZ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsections&#xA0;(7) and (8), a lower universal anchorage system shall be installed in a vehicle</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EBIZ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a vehicle, other than a school bus, that has only one row of forward-facing designated seating positions, at one forward-facing designated seating position other than that of the driver;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EBHZ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a vehicle, other than a school bus, that has two or more rows of designated seating positions, and not more than two forward-facing designated seating positions located to the rear of the first row of designated seating positions, at all forward-facing designated seating positions located to the rear of the first row of designated seating positions;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(4)p-(c)ID0EBGZ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a vehicle, other than a school bus, that has two or more rows of designated seating positions, and three or more forward-facing designated seating positions located to the rear of the first row of designated seating positions, at two forward-facing designated seating positions located to the rear of the first row of designated seating positions, with at least one lower universal anchorage system being installed at a forward-facing designated seating position in the second row of designated seating positions;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(4)p-(d)ID0EBFZ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a school bus that has not more than 24&#xA0;passenger designated seating positions, and only one forward-facing designated seating position other than that of the driver and those of a bench seat that is next to an emergency exit and contains an adjacent seat, at that forward-facing designated seating position;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(4)p-(e)ID0EBEZ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a school bus that has not more than 24&#xA0;passenger designated seating positions, and two or more forward-facing designated seating positions other than that of the driver and those of a bench seat that is next to an emergency exit and contains an adjacent seat, at two of those forward-facing designated seating positions;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(4)p-(f)ID0EBDZ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a school bus that has 25 or more, but not more than 65, passenger designated seating positions, and not more than three forward-facing designated seating positions other than that of the driver and those of a bench seat that is next to an emergency exit and contains an adjacent seat, at all of those forward-facing designated seating positions;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(4)p-(g)ID0EBCZ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(g)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a school bus that has 25 or more, but not more than 65, passenger designated seating positions, and four or more forward-facing designated seating positions other than that of the driver and those of a bench seat that is next to an emergency exit and contains an adjacent seat, at four of those forward-facing designated seating positions;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(4)p-(h)ID0EBBZ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(h)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a school bus that has 66 or more passenger designated seating positions, and not more than seven forward-facing designated seating positions other than that of the driver and those of a bench seat that is next to an emergency exit and contains an adjacent seat, at all of those forward-facing designated seating positions; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(4)p-(i)ID0EBAZ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a school bus that has 66 or more passenger designated seating positions, and eight or more forward-facing designated seating positions other than that of the driver and those of a bench seat that is next to an emergency exit and contains an adjacent seat, at eight of those forward-facing designated seating positions.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(5)ID0EBY0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2008-72, s. 9]</span>
</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(6)ID0EBX0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A lower universal anchorage system shall be installed only at a designated seating position that is equipped with a user-ready tether anchorage, except in the case of a convertible or an open-body type vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(7)ID0EBW0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The number of lower universal anchorage systems required in a vehicle under subsection&#xA0;(4) may be reduced by the number of built-in restraint systems installed in the vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(8)ID0EBV0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Except in the case of a bus, if the distance between the rearward surface of the front seat back of the vehicle and the forward surface of the rear seat back of the vehicle is less than 720&#xA0;mm, as measured in accordance with Figure&#xA0;6, and if the vehicle is equipped with the manual cut-off switch referred to in paragraph&#xA0;(2)(<em>c</em>), a lower universal anchorage system may be installed at a passenger designated seating position in the first row of designated seating positions instead of at a designated seating position located to the rear of the first row of designated seating positions.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(9)ID0EBU0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A vehicle that is equipped with a seat that slides sideways or that can be installed in any other seating position in the vehicle shall meet the requirements of this section with the seat adjusted in any adjustment position.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(10)ID0EBT0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2008-72, s. 9]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Lower Universal Anchorage System Positioning</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(11)ID0EBR0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Each bar of the lower universal anchorage system shall be installed so that a child restraint fixture can be attached to the system as shown in Figure&#xA0;1.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(12)ID0EBQ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of subsection&#xA0;(11), the vehicle seat shall be adjusted to its full rearward and full downward position, with the seat back in the nominal design riding position and the child restraint fixture shown in Figures&#xA0;2 and 3 or in Figure&#xA0;4 installed in the seat.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Strength Requirements</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(13)ID0EDO0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(13)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A lower universal anchorage system installed in a row of designated seating positions shall not separate completely from the vehicle seat or seat anchorage or the structure of the vehicle when tested</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(13)p-(a)ID0EGBO0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;subject to subsection&#xA0;(15), by pulling with a force of 15&#xA0;000&#xA0;N, which force is</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(13)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBEBO0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;applied by means of a test device shown in Figures&#xA0;7 and 8 that is installed using both the associated user-ready tether anchorage and the lower universal anchorage system as a child restraint system would be installed in accordance with the vehicle manufacturer&#x2019;s instructions,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(13)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBDBO0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;applied in a forward direction parallel to the vehicle&#x2019;s vertical longitudinal plane through the X point on the test device, starting with a pre-load force of 500&#xA0;N,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(13)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBCBO0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;applied initially, along a line above the horizontal line, at an angle of 10&#xB0; &#xB1; 5&#xB0; to it,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(13)p-(a)subp-(iv)ID0EBBBO0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iv)</span>
</a>&#xA0;attained within 30&#xA0;seconds, at any onset force rate of not more than 135&#xA0;000&#xA0;N/s, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(13)p-(a)subp-(v)ID0EBABO0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(v)</span>
</a>&#xA0;maintained at a level of 15&#xA0;000&#xA0;N for a minimum of one second; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(13)p-(b)ID0EGAO0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;by pulling with a force of 5&#xA0;000&#xA0;N, which force is</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(13)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBEAO0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;applied by means of a test device shown in Figures&#xA0;7 and 8 that is installed as a child restraint system would be installed in accordance with the vehicle manufacturer&#x2019;s instructions using both the user ready tether anchorage and the lower universal anchorage system or, at the manufacturer&#x2019;s option, using only the lower universal anchorage system,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(13)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBDAO0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;applied along a vertical longitudinal plane that is at an angle of 75 &#xB1; 5 to either side of a vertical longitudinal plane that is parallel to the vehicle&#x2019;s longitudinal centre line, through the X point on the test device, starting with a pre-load force of 500&#xA0;N,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(13)p-(b)subp-(iii)ID0EBCAO0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;applied initially, along a horizontal line or along any line below or above that line that is at an angle to that line of not more than 5&#xB0;,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(13)p-(b)subp-(iv)ID0EBBAO0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iv)</span>
</a>&#xA0;attained within 30&#xA0;seconds, at any onset force rate of not more than 135&#xA0;000&#xA0;N/s, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(13)p-(b)subp-(v)ID0EBAAO0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(v)</span>
</a>&#xA0;maintained at a level of 5&#xA0;000&#xA0;N for a minimum of 1&#xA0;second.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(14)ID0EBN0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(14)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When a force of 5&#xA0;000&#xA0;N is applied in accordance with paragraph&#xA0;(13)(<em>b</em>), the lower universal anchorage system shall not permit the X point on the test device to be displaced in the direction of the applied force by more than 125&#xA0;mm if the test device is installed in an outboard designated seating position or by more than 150&#xA0;mm if the test device is installed in an inboard designated seating position.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(15)ID0EGM0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(15)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A lower universal anchorage system installed in a designated seating position that is not equipped with an associated user-ready tether anchorage shall be tested by the application of a force of 11&#xA0;000&#xA0;N that is</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(15)p-(a)ID0EBEM0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;applied by means of a test device shown in Figures&#xA0;7 and 8 that is installed using only the lower universal anchorage system;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(15)p-(b)ID0EBDM0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;applied in a forward direction parallel to the vehicle&#x2019;s vertical longitudinal plane through the X&#xA0;point on the test device, starting with a pre-load force of 500&#xA0;N;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(15)p-(c)ID0EBCM0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;applied initially, along a line above the horizontal line, at an angle of 10&#xB0; &#xB1; 5&#xB0; to it;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(15)p-(d)ID0EBBM0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;attained within 30&#xA0;seconds, at any onset force rate of not more than 135&#xA0;000&#xA0;N/s; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(15)p-(e)ID0EBAM0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;maintained at a level of 11&#xA0;000&#xA0;N for a minimum of one second.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Test Requirements</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(16)ID0EBK0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(16)</span>
</a>&#xA0;If a bench seat in a bus or a row of designated seating positions in another vehicle has more than one lower universal anchorage system and a distance of 400&#xA0;mm or more, measured in accordance with Figure&#xA0;9, separates the midpoints of any adjacent designated seating positions, the force referred to in subsection&#xA0;(13) or (15) shall be applied simultaneously to each anchorage system in the manner specified in that subsection.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(17)ID0EGJ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(17)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The strength requirement tests shall be carried out under the following conditions:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(17)p-(a)ID0EBEJ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the vehicle seat is installed in the vehicle;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(17)p-(b)ID0EBDJ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the vehicle seat is adjusted to its full rearward and full downward position;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(17)p-(c)ID0EBCJ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the vehicle seat back is adjusted in the nominal design riding position;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(17)p-(d)ID0EBBJ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the head restraints, if installed at a designated seating position that is equipped with a lower universal anchorage system, are adjusted in accordance with the manufacturer&#x2019;s instructions; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(17)p-(e)ID0EBAJ0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a rearward force of 135&#xA0;N &#xB1; 15&#xA0;N is applied to the centre of the lower front crossbar of the test device shown in Figures&#xA0;7 and 8 to press the test device against the seat back as the position of the lower connectors of the test device is adjusted to remove slack or tension.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(17.1)ID0EEI0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(17.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite subsection&#xA0;(17), in the case of a bus, the strength requirement tests may be carried out when the vehicle seat is not installed in the vehicle if</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(17.1)p-(a)ID0EBCI0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the user-ready tether anchorage is installed on the vehicle seat in accordance with the tether anchorage positioning requirements of section&#xA0;210.1 for a designated seating position of the vehicle;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(17.1)p-(b)ID0EBBI0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the structure on which the seat is installed, the seat anchorage and all associated hardware are equivalent to those used when the vehicle seat is installed in the vehicle; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(17.1)p-(c)ID0EBAI0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a rearward force of 135&#xA0;N &#xB1; 15&#xA0;N is applied to the centre of the lower front crossbar of the test device shown in Figures&#xA0;7 and 8 to press the test device against the seat back as the position of the lower connectors of the test device is adjusted to remove slack or tension.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Information Respecting Lower Universal Anchorage Systems</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(18)ID0EGG0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(18)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsections&#xA0;(19) and (20), if a lower universal anchorage system is not visible along a line making an upward angle of at least 30&#xB0; with the horizontal plane without compression of the seat cushion or seat back of the seating position, the presence of each bar of the system shall be indicated by the symbol shown in Figure&#xA0;10, consisting of a circle containing a pictogram, which symbol shall meet the following conditions:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(18)p-(a)ID0EBEG0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the pictogram shall contrast with the background of the circle;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(18)p-(b)ID0EBDG0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the circle shall contrast with its background, namely, the seat back or seat cushion of the vehicle;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(18)p-(c)ID0EBCG0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;its centre shall be located no more than 25&#xA0;mm from the vertical longitudinal plane that passes through the centre of each bar of the system;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(18)p-(d)ID0EBBG0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;it shall be marked on the seat back or on the seat cushion of the vehicle in accordance with Figure&#xA0;11; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(18)p-(e)ID0EBAG0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;it shall be permanently marked by any means in a manner that makes it impossible to remove without defacing or destruction.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(19)ID0EBF0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(19)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In the case of a foldable lower universal anchorage system, its presence shall be indicated by the symbol shown in Figure&#xA0;10 marked in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(18) or marked on the mechanism for deploying each bar of the foldable system and visible at the junction of the seat back and the seat cushion when the system is in the folded position.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(20)ID0EDE0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(20)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In the case of a lower universal anchorage system hidden by one or more covers, its presence may be indicated by the symbol shown in Figure&#xA0;10 marked on each cover in the following cases:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(20)p-(a)ID0EBBE0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the covers are not entirely removable; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(20)p-(b)ID0EBAE0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the system is visible in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(18) if the covers are entirely removed.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(21)ID0EBD0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(21)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2008-72, s. 9]</span>
</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(22)ID0EIC0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(22)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The English and French versions of the owner&#x2019;s manual for a vehicle that is equipped with a lower universal anchorage system shall contain the following information:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(22)p-(a)ID0EBGC0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if the symbol shown in Figure&#xA0;10 is marked on a seat back, seat cushion or cover over the lower universal anchorage system, an explanation that the symbol indicates the presence of a lower universal anchorage system, and a reproduction of the symbol;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(22)p-(b)ID0EBFC0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2008-72, s.&#xA0;9]</span>
</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(22)p-(c)ID0EBEC0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an identification, by means of the symbol shown in Figure&#xA0;10 or any other mark used to indicate the presence of a lower universal anchorage system, as applicable, of the designated seating positions that are equipped with a lower universal anchorage system;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(22)p-(d)ID0EBDC0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if the vehicle is equipped with a foldable system, instructions on how to deploy the system;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(22)p-(e)ID0EBCC0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if the vehicle is equipped with head restraints at the seating positions equipped with a lower universal anchorage system, instructions on the correct manner of adjusting the head restraints for use with user-ready tether anchorages;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(22)p-(f)ID0EBBC0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if the vehicle has more than one row of designated seating positions, a statement that children and infants are safer when properly restrained in a child restraint system or infant restraint system secured in a rear seating position; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-210.2ss-(22)p-(g)ID0EBAC0YB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(g)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if the vehicle is a convertible or an open-body type vehicle that has no designated seating position equipped with a user-ready tether anchorage, a statement that neither a restraint system nor a booster seat requiring the use of a tether strap can be properly secured to the vehicle.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>

</h6>
<figure>
<ul class="noBullet">
<li>

<span class="lawlabel">1</span>
</a>&#xA0;</div>
<div class="listItemText2">Adjustable seats are in the adjustment position midway between the forwardmost and rearmost positions and, if separately adjustable in a vertical direction, are at the lowest position. If an adjustment position does not exist midway between the forwardmost and rearmost positions, the closest adjustment position to the rear of the midpoint is used.</div>
</div>
</li>
<li>
<div class="listItemBlock0">
<div class="listItemLabel">

<span class="lawlabel">2</span>
</a>&#xA0;</div>
<div class="listItemText2">Place adjustable seat backs in the nominal design riding position as recommended by the manufacturer, in the manner specified by the manufacturer. Place adjustable anchorages in the nominal design riding position recommended by the manufacturer for a 50th&#xA0;percentile adult male occupant. Place each adjustable head restraint in its highest adjustment position. Adjustable lumbar supports are positioned so that the lumbar support is in its least firm adjustment position.</div>
</div>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="listItemBlock0">

</a>&#xA0;</div>

</li>
