<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Windshield Mounting</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>212</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-212ss-(1)ID0EBD0VB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every passenger car, other than a forward control configuration vehicle or an open-body type vehicle with a fold-down or removable windshield, shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No. 212, Windshield Mounting</cite> (TSD 212), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-212ss-(2)ID0EBC0VB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every truck, bus and multi-purpose passenger vehicle with a GVWR of 4 536 kg or less, other than a walk-in van, a forward control configuration vehicle or an open-body type vehicle with a fold-down or removable windshield, shall conform to the requirements of TSD 212, as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-212ss-(3)ID0EBB0VB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 19]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/80-282, s. 3;</li>
<li> SOR/82-274, s. 1;</li>
<li> SOR/90-387, s. 2(F);</li>
<li> SOR/93-5, s. 6;</li>
<li> SOR/94-692, s. 2(F);</li>
<li> SOR/95-536, s. 7(F);</li>
<li> SOR/97-201, s. 5;</li>
<li> SOR/97-421, ss. 17, 22(F);</li>
<li> SOR/2003-57, s. 2;</li>
<li> SOR/2008-72, s. 10(F);</li>
<li> SOR/2009-121, s. 3;</li>
<li> SOR/2013-9, s. 7;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-307, s. 19.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Section">
<strong>213. to 213.3</strong>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/98-160, s. 3]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Built-in Restraint Systems and Built-in Booster Seats (Standard&#xA0;213.4)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>213.4</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(1)ID0EDY0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The following definitions apply in this section.</p>
<dl class="Definition">
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>Test Method&#xA0;213.4</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>Test Method&#xA0;213.4</dfn>
</span> means <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method&#xA0;213.4 &#x2014; Built-in Restraint Systems and Built-in Booster Seats</cite> (November 2012). (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">M&#xE9;thode d&#x2019;essai 213.4</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>TSD 209</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>TSD 209</dfn>
</span> means <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;209, Seat Belt Assemblies</cite>, as amended from time to time. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">DNT 209</span>) </p>
</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(2)ID0EBX0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of this section, a reference in TSD 209 to webbing, a belt buckle or a related piece of adjustment hardware that is part of a Type&#xA0;1 seat belt assembly is to be read as a reference to webbing, a belt buckle or a related piece of adjustment hardware that is part of a built-in restraint system.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(3)ID0EBW0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every built-in restraint system and built-in booster seat shall be constructed only of materials that conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;302, Flammability of Interior Materials</cite>, as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(4)ID0EEV0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every built-in restraint system shall, when the anthropomorphic test device is positioned in the restraint system in accordance with subsection&#xA0;5.4 of Test Method&#xA0;213.4,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EDCV0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;restrain the upper torso by means of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(4)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBBCV0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;belts passing over each shoulder, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(4)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBACV0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a fixed or movable surface that conforms to the requirements of subsection&#xA0;(11);</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EDBV0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;restrain the lower torso by means of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(4)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBBV0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a belt making an angle of at least&#xA0;45&#xB0; but not more than&#xA0;90&#xB0; with the seating surface of the restraint system at the belt attachment points, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(4)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBABV0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a fixed or movable surface that conforms to the requirements of subsection&#xA0;(11); and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(4)p-(c)ID0EDAV0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;restrain the crotch by means of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(4)p-(c)subp-(i)ID0EBBAV0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a crotch belt that is connectable to the belt referred to in subparagraph (<em>b</em>)(i) or to the surface referred to in subparagraph (<em>b</em>)(ii), or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(4)p-(c)subp-(ii)ID0EBAAV0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a fixed or movable surface that conforms to the requirements of subsection&#xA0;(11).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(5)ID0EBU0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every belt that is part of a built-in restraint system and that is designed to restrain a person shall be adjustable to snugly fit a person whose mass and height are within the ranges indicated in the statement required by paragraph&#xA0;(19)(<em>a</em>), when the person is positioned in the restraint system in accordance with the instructions referred to in subsection&#xA0;(21).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(6)ID0EBT0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every belt buckle and related piece of adjustment hardware that is part of a built-in restraint system shall conform to the requirements of S4.3(a)(2), except the requirement respecting the transfer of corrosion, and S4.3(b) of TSD&#xA0;209.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(7)ID0EFS0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every belt buckle that is fitted on a belt designed to restrain a person in a built-in restraint system shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(7)p-(a)ID0EDDS0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;under the conditions set out in section&#xA0;4 of Test Method&#xA0;213.4,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(7)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBBDS0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;not release when any force of less than 40&#xA0;N is applied, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(7)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBADS0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;release when a force of at least 40&#xA0;N but not more than 62&#xA0;N is applied;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(7)p-(b)ID0EBCS0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;under the conditions set out in section&#xA0;6 of Test Method&#xA0;213.4, release when a force of not more than 71&#xA0;N is applied;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(7)p-(c)ID0EBBS0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;conform to the requirements of S4.3(d)(2) of TSD&#xA0;209, except that the surface area of the push-button of a belt buckle designed for push-button application shall be at least 385&#xA0;mm<sup>2</sup>; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(7)p-(d)ID0EBAS0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;not release during the dynamic test specified in section&#xA0;5 of Test Method 213.4.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(8)ID0EHR0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Any webbing that is designed to restrain a person within a built-in restraint system shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(8)p-(a)ID0EBFR0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;when tested in accordance with S5.1(b) of TSD&#xA0;209 before being tested as set out in paragraphs (<em>b</em>) to (<em>d</em>), have a breaking strength of at least 11&#xA0;000&#xA0;N;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(8)p-(b)ID0EBER0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;when tested in accordance with S5.1(b) of TSD&#xA0;209 after being subjected to abrasion as specified in S5.1(d) of TSD&#xA0;209, have a breaking strength of at least 75% of the breaking strength determined in accordance with paragraph&#xA0;(<em>a</em>);</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(8)p-(c)ID0EBDR0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;when tested in accordance with S5.1(b) of TSD&#xA0;209 after being subjected to buckle abrasion as specified in S5.3(c) of TSD&#xA0;209, have a breaking strength of at least 75% of the breaking strength determined in accordance with paragraph&#xA0;(<em>a</em>):</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(8)p-(d)ID0EBCR0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;when tested in accordance with S5.1(b) of TSD&#xA0;209 after being subjected to light exposure as specified in S5.1(e) of TSD&#xA0;209, have a breaking strength of at least 60% of the breaking strength determined in accordance with paragraph&#xA0;(<em>a</em>);</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(8)p-(e)ID0EBBR0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;when tested in accordance with S5.1(b) of TSD&#xA0;209 after being subjected to micro-organism exposure as specified in S5.1(f) of TSD&#xA0;209, have a breaking strength of at least 85% of the breaking strength determined in accordance with paragraph&#xA0;(<em>a</em>); and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(8)p-(f)ID0EBAR0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if contactable by the torso of an anthropomorphic test device when the restraint system is tested in accordance with section&#xA0;5 of Test Method&#xA0;213.4, have a width of not less than 38&#xA0;mm when measured as specified in S5.1(a) of TSD&#xA0;209.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(9)ID0EBQ0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every built-in restraint system and built-in booster seat shall provide, for the support of a person&#x2019;s back, a continuous surface that is flat or concave and has an area of not less than 54&#xA0;800&#xA0;mm<sup>2</sup>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(10)ID0EBP0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A built-in restraint system shall not have any surface directly in front of a person, unless the surface is designed to limit the forward movement of the person.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(11)ID0EBO0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every horizontal cross-section of a surface of a built-in restraint system that is designed to limit the forward movement of a person shall be flat or concave, and every vertical longitudinal cross-section of that surface shall be flat or convex with a radius of curvature of the underlying structure of not less than 50&#xA0;mm.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(12)ID0EDN0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Any rigid structural component underlying a contactable surface of a built-in restraint system or built-in booster seat shall not have</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(12)p-(a)ID0EBBN0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a protrusion, with any padding or flexible overlay material removed, of more than 9.5&#xA0;mm; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(12)p-(b)ID0EBAN0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an exposed edge with a radius of less than 6.4&#xA0;mm.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(13)ID0EJM0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(13)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every built-in restraint system and built-in booster seat, when tested in accordance with section&#xA0;5 of Test Method 213.4, shall, in any of the positions that the restraint system, booster seat or vehicle seat can be used while the vehicle is in motion,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(13)p-(a)ID0EDHM0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;exhibit no complete separation of any load-bearing structural element and no partial separation exposing a surface with</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(13)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBBHM0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a protrusion of more than&#xA0;9.5&#xA0;mm, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(13)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBAHM0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a radius of less than&#xA0;6.4&#xA0;mm;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(13)p-(b)ID0EBGM0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;remain in the same adjustment position during the test as it was in immediately before the test began;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(13)p-(c)ID0EBFM0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;limit the movement of the head of the anthropomorphic test device toward the rear of the restraint system or booster seat by means of a continuous seat back that is an integral part of the restraint system or booster seat;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(13)p-(d)ID0EBEM0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;limit the rotation of the head of the anthropomorphic test device toward the rear of the restraint system or booster seat, in the head&#x2019;s midsagittal plane, by means of a continuous seat back that is an integral part of the restraint system or booster seat, so that the angle between the head and the torso is at no time during the test more than 45&#xB0; as compared to the angle between the head and the torso immediately before the test began;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(13)p-(e)ID0EBDM0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;except in the case of a restraint system or booster seat tested with the anthropomorphic test device specified in subpart&#xA0;O or S, part&#xA0;572, chapter&#xA0;V, Title&#xA0;49 of the <cite class="XRefExternal">Code of Federal Regulations</cite> of the United States (revised as of October&#xA0;1, 2012), limit the resultant acceleration at the location of the accelerometer mounted in the upper thorax of the anthropomorphic test device to not more than 60&#xA0;g, except for intervals of not more than 3&#xA0;ms;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(13)p-(f)ID0EBCM0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;except in the case of a restraint system or booster seat tested with the anthropomorphic test device specified in subpart&#xA0;O or S, part&#xA0;572, chapter&#xA0;V, Title&#xA0;49 of the <cite class="XRefExternal">Code of Federal Regulations</cite> of the United States (revised as of October&#xA0;1, 2012), limit the resultant acceleration of the centre of gravity of the head of the anthropomorphic test device to not more than 80&#xA0;g, except for intervals of not more than 3 ms, unless it is established that any resultant acceleration above 80&#xA0;g is caused by another part of the anthropomorphic test device striking its head;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(13)p-(g)ID0EBBM0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(g)</span>
</a>&#xA0;not allow the angle between the back support surface and seating surface of the restraint system or booster seat to be less than 45&#xB0; at the completion of the test; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(13)p-(h)ID0EBAM0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(h)</span>
</a>&#xA0;except in the case of a restraint system or booster seat tested with the anthropomorphic test device specified in subpart&#xA0;O or S, part&#xA0;572, chapter&#xA0;V, Title&#xA0;49 of the <cite class="XRefExternal">Code of Federal Regulations</cite> of the United States (revised as of October&#xA0;1, 2012), limit the distance that either knee pivot can extend in a forward longitudinal direction, at any time during and immediately after the test, to not more than 305&#xA0;mm from the pre-test position.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(14)ID0EBL0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(14)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every belt that is part of a built-in restraint system and that is designed to restrain a person in the restraint system shall not, when the restraint system is subjected to a dynamic test in accordance with section&#xA0;5 of Test Method&#xA0;213.4, impose on the anthropomorphic test device any loads that result from the mass of the restraint system or the mass of any part of the vehicle into which the restraint system is built.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(15)ID0EDK0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(15)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The continuous seat back referred to in paragraphs&#xA0;(13)(<em>c</em>) and (<em>d</em>) shall have</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(15)p-(a)ID0EDBK0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a height</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(15)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBBBK0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;of at least 500&#xA0;mm, in the case of a built-in restraint system recommended by the manufacturer for use only by persons whose mass is 18&#xA0;kg or less, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(15)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBABK0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;of at least 560&#xA0;mm, in the case of a built-in restraint system recommended by the manufacturer for use by a person whose mass is more than 18&#xA0;kg; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(15)p-(b)ID0EBAK0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a width of at least 200&#xA0;mm, measured in the horizontal plane at a height of 500&#xA0;mm in the case of a built-in restraint system described in subparagraph (<em>a</em>)(i) or at a height of 560&#xA0;mm in the case of a built-in restraint system described in subparagraph&#xA0;(<em>a</em>)(ii).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(16)ID0EDJ0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(16)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subsection (15) does not apply in the case of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(16)p-(a)ID0EBBJ0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a built-in restraint system that is designed to accommodate an anthropomorphic test device having, on either side, a target point that, when the anthropomorphic test device is positioned in the built-in restraint system in accordance with Test Method 213.4, is below a horizontal plane tangent to the top of the vehicle seat; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(16)p-(b)ID0EBAJ0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a built-in restraint system that is designed to accommodate the anthropomorphic test device specified in subpart&#xA0;N, part&#xA0;572, chapter&#xA0;V, Title&#xA0;49 of the <cite class="XRefExternal">Code of Federal Regulations</cite> of the United States (revised as of October&#xA0;1, 2012), or a larger anthropomorphic test device.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(17)ID0EBI0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(17)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of subsection&#xA0;(15), the height of the continuous seat back shall be measured, in a plane parallel to the surface of the seat back of the built-in restraint system and orthogonal to the vertical longitudinal plane passing through the longitudinal centreline of the restraint system, from the lowest point of the restraint system&#x2019;s seating surface that is contacted by the buttocks of the seated anthropomorphic test device.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(18)ID0EBH0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(18)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite paragraph&#xA0;(15)(<em>b</em>), if a built-in restraint system or built-in booster seat provides surfaces for the support of the sides of the torso, and those surfaces extend at least 100&#xA0;mm forward from the padded surface of the portion of the restraint system or booster seat provided for the support of the head of the anthropomorphic test device, the restraint system or booster seat may have a continuous seat back width of at least 150&#xA0;mm.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(19)ID0EDG0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(19)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every built-in restraint system and built-in booster seat shall have the following information stitched onto it, indelibly moulded into or onto it, or indelibly printed on a label affixed to it in a permanent manner:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(19)p-(a)ID0EDBG0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a statement that indicates</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(19)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBBBG0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in units based on the International System of Units and in imperial units, the mass and height ranges of the persons for whom the manufacturer recommends the restraint system or booster seat, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(19)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBABG0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a booster seat, that the booster seat is for use by a person whose mass is at least 18&#xA0;kg; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(19)p-(b)ID0EDAG0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a warning that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(19)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBAG0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if the manufacturer&#x2019;s instructions on the use of the restraint system or booster seat are not followed, death or serious injury may occur, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(19)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBAAG0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if the restraint system is equipped with belts for restraining the person, the belts must be snugly adjusted around the person.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(20)ID0EDF0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(20)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The information referred to in subsection&#xA0;(19) shall be</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(20)p-(a)ID0EBBF0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in both official languages and in characters of at least 10&#xA0;points; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(20)p-(b)ID0EBAF0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;fully visible when the built-in restraint system or built-in booster seat is configured for use.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(21)ID0EEE0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(21)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every built-in restraint system and built-in booster seat shall be accompanied by printed instructions, in both official languages, that set out a step-by-step procedure, including diagrams, for</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(21)p-(a)ID0EBCE0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;using the restraint system or booster seat;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(21)p-(b)ID0EBBE0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;positioning a person in the restraint system or booster seat; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(21)p-(c)ID0EBAE0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;adjusting every part of the restraint system or booster seat that is designed to restrain the person.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(22)ID0EDD0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(22)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The instructions referred to in subsection&#xA0;(21) shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(22)p-(a)ID0EBBD0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;explain the primary consequences of not following the warnings referred to in paragraph&#xA0;19(<em>b</em>) or the instructions referred to in subsection&#xA0;(21); and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(22)p-(b)ID0EBAD0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a vehicle seat that is removable from the vehicle by means of a latch mechanism and that is equipped with a built-in restraint system or built-in booster seat, state that the vehicle seat, whether occupied or not, must be securely latched to the vehicle.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(23)ID0EBC0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(23)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 20]</span>
</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-213.4ss-(24)ID0EBB0SB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(24)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Until September&#xA0;1, 2013, a built-in restraint system or built-in booster seat may conform to the requirements of this section as it read on the day before the day on which this subsection came into force.</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Side Door Strength</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>214</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(1)ID0EEH0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In this section,</p>
<dl class="Definition">
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>initial crush resistance</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>initial crush resistance</dfn>
</span> means the average force required to deform the door of a vehicle, measured over the initial 152&#xA0;mm of crush; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">r&#xE9;sistance initiale &#x00E0; la d&#xE9;formation</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>intermediate crush resistance</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>intermediate crush resistance</dfn>
</span> means the average force required to deform the door of a vehicle, measured over the initial 305&#xA0;mm of crush; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">r&#xE9;sistance interm&#xE9;diaire &#x00E0; la d&#xE9;formation</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>peak crush resistance</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>peak crush resistance</dfn>
</span> means the greatest force required to deform the door of a vehicle over the entire crush distance of 457&#xA0;mm; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">r&#xE9;sistance maximale &#x00E0; la d&#xE9;formation</span>) </p>
</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(2)ID0EDG0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every side door that is designed to be used for the egress of occupants from a truck, multi-purpose passenger vehicle or bus with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less or from a passenger car or three-wheeled vehicle shall demonstrate the following resistances, calculated in accordance with <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 214 &#x2014; Side Door Strength</cite> (November&#xA0;14, 1996), when tested in accordance with those test methods with the seats removed or installed, at the option of the manufacturer:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EEBG0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;when tested with the seats removed,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(2)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBCBG0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an initial crush resistance of not less than 10.01&#xA0;kN,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(2)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBBBG0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an intermediate crush resistance of not less than 15.57&#xA0;kN, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(2)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBABG0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a peak crush resistance of not less than two times the curb mass of the vehicle or 31.14&#xA0;kN, whichever is the lesser; or</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EEAG0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;when tested with the seats installed,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBCAG0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an initial crush resistance of not less than 10.01&#xA0;kN,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBBAG0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an intermediate crush resistance of not less than 19.46&#xA0;kN, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(iii)ID0EBAAG0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a peak crush resistance of not less than three and one- half times the curb mass of the vehicle or 53.38&#xA0;kN, whichever is the lesser.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(3)ID0EBF0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of paragraph&#xA0;(2)(<em>a</em>), only those seats that may affect any load applied during the test must be removed from the vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(4)ID0EEE0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subsection&#xA0;(2) does not apply in respect of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EBCE0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the detachable side doors of a vehicle that is designed to be used without side doors;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EBBE0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the side doors of a walk-in van; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(4)p-(c)ID0EDAE0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the side doors of a vehicle where, with an H-point template described in section&#xA0;4.1 of SAE Standard J826, <cite class="XRefExternal">Devices for Use in Defining and Measuring Vehicle Seating Accommodation</cite> (July 1995) positioned in any seat, the seat adjusted to any position and the seat back placed in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(6),</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(4)p-(c)subp-(i)ID0EBBAE0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;no point on a 254&#xA0;mm horizontal longitudinal line passing through and bisected by the H-point falls within the transverse, horizontal projection of the door&#x2019;s opening, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(4)p-(c)subp-(ii)ID0EBAAE0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;no point on a longitudinal vertical plane tangent to the outboard side of the seat cushion is less than 254&#xA0;mm from the innermost point on the inside surface of the door, which point is situated vertically between the H-point and shoulder reference point of the template and longitudinally between the front edge of the cushion with the seat adjusted to its forwardmost position and the rear edge of the cushion with the seat adjusted to its rearmost position, as illustrated in the figure.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(5)ID0EBD0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Where a vehicle has seat anchoring hardware, the conditions set out in paragraph&#xA0;(4)(<em>c</em>) shall be met with any seat recommended by the manufacturer installed in any position for which there is seat anchoring hardware.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-(6)ID0EBC0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of paragraph&#xA0;(4)(<em>c</em>), the seat back shall be placed in the manufacturer&#x2019;s nominal design riding position in the manner specified by the manufacturer or, if the manner is not specified by the manufacturer, at the first detent rearward of 25&#xB0; from the vertical, with every adjustable head restraint placed in its highest adjustment position and the adjustable lumbar support placed so that it is set in its released, full-back position.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-214ss-ID0ECB0QB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">
</span>
</a>&#xA0;</p>
<figure>
<div class="imageGroupcenter">
<img src="http://laws-lois.justice.gc.ca/images/CRC1038img/CRC1038_e066.png" alt="Diagram showing the Door Clearance with measurements and descriptions">
</div>
<figcaption>
<p class="caption Centered">FIGURE &#x2014; DOOR CLEARANCE</p>
</figcaption>
</figure>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">

<li> SOR/97-201, s. 3;</li>
<li> SOR/2003-272, s. 28;</li>
<li> SOR/2006-94, s. 4(E);</li>
<li> SOR/2007-180, s. 17.</li>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Bumpers</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>215</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-215ss-(1)ID0EDD0OB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A passenger car shall be equipped with bumpers that conform to either</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-215ss-(1)p-(a)ID0EBBD0OB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the requirements set out in paragraph 6, and the low-speed-impact test procedure set out in Annex&#xA0;3 &#x2014; except for paragraph&#xA0;4 of that Annex, of ECE Regulation No.&#xA0;42 &#x2014; <cite class="XRefExternal">Uniform Provisions Concerning the Approval of Vehicles with Regard to Their Front and Rear Protective Devices (Bumpers, etc.)</cite>, in the version dated June&#xA0;12, 2007, as amended after that date by any amendment in the 00 series of amendments; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-215ss-(1)p-(b)ID0EBAD0OB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the requirements, conditions and test procedures set out in title&#xA0;49, part&#xA0;581, of the <cite class="XRefExternal">Code of Federal Regulations</cite> of the United States (revised as of October&#xA0;1, 2006).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-215ss-(2)ID0EBC0OB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Until August&#xA0;31, 2009, a passenger car may conform either to the requirements of this section in its current version or as it read before the coming into force of these Regulations.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-215ss-(3)ID0EBB0OB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A passenger car shall conform to the requirements of this section as of September&#xA0;1, 2009.</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Roof Crush Resistance (Standard 216)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>216</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-216ss-(1)ID0EBE0MB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck or bus with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less, except trucks with a GVWR greater than 2&#xA0;722&#xA0;kg built from a cutaway chassis, school buses and convertibles, shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;216, Roof Crush Resistance</cite> (TSD&#xA0;216), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-216ss-(2)ID0EBD0MB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck or bus with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less that is built in two or more stages not using a chassis-cab and every passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck or bus with a GVWR greater than 2&#xA0;722&#xA0;kg but not greater than 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg that has an altered roof shall conform to the requirements of TSD&#xA0;216 or TSD&#xA0;220, which is referred to in section&#xA0;220 of this schedule.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-216ss-(3)ID0EBC0MB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Until August 31, 2016, the vehicles referred to in subsections&#xA0;(1) and (2) may conform to the requirements of this section as it read on the day before the day on which this version of the section came into force.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-216ss-(4)ID0EBB0MB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 21]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/94-291, s. 5;</li>
<li> SOR/2000-402, s. 1;</li>
<li> SOR/2006-94, s. 4(E);</li>
<li> SOR/2009-291, s. 4;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-82, s. 6;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-307, s. 21.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Bus Window Retention, Release and Emergency Exits</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>217</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(1)ID0EB60KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subsections&#xA0;(2) and (2.1) do not apply to a windshield or a window of a size such that the length of the smallest chord along the surface of the glazing passing through the centroid is less than 200&#xA0;mm (8&#xA0;in.).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(2)ID0EB50KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every window glazing and surrounding window frame in a bus shall be retained by its surrounding structure in a manner that prevents the formation of an opening large enough to admit the passage of a sphere with a diameter of 100&#xA0;mm (4&#xA0;inches) that is pressed through the opening by a force of 22&#xA0;N (5&#xA0;pounds) including the weight of the sphere, when the window is tested according to the procedure set out in subsection&#xA0;(2.1).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(2.1)ID0EF40KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Under the conditions set out in subsections&#xA0;(24) and (25), an increasing force shall be applied to the head form specified in Figure&#xA0;4 to this section to cause it to move at a velocity of 51&#xA0;mm per minute (2&#xA0;in. per minute) from a point inside the vehicle that is at the centroid of the window glazing in a direction that is outward and perpendicular to the undisturbed surface of the glazing until one of the following occurs:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(2.1)p-(a)ID0EBD40KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the force equals 5&#xA0;300&#xA0;N (1,200&#xA0;lb.);</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(2.1)p-(b)ID0EBC40KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;cracks have developed that penetrate to a depth of at least 80 per cent of the thickness of the glazing and radiate outward from the point of contact of the head form to two or more points at the window frame;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(2.1)p-(c)ID0EBB40KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the glazing shatters; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(2.1)p-(d)ID0EDA40KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the inner surface of the glazing at the centroid has moved perpendicularly to the undisturbed surface of the glazing a distance equal to the square root of the length of the smallest chord along the surface of the glazing passing through the centroid divided by</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(2.1)p-(d)subp-(i)ID0EBBA40KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;1.25, where the distance is measured in centimetres, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(2.1)p-(d)subp-(ii)ID0EBAA40KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;2, where the distance is measured in inches.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(3)ID0ED30KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every bus, other than a school bus and a bus manufactured for the purpose of transporting persons under physical restraint, shall be provided with unobstructed openings for rapidly urgent egress, the combined areas of which, when measured</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBB30KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in square centimetres, is equal to at least 430&#xA0;times the number of designated seating positions on the bus; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBA30KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in square inches, is equal to at least 67&#xA0;times the number of designated seating positions on the bus.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(4)ID0EB20KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A minimum of 40 per cent of the combined areas of the unobstructed openings required by subsection&#xA0;(3) shall be provided on each side of the bus.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(5)ID0EB10KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In determining the combined areas of unobstructed openings provided in a bus, no emergency exit, regardless of its actual area, shall be deemed to measure more than 3&#xA0;450&#xA0;cm<sup>2</sup> (536&#xA0;square inches).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(6)ID0EDZ0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(7), the unobstructed openings required by subsection&#xA0;(3) shall be provided in every bus with a GVWR of more than 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg (10,000&#xA0;lb.) by</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(6)p-(a)ID0EBBZ0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at least one side door for each three designated seating positions in the vehicle; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(6)p-(b)ID0EBAZ0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;side exits and at least one rear emergency exit that meets the requirements of subsections&#xA0;(11) to (14) when the bus is upright and when it is overturned on its side and any occupant is standing facing the rear emergency exit.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(7)ID0EBY0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Where the configuration of a bus described in subsection&#xA0;(6) precludes the installation of an accessible rear emergency exit, the bus shall be equipped in its rear half with a roof emergency exit that meets the requirements of subsections&#xA0;(11) to (14) when the bus is overturned on its side and any occupant is standing facing the roof emergency exit.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(8)ID0EEX0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The unobstructed openings required by subsection&#xA0;(3) shall be provided in every bus with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg (10,000&#xA0;lb.) or less by</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(8)p-(a)ID0EBCX0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;devices that meet the requirements of subsections&#xA0;(11) to (14) and do not use remote controls or central power systems;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(8)p-(b)ID0EBBX0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;windows that can be opened manually to a position providing an opening large enough to admit unobstructed passage of an ellipsoid, with its major axis parallel to the longitudinal axis of the vehicle, that is generated by the rotation about its minor axis of an ellipse having a major axis of 500&#xA0;mm (20&#xA0;inches) and a minor axis of 330&#xA0;mm (13&#xA0;inches); or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(8)p-(c)ID0EBAX0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;doors.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(9)ID0EEW0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every school bus shall be provided with, at the option of the manufacturer,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(9)p-(a)ID0EBCW0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;one rear emergency door that opens outward and is hinged on the right side for a bus with a GVWR of more than 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg (10,000&#xA0;lb.);</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(9)p-(b)ID0EBBW0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at least one rear emergency door that opens outward and is hinged on either side for a bus with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg (10,000&#xA0;lb.) or less; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(9)p-(c)ID0EDAW0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the following emergency exits, namely,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(9)p-(c)subp-(i)ID0EDBAW0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;one emergency door</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(9)p-(c)subp-(i)Clause(A)ID0EBBBAW0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(A)</span>
</a>&#xA0;hinged on its forward side, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(9)p-(c)subp-(i)Clause(B)ID0EBABAW0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(B)</span>
</a>&#xA0;located on the left side of the bus in the rear half of the bus passenger compartment, and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(9)p-(c)subp-(ii)ID0EEAAW0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;one push-out rear window that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(9)p-(c)subp-(ii)Clause(A)ID0EBCAAW0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(A)</span>
</a>&#xA0;provides a minimum opening clearance 400&#xA0;mm (16&#xA0;in.) high and 1&#xA0;200&#xA0;mm (48&#xA0;in.) wide,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(9)p-(c)subp-(ii)Clause(B)ID0EBBAAW0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(B)</span>
</a>&#xA0;is capable of being released by the operation of not more than two mechanisms that are located in the high-force access region as shown in Figure&#xA0;3C and that do not have to be operated simultaneously, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Clause">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(9)p-(c)subp-(ii)Clause(C)ID0EBAAAW0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(C)</span>
</a>&#xA0;for release and opening, requires a force of not more than 180&#xA0;N (40&#xA0;lb.) applied in the directions specified in subsections&#xA0;(13) and (14).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(10)ID0EDV0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every school bus shall be provided with a warning system that shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(10)p-(a)ID0EEBV0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be activated when the vehicle ignition is in the ON position and</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(10)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBCBV0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;any emergency exit of the bus is locked in such a manner that the release mechanism of the exit cannot be activated by a person at that exit without the use of a special device, such as a key, or special information, such as a lock combination,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(10)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBBBV0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a release mechanism that opens an emergency exit is not in the fully latched position, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(10)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBABV0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;one or more emergency exits are not in the fully closed position; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(10)p-(b)ID0EBAV0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;generate a continuous warning sound audible at the driver&#x2019;s seating position and in the immediate vicinity of the emergency door or push-out window that caused the system to be activated.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(11)ID0EBU0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every push-out window or other emergency exit not required by subsection&#xA0;(9) shall have one or two release mechanisms located within the access regions shown in Figure&#xA0;1, Figure&#xA0;2 or Figure&#xA0;3.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(12)ID0EET0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The lower edge of the low-force access region in Figure&#xA0;1 and the lower edge of region&#xA0;B of the high-force access region in Figure&#xA0;2 shall be located</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(12)p-(a)ID0EBCT0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;130&#xA0;mm (five inches) above the adjacent seat, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(12)p-(b)ID0EBBT0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;if an arm rest is fitted, 50&#xA0;mm (two inches) above the arm rest,</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="ContinuedSectionSubsection">whichever is the higher.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(13)ID0EDS0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(13)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When tested in accordance with the conditions set out in subsections&#xA0;(24) and (26) both before and after the window retention test described by subsection&#xA0;(2), every emergency exit of a bus, other than an emergency door required by subsection&#xA0;(9), shall allow manual release of the exit release mechanism by an occupant using, at the option of the manufacturer,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(13)p-(a)ID0EBBS0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a low-force application of not more than 90&#xA0;N (20&#xA0;pounds) in a rotational or linear direction if the emergency exit release mechanism is located as shown in Figure&#xA0;1 or Figure&#xA0;3 of this section; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(13)p-(b)ID0EBAS0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a high-force application of not more than 270&#xA0;N (60&#xA0;pounds) in a linear direction perpendicular to the undisturbed emergency exit surface if the emergency exit release mechanism is located as shown in Figure&#xA0;2 or Figure&#xA0;3 of this section.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(14)ID0EBR0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(14)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every emergency exit release mechanism shall require for its operation not more than two applications of force, one of which must differ by 90 to 180&#xA0;degrees from the direction of the initial push-out motion of the emergency exit.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(15)ID0EEQ0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(15)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Under the conditions set out in subsections&#xA0;(24) and (26), both before and after the window retention test described in subsection&#xA0;(2.1), every school bus emergency door shall be capable of being manually released by one person, from inside and outside the bus, using a force not exceeding 180&#xA0;N (40&#xA0;lb.) that is applied</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(15)p-(a)ID0EBCQ0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;within the access region for high forces shown in Figure&#xA0;3B to this section for a side emergency exit door and in Figure&#xA0;3D to this section for a rear emergency exit door;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(15)p-(b)ID0EBBQ0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in any direction from outside the bus; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(15)p-(c)ID0EBAQ0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in an upward direction from inside the bus.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(16)ID0EBP0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(16)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every school bus emergency door release mechanism shall be capable of being operated without the use of remote controls or tools and shall function independently of the vehicle&#x2019;s power system.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(17)ID0EBO0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(17)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every emergency exit of a bus, other than an emergency door required by subsection&#xA0;(9), shall, after the release mechanism has been operated, be capable of being opened outward manually by an occupant, using the force applications described in subsection&#xA0;(13), to a position providing an opening large enough to allow the unobstructed passage of the ellipsoid described in paragraph&#xA0;(8)(<em>b</em>).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(18)ID0EDN0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(18)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Under the conditions set out in subsections&#xA0;(24) and (26), both before and after the window retention test described in subsection&#xA0;(2.1), every emergency exit door of a school bus shall, after the release mechanism has been operated, be capable of being opened outward manually by one person to a position that provides</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(18)p-(a)ID0EBBN0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a side emergency exit door, an opening at least 1&#xA0;143&#xA0;mm (45 in.) high and 610&#xA0;mm (24&#xA0;in.) wide located so that a vertical transverse plane tangent to the rearmost point of the closest seat back passes through the forward edge of the side emergency exit door; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(18)p-(b)ID0EBAN0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a rear emergency exit door, an opening at least 610&#xA0;mm (24&#xA0;in.) wide that allows the unobstructed passage of a rectangular parallelepiped that measures l&#xA0;143&#xA0;mm (45&#xA0;in.) in height, 305&#xA0;mm (12&#xA0;in.) in width perpendicular to the sides of the bus, and 610&#xA0;mm (24&#xA0;in.) in depth parallel to the sides of the bus, the bottom of which remains within 25&#xA0;mm (1&#xA0;in.) of the floor at all times during its passage through the opening.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(18.1)ID0EBM0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(18.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;After insertion of a rectangular parallelepiped described in paragraph&#xA0;(18)(<em>b</em>), a rear emergency exit door or, where there are two rear emergency exit doors, both doors, shall be capable of being closed and latched.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(18.2)ID0EEL0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(18.2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A school bus that has a GVWR of less than 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg (10,000&#xA0;lb.) and two rear doors that function as emergency exit doors shall have</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(18.2)p-(a)ID0EBCL0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a single release mechanism that simultaneously opens both rear doors in a manner such that neither rear door can interfere with the opening of the other rear door under any circumstances;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(18.2)p-(b)ID0EBBL0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;hinging and latching mechanisms that prevent the rear doors from opening when they are closed and fully latched and, under the conditions set out in subsections&#xA0;(24) and (26), a force of 9&#xA0;000&#xA0;N (2,000&#xA0;lb.) is applied perpendicularly to any part of the door other than the window glass by a circular steel plate having a diameter of 150&#xA0;mm (6&#xA0;in.) and a thickness of 13&#xA0;mm (&#xA0;in.); and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(18.2)p-(c)ID0EBAL0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a single interior handle that operates the latching mechanisms and that is situated within 150&#xA0;mm (6&#xA0;in.) of a vertical plane equidistant from both sides of the aisle leading to the rear doors when the rear doors are closed and fully latched.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(18.3)ID0EBK0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(18.3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The rear doors of a school bus referred to in subsection&#xA0;(18.2) shall, under the conditions set out in subsections&#xA0;(24) and (26) and, after undergoing the test specified in paragraph (18.2)(<em>b</em>), be capable of being opened from outside and inside the bus using a force not exceeding 180&#xA0;N (40&#xA0;lb.).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(19)ID0EBJ0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(19)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every push-out window or other emergency exit in a bus shall, for the purposes of identification and operation, be identified with a label located within 150&#xA0;mm (six inches) of its release mechanism bearing words in both official languages or an approved symbol that identifies the emergency exit, and followed by concise operation instructions in both official languages, except that school bus emergency exits shall be identified in accordance with the requirements of subsection&#xA0;(23).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(20)ID0EBI0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(20)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Where a release mechanism is not located within the occupant space of an adjacent seat, a label indicating the location of the nearest release mechanism in both official languages and meeting the requirements of subsection&#xA0;(21) shall be placed within the occupant space.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(21)ID0EDH0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(21)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The marking on every label referred to in subsections&#xA0;(19) and (20) shall be legible to an occupant with corrected visual acuity corresponding to a Snellen ratio of 20/40 who is a person described in</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(21)p-(a)ID0EBBH0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;paragraph&#xA0;(22)(<em>a</em>), (<em>b</em>) or (<em>c</em>) when the locations described in the other two of those paragraphs are occupied; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(21)p-(b)ID0EBAH0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;paragraph&#xA0;(22)(<em>d</em>) or (<em>e</em>) when the only source of light is the normal night time illumination of the bus interior and the occupant is a person described in subsection&#xA0;(22).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(22)ID0EGG0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(22)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of subsection&#xA0;(21), the following persons are described:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(22)p-(a)ID0EBEG0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a person seated in the adjacent seat;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(22)p-(b)ID0EBDG0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a person seated in the seat directly adjoining the adjacent seat;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(22)p-(c)ID0EBCG0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a person standing in the aisle location that is closest to the adjacent seat;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(22)p-(d)ID0EBBG0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a person standing in the aisle location nearest to the emergency exit when the exit has no adjacent seat; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(22)p-(e)ID0EBAG0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a person lying with his back against the floor opposite the roof emergency exit if the vehicle is so equipped.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(23)ID0EDF0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(23)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Each school bus emergency exit provided in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(9) shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(23)p-(a)ID0EBBF0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be identified as &#x201C;Emergency Door&#x201D; and &#x201C;<span class="otherLang" lang="fr">Porte de secours</span>&#x201D; or &#x201C;Emergency Exit&#x201D; and &#x201C;<span class="otherLang" lang="fr">Issue de secours</span>&#x201D; or &#x201C;<span class="otherLang" lang="fr">Sortie de secours</span>&#x201D;, whichever is applicable, in letters at least 50&#xA0;mm (2&#xA0;in.) high of a colour that contrasts with its background located at the top of or directly above the emergency door or exit on both the inside and outside surfaces of the bus; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(23)p-(b)ID0EBAF0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;have concise operating instructions describing the motions and, if applicable, sequence of motions necessary to unlatch and open the emergency door or exit, in letters at least 9.5&#xA0;mm (3/8&#xA0;in.) high of a colour that contrasts with its background, located within 150&#xA0;mm (6&#xA0;in.) of the release mechanism on the inside surface of the bus.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(24)ID0EDE0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(24)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of subsections&#xA0;(2), (13), (15), (17) and (18)</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(24)p-(a)ID0EBBE0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the vehicle shall be on a flat, horizontal surface; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(24)p-(b)ID0EBAE0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the temperature inside and outside shall be maintained between 20&#xB0;C and 30&#xB0;C (70&#xB0;F and 85&#xB0;F) for a period of four hours immediately preceding the tests and during the tests.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(25)ID0EBD0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(25)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purpose of subsection&#xA0;(2), all windows installed in the vehicle shall be closed and latched in the manner intended for normal bus operation if latches are provided, except that to demonstrate compliance of windows installed in folding doors, the test need not be performed with the doors installed in the vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-(26)ID0EBC0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(26)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of subsections&#xA0;(13), (15), (17) and (18), all seats, arm rests and interior objects near the windows of the vehicle shall be adjusted for normal use with the seats in the upright position.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-217ss-ID0EFB0KB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">
</span>
</a>&#xA0;</p>
