<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Windshield Zone Intrusion</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>219</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-219ss-(1)ID0EBD0IB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every passenger car, other than a forward control configuration vehicle or an open-body type vehicle with a fold-down or removable windshield, shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No. 219, Windshield Zone Intrusion</cite> (TSD 219), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-219ss-(2)ID0EBC0IB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every truck, bus and multi-purpose passenger vehicle with a GVWR of 4 536 kg or less, other than a walk-in van, a forward control configuration vehicle or an open-body type vehicle with a fold-down or removable windshield, shall conform to the requirements of TSD 219, as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-219ss-(3)ID0EBB0IB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 22]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/81-665, s. 2;</li>
<li> SOR/97-201, s. 4;</li>
<li> SOR/97-421, ss. 17, 22(F);</li>
<li> SOR/2008-72, s. 12(F);</li>
<li> SOR/2009-121, s. 4;</li>
<li> SOR/2013-9, s. 8;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-307, s. 22.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Rollover Protection (Standard 220)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>220</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-220ss-(1)ID0EBD0GB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every school bus shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;220, Rollover Protection</cite> (TSD&#xA0;220), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-220ss-(2)ID0EBC0GB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck or bus with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less that is built in two or more stages not using a chassis-cab and every passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck or bus with a GVWR greater than 2&#xA0;722&#xA0;kg but not greater than 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg that has an altered roof shall conform to the requirements of TSD&#xA0;220 or TSD&#xA0;216, which is referred to in section&#xA0;216 of this schedule.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-220ss-(3)ID0EBB0GB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 23]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/79-940, s. 9;</li>
<li> SOR/2009-291, s. 5;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-82, s. 7;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-307, s. 23.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">School Bus Body Joint Strength (Standard&#xA0;221)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>221</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-221ss-(1)ID0EHI0EB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The following definitions in this subsection apply in this section.</p>
<dl class="Definition">
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>body component</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>body component</dfn>
</span> means a part of a bus body, including floor panels, made from a single piece of homogeneous material or from a single piece of composite material such as plywood or plastic. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">&#xE9;l&#xE9;ment de carrosserie</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>body panel</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>body panel</dfn>
</span> means a body component used on the exterior or interior surface of a bus to enclose the bus occupant space. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">panneau de carrosserie</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>body panel joint</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>body panel joint</dfn>
</span> means the area of contact, attachment or close proximity between the edges of a body panel and another body component. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">joint de panneau de carrosserie</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>bus body</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>bus body</dfn>
</span> means the portion of a bus that encloses the bus occupant space, including the floor and the body panel separating the engine compartment from the occupant space, but excluding the bumpers and chassis frame. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">carrosserie d&#x2019;autobus</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>maintenance access panel</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>maintenance access panel</dfn>
</span> means a body panel that must be moved or removed to provide access to serviceable components. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">panneau d&#x2019;accs pour l&#x2019;entretien</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>serviceable component</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>serviceable component</dfn>
</span> means any part of a bus, of either a mechanical or electrical nature, that is explicitly identified in the owner&#x2019;s manual or factory service manual as requiring routine maintenance actions at intervals of one year or less. Tubing, wires and harnesses are considered to be serviceable components only at their attachments. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">&#xE9;l&#xE9;ment n&#xE9;cessitant de l&#x2019;entretien</span>) </p>
</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-221ss-(2)ID0EGH0EB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;This section applies in respect of all school bus body panel joints that lie rearward of the vertical transverse plane located 762&#xA0;mm in front of the forward-most passenger seating reference point, except those that contact or are attached to or in close proximity to</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-221ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EBEH0EB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;components such as rub rails that are entirely outside of body panels;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-221ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EBDH0EB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;doors, windows, ventilation panels, engine access covers or destination sign covers;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-221ss-(2)p-(c)ID0EBCH0EB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;trim or decorative parts that do not contribute to the strength of a body panel joint;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-221ss-(2)p-(d)ID0EBBH0EB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;interior maintenance access panels that are 305&#xA0;mm or less when measured across any two points on the diametrically opposite sides of the opening; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-221ss-(2)p-(e)ID0EBAH0EB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;all exterior maintenance access panels.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-221ss-(3)ID0EBG0EB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(4), when tested in accordance with <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 221, School Bus Body Joint Strength</cite> (October 20, 2000), every body panel joint shall be capable of sustaining, without separation, a tensile force that is equal to 60% of the breaking tensile strength within the weakest body panel component attached by the joint.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-221ss-(4)ID0EBF0EB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A body panel joint is not required to be tested if a test specimen cannot be obtained in accordance with <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 221, School Bus Body Joint Strength</cite> (October&#xA0;20, 2000) or it has only one discrete fastener or spot weld.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-221ss-(5)ID0EBE0EB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Despite subsection&#xA0;(2), the maintenance access panels referred to in paragraph&#xA0;(2)(<em>d</em>) shall have no unattached segment at the joint longer than 110&#xA0;mm.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-221ss-(6)ID0EBD0EB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;On or before January&#xA0;14, 2002, a school bus having a GVWR of more than 4,536&#xA0;kg may conform to this section or to section&#xA0;221 as it read before the coming into force of this section.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-221ss-(7)ID0EBC0EB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;On or before January&#xA0;14, 2002, a school bus having a GVWR of 4,536&#xA0;kg or less may conform to this section.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-221ss-(8)ID0EBB0EB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;After January&#xA0;14, 2002, every school bus shall conform to this section.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/80-160, s. 2;</li>
<li> SOR/97-421, s. 17;</li>
<li> SOR/2001-36, s. 1.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">School Bus Passenger Seating and Crash Protection</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>222</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(1)ID0EGQ0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In this section,</p>
<dl class="Definition">
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>contactable surface</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>contactable surface</dfn>
</span> means any surface within the head protection zone that is contactable from any direction by a head form test device, except any surface on the front of a seat back or restraining barrier 76&#xA0;mm (three inches) or more below the top of the seat back or restraining barrier; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">surface de contact</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>head protection zones</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>head protection zones</dfn>
</span> means the spaces in front of each school bus passenger seat that are not occupied by any sidewall, window or door structure and that, in relation to that seat and its seating reference point, are enclosed by the following planes: </p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(1)Definitionp-(a)ID0EBDDQ0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;horizontal planes 300&#xA0;mm (12&#xA0;inches) and 1 016&#xA0;mm (40&#xA0;inches) above the seating reference point,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(1)Definitionp-(b)ID0EBCDQ0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a vertical longitudinal plane tangent to the inboard (aisle side) edge of the seat,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(1)Definitionp-(c)ID0EBBDQ0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a vertical longitudinal plane 83&#xA0;mm (3.25&#xA0;inches) inboard of the outboard edge of the seat, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(1)Definitionp-(d)ID0EBADQ0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;vertical transverse planes through and 760&#xA0;mm (30&#xA0;inches) forward of the seating reference point; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">zone de protection de la tte</span>)</p>
</li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>leg protection zones</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>leg protection zones</dfn>
</span> means those parts of a school bus passenger seat back or restraining barrier that are bounded by horizontal planes 300&#xA0;mm (12&#xA0;inches) above and 100&#xA0;mm (four inches) below the seating reference point of the school bus passenger seat immediately behind the seat back or restraining barrier; (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">zone de protection des jambes</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>school bus passenger seat</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>school bus passenger seat</dfn>
</span> means a seat in a school bus, other than the driver&#x2019;s seat or a seat that is installed to accommodate a handicapped or convalescent passenger and is oriented in a direction that is more than 45&#xA0;degrees to the left or right of the longitudinal centre-line of the vehicle. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">sige pour passager d&#x2019;autobus scolaire</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>W</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>W</dfn>
</span> means the number of seating positions in a bench seat when calculated as the bench width in millimetres (inches) divided by 381&#xA0;mm (15&#xA0;inches) with the quotient rounded to the nearest whole number or, if the quotient is equidistant from two whole numbers, to the higher thereof. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">W</span>) </p>
</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(2)ID0EBP0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every school bus shall, when subjected to Motor Vehicle Safety Test Methods, Section&#xA0;222, School Bus Passenger Seating and Crash Protection, (December&#xA0;19, 1983) meet, at all designated seating positions other than the driver&#x2019;s seat, all the requirements of subsections&#xA0;(6) to (12).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(3)ID0EDO0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Any particular passenger seat of a school bus used as a test specimen when the school bus is subjected to the test methods referred to in subsection&#xA0;(2), need not meet further requirements after having been subjected to the requirements of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBBO0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;subsections&#xA0;(6) and (9); or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBAO0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;subsection&#xA0;(7), (8), (11) or (12).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(4)ID0EBN0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Passenger seats on a school bus shall face directly either the front or the rear of the vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(5)ID0EBM0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The number of seating positions in a bench type seat shall be obtained by dividing the bench width measured in millimetres or inches by 381&#xA0;mm or 15&#xA0;inches, as the case may be, and rounding the quotient to the nearest whole number or, if the quotient is equidistant from two whole numbers, to the higher thereof.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(6)ID0EDL0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every school bus passenger seat shall be equipped with a seat back having</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(6)p-(a)ID0EDBL0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a height of not less than</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(6)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBBBL0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;508&#xA0;mm (20&#xA0;inches) above the seating reference point, where the seat faces the front of the vehicle, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(6)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBABL0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;762&#xA0;mm (30&#xA0;inches) above the seating reference point, where the seat faces the rear of the vehicle; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(6)p-(b)ID0EDAL0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a front surface area of not less than 90 per cent of the seat bench width measured in millimetres or inches multiplied by 508&#xA0;mm or 20&#xA0;inches, as the case may be, that is</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(6)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBAL0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;above the horizontal plane that passes through the seating reference point, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(6)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBAAL0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;below the horizontal plane that passes through a point 508&#xA0;mm or 20&#xA0;inches above the seating reference point.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(7)ID0EHK0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Where a school bus passenger seat that has another seat behind it is subjected to forward performance tests as specified in the test methods referred to in subsection&#xA0;(2)</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(7)p-(a)ID0EBFK0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat back force/deflection curve shall fall within the zone specified in Figure&#xA0;1;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(7)p-(b)ID0EBEK0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat back deflection shall not exceed 356&#xA0;mm (14&#xA0;inches), as determined from the force/deflection curve;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(7)p-(c)ID0EBDK0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat shall not deflect by an amount such that any part of the seat moves to within 100&#xA0;mm (four inches) of any part of another school bus passenger seat or restraining barrier in its originally installed position;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(7)p-(d)ID0EBCK0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat shall not separate from the vehicle at any attachment point;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(7)p-(e)ID0EBBK0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat components shall not separate at any attachment point; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(7)p-(f)ID0EBAK0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the energy absorbed in deflecting the seat back shall be not less than 452W&#xA0;Nm (4000W&#xA0;inch-pounds), as determined from the force/deflection curve.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(7.1)ID0EDJ0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In subsection&#xA0;(7), <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>force/deflection curve</dfn>
</span> means,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(7.1)p-(a)ID0EBBJ0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;for the purposes of paragraphs&#xA0;(7)(<em>a</em>) and (<em>b</em>), the force applied by means of the upper loading bar and the forward travel distance of the pivot attachment point of the upper loading bar, measured from the point at which the initial application of 44.5&#xA0;N (10&#xA0;pounds) of force is attained; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(7.1)p-(b)ID0EBAJ0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;for the purposes of paragraph&#xA0;(7)(<em>f</em>), the force applied by means of the upper loading bar and the forward and rearward travel distance of the pivot attachment point of the upper loading bar measured from the position at which the initial application of 44.5&#xA0;N (10&#xA0;pounds) of force is attained.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(8)ID0EHI0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Where a school bus passenger seat that has another seat behind it is subjected to rearward performance tests as specified in the test methods referred to in subsection&#xA0;(2),</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(8)p-(a)ID0EBFI0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat back force shall not exceed 9&#xA0;876&#xA0;N (2,200&#xA0;pounds), as determined from the force/deflection curve;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(8)p-(b)ID0EBEI0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat back deflection shall not exceed 250&#xA0;mm (10&#xA0;inches), as determined by the force/deflection curve;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(8)p-(c)ID0EBDI0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat shall not deflect by an amount such that any part of the seat moves to within 100&#xA0;mm (four inches) of any part of another school bus passenger seat in its originally installed position;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(8)p-(d)ID0EBCI0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat shall not separate from the vehicle at any attachment point;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(8)p-(e)ID0EBBI0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(e)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the seat components shall not separate at any attachment point; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(8)p-(f)ID0EBAI0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(f)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the energy absorbed in deflecting the seat back shall be not less than 316.4&#xA0;W&#xA0;Nm (2800W&#xA0;inch-pounds), as determined from the force/deflection curve.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(8.1)ID0EDH0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In subsection&#xA0;(8) <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>force/deflection curve</dfn>
</span> means</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(8.1)p-(a)ID0EBBH0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;for the purposes of paragraphs&#xA0;(8)(<em>a</em>) and (<em>b</em>), the force applied by means of the loading bar and the rearward travel distance of the pivot attachment point of the loading bar measured from the point at which the initial application of 222.4&#xA0;N (50&#xA0;pounds) of force is attained; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(8.1)p-(b)ID0EBAH0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;for the purposes of paragraph&#xA0;(8)(<em>f</em>), the force applied by means of the loading bar and the rearward and forward travel distance of the pivot attachment point of the loading bar measured from the position at which the initial application of 222.4&#xA0;N (50&#xA0;pounds) of force is attained.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(9)ID0EBG0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;No seat cushion with which a school bus passenger seat is equipped shall, where all the manual attachment devices between the seat and the seat cushion are in the manufacturer&#x2019;s designed position for attachment, separate from the seat at any attachment point when subjected to an upward force of five times the seat cushion weight, applied in any period of not less than one nor more than two seconds, and maintained for five seconds.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(10)ID0EEF0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A restraining barrier shall be provided forward of any designated seating position that does not have the rear surface of another school bus passenger seat within 610&#xA0;mm (24&#xA0;inches) of the seating reference point, measured along a horizontal line through the seating reference point in the forward direction, such that</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(10)p-(a)ID0EBCF0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the horizontal distance between the restraining barrier&#x2019;s rear surface and the seating reference point of the seat in front of which it is required is not more than 610&#xA0;mm (24&#xA0;inches);</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(10)p-(b)ID0EBBF0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the position and rear surface area of the restraining barrier shall be such that, in a front projected view of the bus, each point of the barrier&#x2019;s perimeter coincides with or lies outside of the perimeter of the seat back of the seat for which it is required; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(10)p-(c)ID0EBAF0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;when subjected to a forward force, as specified in the test methods referred to in subsection&#xA0;(2), the restraining barrier shall meet all the requirements specified in paragraphs&#xA0;(7)(<em>a</em>), (<em>b</em>), (<em>d</em>), (<em>e</em>) and (<em>f</em>) as they apply to a seat, and the restraining barrier deflection shall not interfere with normal door operation.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(11)ID0EDE0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When any contactable surface of a school bus within the head protection zones is impacted from any direction by a head form test device, as specified in the test methods referred to in subsection&#xA0;(2),</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(11)p-(a)ID0EDBE0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at 6.7&#xA0;m/s (22&#xA0;feet per second),</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(11)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EDBBE0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the axial acceleration at the centre of gravity of the head form test device shall be such that the expression</p>
<div class="Subparagraph">
<figure>
<div class="imageGroupcenter">
<img src="http://laws-lois.justice.gc.ca/images/C.R.C.,_c._1038_e_graphics/C.R.C.,_c._1038_e_012.jpg" alt="Formula used to determine the head injury criteria of the head of each anthropomorphic test device">
</div>
</figure>
</div>
<p class="ContinuedSubparagraph">shall not exceed 1,000, where &#x201C;a&#x201D; is the axial acceleration expressed as a multiple of &#x201C;g&#x201D; (the acceleration due to gravity), and t<sub>1</sub> and t<sub>2</sub> are any two points in time during the impact, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(11)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBABE0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the energy necessary to deflect the impacted material shall be not less than 4.52&#xA0;Nm (40&#xA0;inch-pounds) before the force level on the head form test device exceeds 667&#xA0;N (150&#xA0;pounds); and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(11)p-(b)ID0EBAE0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at 1.5&#xA0;m/s (five feet per second) the contact area on the head form test device surface shall not be less than 1&#xA0;935&#xA0;mm<sup>2</sup> (three square inches).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(12)ID0EDD0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When any point on the rear surface of a part of a seat back or restraining barrier within the leg protection zone is impacted from any direction by a knee form test device, as specified in the test methods referred to in subsection&#xA0;(2) at 4.88&#xA0;m/s (16&#xA0;feet per second)</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(12)p-(a)ID0EBBD0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the resisting force of the impacted material shall not exceed 2&#xA0;669&#xA0;N (600&#xA0;pounds); and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(12)p-(b)ID0EBAD0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the contact area on the knee form test device surface shall not be less than 1&#xA0;935&#xA0;mm<sup>2</sup> (three square inches).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-(13)ID0EBC0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(13)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every school bus passenger seat shall be fastened to the floor of the bus by bolts that have nuts and locking devices such as lock washers.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-222ss-ID0ECB0CB0BA">
<span class="lawlabel">
</span>
</a>&#xA0;</p>
<figure>
<figcaption>
<p class="caption Centered">FIGURE 1 &#x2014; FORCE/DEFLECTION ZONE</p>
</figcaption>
<div class="imageGroupcenter">
<img src="http://laws-lois.justice.gc.ca/images/CRC1038img/CRC1038_e084.png" alt="Diagram showing the Force / Deflection Zone">
</div>
</figure>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">

<li> SOR/86-4 53, s. 3;</li>
<li> SOR/91-593, s. 1.</li>
</ul>

</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Rear Impact Guards (Standard&#xA0;223)</span>
</h3>
<h4 class="SchedHeadL3">
<span class="HTitleText3">Interpretation</span>
</h4>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>223</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(1)ID0EPR6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The definitions in this subsection apply in this section.</p>
<dl class="Definition">
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>dangerous goods</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>dangerous goods</dfn>
</span> has the same meaning as in section&#xA0;2 of the Transportation of Dangerous Goods Act, 1992. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">marchandises dangereuses</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>ground clearance</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>ground clearance</dfn>
</span> means the vertical distance from the bottom edge of a horizontal member to the ground. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">garde au sol</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>guard width</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>guard width</dfn>
</span> means, in respect of a rear impact guard that is installed on a trailer, the maximum horizontal guard dimension that is perpendicular to the longitudinal vertical plane passing through the longitudinal centreline of the trailer. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">largeur du dispositif de protection</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>horizontal member</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>horizontal member</dfn>
</span> means the horizontal structural member of a rear impact guard. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">pice horizontale</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>hydraulic guard</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>hydraulic guard</dfn>
</span> means a rear impact guard designed to use fluid properties to provide a resistance force to deformation. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">dispositif de protection hydraulique</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>low-chassis trailer</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>low-chassis trailer</dfn>
</span> means a trailer that has a chassis that extends behind the rearmost point of the rearmost tires and that has a lower rear surface that meets the configuration requirements of subsections&#xA0;(6) to (8). (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">remorque &#x00E0; ch&#xE2;ssis surbaiss&#xE9;</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>outboard</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>outboard</dfn>
</span> means, in respect of a trailer, away from the trailer centreline and toward the side extremities of the trailer. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">ext&#xE9;rieur</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>pulpwood trailer</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>pulpwood trailer</dfn>
</span> means a trailer that is designed exclusively to carry harvested logs or pulpwood and that is constructed with a skeletal frame with no means for the attachment of a solid bed, body or container. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">remorque pour bois &#x00E0; p&#xE2;te</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>rear extremity</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>rear extremity</dfn>
</span> means the rearmost point on a trailer that is above a horizontal plane located above the ground clearance and below a horizontal plane located 1&#xA0;900&#xA0;mm above the ground when the trailer is configured as specified in subsection&#xA0;(7) and when the trailer&#x2019;s cargo doors, tailgate and other permanent structures are positioned as they normally are when the trailer is in motion. However, non-structural protrusions, including but not limited to the following, are excluded from the determination of the rearmost point: </p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(1)Definitionp-(a)ID0EBDFR6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;tail lamps;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(1)Definitionp-(b)ID0EBCFR6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;rubber bumpers;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(1)Definitionp-(c)ID0EBBFR6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;hinges and latches; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(1)Definitionp-(d)ID0EBAFR6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;flexible aerodynamic devices that are capable of being folded to within 305&#xA0;mm from the transverse vertical plane tangent to the rearmost surface of the horizontal member and that, while positioned as they normally are when the trailer is in motion, are located forward of the transverse plane that is tangent to the rear bottom edge of the horizontal member and that intersects a point located 1&#xA0;210&#xA0;mm rearward of the rearmost surface of the horizontal member and 1&#xA0;740&#xA0;mm above the ground. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">extr&#xE9;mit&#xE9; arrire</span>)</p>
</li>
</ul>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>rear impact guard</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>rear impact guard</dfn>
</span> means a device installed on or near the rear of a trailer so that, when the trailer is struck from the rear, the device limits the distance that the striking vehicle&#x2019;s front end slides under the rear end of the trailer. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">dispositif de protection arrire</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>rounded corners</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>rounded corners</dfn>
</span> means the outermost ends of a rear impact guard&#x2019;s horizontal member that curve upward. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">coins arrondis</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>side extremity</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>side extremity</dfn>
</span> means the outermost point on a trailer&#x2019;s side that is above a horizontal plane located above the ground clearance, below a horizontal plane located 1&#xA0;900&#xA0;mm above the ground, and between a transverse vertical plane tangent to the rear extremity of the trailer and a transverse vertical plane located 305&#xA0;mm forward of that plane, with non-structural protrusions such as tail lamps, rubber bumpers, hinges and latches excluded from the determination of the outermost point. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">extr&#xE9;mit&#xE9; lat&#xE9;rale</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>tanker trailer</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>tanker trailer</dfn>
</span> means a trailer that is designed exclusively to transport dangerous goods and that meets the rear impact protection requirements of National Standard of Canada CAN/CSA-B620-98, <cite class="XRefExternal">Highway Tanks and Portable Tanks for the Transportation of Dangerous Goods</cite> (August 1998), including Appendices&#xA0;A and B, as amended in April 1999, March 2000, July 2000, April 2001, November 2001 and May 2002, published by CSA. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">remorque-citerne</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>wheels back trailer</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>wheels back trailer</dfn>
</span> means a trailer whose rearmost axle is permanently fixed and located such that the rearmost surface of the rearmost tires of the size recommended by the trailer manufacturer for that axle is not more than 305&#xA0;mm forward of the transverse vertical plane tangent to the rear extremity of the trailer. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">remorque &#x00E0; roues arrire recul&#xE9;es</span>) </p>
</dd>
</dl>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Application</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(2)ID0EEP6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;This section applies to every trailer with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or more other than</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EBCP6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a pole trailer, a pulpwood trailer, a wheels back trailer or a trailer designed to be used as temporary living quarters;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EBBP6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a low-chassis trailer; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(2)p-(c)ID0EBAP6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a trailer designed to interact with, or having, work-performing equipment located in or moving through the area that would be occupied by a horizontal member that meets the configuration requirements of subsections&#xA0;(6) to (8).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Rear Impact Guard Requirement</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(3)ID0EBN6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every trailer shall be equipped with a rear impact guard that meets the configuration requirements of subsections&#xA0;(5) to (8), as well as the applicable test requirements of subsections&#xA0;(9) to (12) when tested in accordance with <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 223 &#x2013; Rear Impact Guard</cite> (December 2003).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(4)ID0EBM6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Until September&#xA0;1, 2007, instead of being equipped with a rear impact guard in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(3), at the option of the manufacturer who installs the rear impact guard, a trailer may be equipped with a rear impact guard that is installed in accordance with <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;224 Rear Impact Protection</cite>, as amended from time to time and labelled in accordance with section&#xA0;571.223 of the <cite class="XRefExternalRegulation">Code of Federal Regulations</cite> of the United States, Title&#xA0;49 (revised as of October&#xA0;1, 2000).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Configuration Requirements</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(5)ID0EBK6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The horizontal member of a rear impact guard shall have a cross-sectional vertical height of at least 100&#xA0;mm at any point across the guard width when installed on a trailer.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(6)ID0EBJ6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The outermost surfaces of the horizontal member shall extend outboard to within 100&#xA0;mm of the longitudinal vertical planes that are tangent to the side extremities, but shall not extend outboard of those planes.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(7)ID0EBI6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When the trailer is resting on level ground, unloaded, with its full capacity of fuel, its tires inflated and its air suspension, if so equipped, pressurized in accordance with the manufacturer&#x2019;s recommendations, the ground clearance shall not exceed 560&#xA0;mm at any point across the full width of the horizontal member. However, rounded corners may curve upward within 255&#xA0;mm of the longitudinal vertical planes that are tangent to the side extremities.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(8)ID0EBH6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;At any height above the ground clearance, the rearmost surface of the horizontal member shall be located as close as practicable to a transverse vertical plane tangent to the rear extremity of the trailer, and no more than 305&#xA0;mm forward of that plane, as shown in Figure&#xA0;1. However, the horizontal member may extend rearward of the plane.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Test Requirements</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(9)ID0EDF6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every rear impact guard shall demonstrate resistance to the following forces applied at the P1 and P2 test locations shown in Figure&#xA0;2 by deflecting no more than 125&#xA0;mm:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(9)p-(a)ID0EBBF6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;50&#xA0;000&#xA0;N at test location P1 on either the left or the right side of the guard if it is symmetrical, but both sides must be independently tested if the guard is not symmetrical; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(9)p-(b)ID0EBAF6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;50&#xA0;000&#xA0;N at test location P2.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(10)ID0EEE6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(11), every rear impact guard shall,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(10)p-(a)ID0EBCE6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;by deflecting no more than 125&#xA0;mm, demonstrate resistance to a uniform test load of at least 350 000 N, which shall be applied uniformly across the horizontal member by a uniform load application structure centred on the guard, as shown in Figure&#xA0;2 of <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 223 &#x2013; Rear Impact Guard</cite> (December 2003);</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(10)p-(b)ID0EBBE6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a guard that demonstrates resistance to a uniform test load of 700&#xA0;000&#xA0;N or less, other than a hydraulic guard or one installed on a tanker trailer, absorb by plastic deformation at least 20 000 J of energy within the first 125&#xA0;mm of deflection; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(10)p-(c)ID0EBAE6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;have a ground clearance not exceeding 560&#xA0;mm, measured at each support to which the horizontal member is attached, as shown in Figure&#xA0;3, after completion of the energy absorption test or, if that test is not required, after completion of the uniform load test.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(11)ID0EBD6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;In the case of a rear impact guard that is symmetrical about the longitudinal vertical plane passing through the centre of the horizontal member, one half of the guard may be tested in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(12) if it is completely severed from the portion of the guard not being tested.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(12)ID0EEC6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When one half of a rear impact guard is tested it shall,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(12)p-(a)ID0EDCC6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;by deflecting no more than 125&#xA0;mm, demonstrate resistance to a test load of at least 175 000 N, which shall be applied</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(12)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBBCC6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;uniformly across the tested portion of the horizontal member by a uniform load application structure centred on that portion, as shown in Figure&#xA0;2 of <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 223 &#x2013; Rear Impact Guard</cite> (December 2003), or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(12)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBACC6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;by a single point load at one of the P3 test locations on the tested portion of the horizontal member, as shown in Figure&#xA0;2;</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(12)p-(b)ID0EBBC6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a tested portion of a horizontal member that demonstrates resistance to a test load of 350&#xA0;000&#xA0;N or less, other than a hydraulic guard or one installed on a tanker trailer, absorb by plastic deformation at least 10&#xA0;000&#xA0;J of energy within the first 125&#xA0;mm of deflection; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-(12)p-(c)ID0EBAC6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;have a ground clearance not exceeding 560&#xA0;mm, measured at each support to which the horizontal member is attached, as shown in Figure&#xA0;3, after completion of the energy absorption test or, if that test is not required, after completion of the uniform load test.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-223ss-ID0EEB6BA">
<span class="lawlabel">
</span>
</a>&#xA0;</p>

<h2 class="SchedHeadL1">
<span class="HLabel1">PART IV</span>
</h2>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Fuel System Integrity (Standard&#xA0;301)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>301</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301ss-(1)ID0EBD3BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every passenger car and every multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck and bus with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less that is equipped with a fuel system that uses a fuel with a boiling point of 0&#xB0;C or higher as a source of energy for its propulsion and every manufacturer of these vehicles shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;301, Fuel System Integrity</cite> (TSD&#xA0;301), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301ss-(2)ID0EBC3BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A school bus with a GVWR of more than 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg that is equipped with a fuel system that uses a fuel with a boiling point of 0&#xB0;C or higher as a source of energy for its propulsion shall conform to the requirements of TSD&#xA0;301.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301ss-(3)ID0EBB3BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 24]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/80-158, s. 1;</li>
<li> SOR/97-421, s. 17;</li>
<li> SOR/2001-152, s. 2;</li>
<li> SOR/2004-89, s. 1;</li>
<li> SOR/2006-94, s. 4(E);</li>
<li> SOR/2008-258, s. 10;</li>
<li> SOR/2009-79, s. 5;</li>
<li> SOR/2011-238, s. 5;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-307, s. 24.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">LPG Fuel System Integrity (Standard&#xA0;301.1)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>301.1</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(1)ID0EDJ1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsections&#xA0;(3) and (3.1), a vehicle that is equipped with a fuel system that uses LPG as a source of energy for its propulsion shall meet the requirements of subsection&#xA0;(2) when tested in accordance with <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 301.1 &#x2014; LPG Fuel System Integrity</cite> (February 28, 2004),</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(1)p-(a)ID0EEBJ1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a vehicle with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBCBJ1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;by the vehicle impacting a fixed collision barrier that is at any angle of up to 30&#xB0; in either direction to the perpendicular to the vehicle&#x2019;s line of travel while the vehicle is travelling longitudinally forward at any speed up to and including 48&#xA0;km/h,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBBBJ1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;by a collision barrier travelling at 48&#xA0;km/h impacting the vehicle from the rear, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBABJ1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;by a collision barrier travelling at 32&#xA0;km/h impacting the vehicle laterally on either side; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(1)p-(b)ID0EBAJ1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a vehicle with a GVWR of more than 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg, by a moving contoured barrier assembly travelling at any speed up to and including 48&#xA0;km/h impacting the vehicle at any point and any angle.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(1.1)ID0EBI1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Instead of being tested in accordance with subparagraph (1)(<em>a</em>)(ii), a vehicle referred to in subsection&#xA0;(1) may be tested in accordance with paragraph S6.2(b) of TSD 301, except the fuel spillage requirements, under the applicable conditions set out in sections&#xA0;3.2 to 3.4 of <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 301.1 &#x2013; LPG Fuel System Integrity</cite> (February&#xA0;28, 2004) and paragraph S7.3(b) of TSD 301.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(1.2)ID0EBH1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1.2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Instead of being tested in accordance with subparagraph (1)(<em>a</em>)(iii), a vehicle referred to in subsection&#xA0;(1) may be tested in accordance with paragraph S6.3(b) of TSD 301, except the fuel spillage requirements, under the applicable conditions set out in sections&#xA0;3.2 to 3.4 of <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 301.1 &#x2013; LPG Fuel System Integrity</cite> (February&#xA0;28, 2004) and paragraph S7.2(b) of TSD 301.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(1.3)ID0EBG1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1.3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 25]</span>
</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(2)ID0EEF1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When a vehicle is tested in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(1), (1.1) or (1.2),</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EBCF1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;fuel spillage from the fuel system after each impact from the moment of the impact until one-half hour after motion of the vehicle ceases shall not exceed 142 g;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EBBF1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the temperature-corrected pressure in the high-pressure portion of the fuel system shall not decrease to less than 95 per cent of the initial system pressure during the one-half hour period after motion of the vehicle ceases; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(2)p-(c)ID0EBAF1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the fuel container shall remain attached to the vehicle at a minimum of one attachment point.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(3)ID0EDE1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Instead of complying with subsections&#xA0;(1) and (2), a vehicle, other than a school bus, that is equipped with a fuel system that uses LPG as a source of energy for its propulsion may comply with</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBBE1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the version of National Standard of Canada CAN/CGA-12.2, <cite class="XRefExternal">Propane Fuel System Components for Use on Highway Vehicles</cite>, that, despite any statement to the contrary in that Standard, is in effect 24&#xA0;months before the date of the last manufacturing operation performed by the manufacturer who installed the fuel system, as shown on the manufacturer&#x2019;s information label, or the date of manufacture of the completed vehicle, as shown on the compliance label, or a more recent version of that Standard; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EDAE1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;section&#xA0;4, Installation of Propane Fuel Systems and Tanks on Highway Vehicles, of the version of National Standard of Canada CAN/CGA-B149.5, <cite class="XRefExternal">Installation Code for Propane Fuel Systems and Tanks on Highway Vehicles</cite>, that is in effect 24&#xA0;months before the date of the last manufacturing operation performed by the manufacturer who installed the fuel system, as shown on the manufacturer&#x2019;s information label, or the date of manufacture of the completed vehicle, as shown on the compliance label, or a more recent version of that Standard, except that the following requirements do not apply:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(3)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBAE1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;any requirement to obtain an approval from an authority having jurisdiction or an inspection authority of a province or territory, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(3)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBAAE1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;any requirement for the inspection or requalification of a fuel system or tank after the main assembly of the vehicle has been completed.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(3.1)ID0EBD1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A three-wheeled vehicle that is equipped with a fuel system that uses LPG as a source of energy for its propulsion shall comply with the standards referred to in subsection&#xA0;(3).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(4)ID0EBC1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A manufacturer of a vehicle that is equipped with a fuel system that uses LPG as a source of energy for its propulsion shall provide to the Minister, on request, information respecting the version of the standard referred to in subsection&#xA0;(3) with which the vehicle complies.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.1ss-(5)ID0EBB1BA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2004-89, s. 2]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/82-754, s. 3;</li>
<li> SOR/97-421, s. 17;</li>
<li> SOR/2001-152, s. 2;</li>
<li> SOR/2002-55, s. 18;</li>
<li> SOR/2003-272, s. 29;</li>
<li> SOR/2004-89, s. 2;</li>
<li> SOR/2008-104, s. 20;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-307, s. 25.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">CNG Fuel System Integrity (Standard&#xA0;301.2)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>301.2</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(1)ID0EDKYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsections&#xA0;(3) and (3.1), a vehicle that is equipped with a fuel system that uses CNG as a source of energy for its propulsion shall meet the requirements of subsection&#xA0;(2) when tested in accordance with <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 301.2 &#x2014; CNG Fuel System Integrity</cite> (February 28, 2004),</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(1)p-(a)ID0EEBKYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a vehicle with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBCBKYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;by the vehicle impacting a fixed collision barrier that is at any angle of up to 30&#xB0; in either direction to the perpendicular to the vehicle&#x2019;s line of travel while the vehicle is travelling longitudinally forward at any speed up to and including 48&#xA0;km/h,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBBBKYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;by a collision barrier travelling at 48&#xA0;km/h impacting the vehicle from the rear, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(1)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBABKYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;by a collision barrier travelling at 32&#xA0;km/h impacting the vehicle laterally on either side; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(1)p-(b)ID0EBAKYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a vehicle with a GVWR of more than 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg, by a moving contoured barrier assembly travelling at any speed up to and including 48&#xA0;km/h impacting the vehicle at any point and any angle.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(1.1)ID0EBJYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Instead of being tested in accordance with subparagraph&#xA0;(1)(<em>a</em>)(ii), a vehicle referred to in subsection&#xA0;(1) may be tested in accordance with paragraph&#xA0;S6.2(b) of TSD&#xA0;301, except for the fuel spillage requirements, under the applicable conditions set out in sections&#xA0;3.2 to 3.4 of <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 301.2 &#x2014; CNG Fuel System Integrity</cite> (February 28, 2004) and paragraph&#xA0;S7.3(b) of TSD&#xA0;301.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(1.2)ID0EBIYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1.2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Instead of being tested in accordance with subparagraph&#xA0;(1)(<em>a</em>)(iii), a vehicle referred to in subsection&#xA0;(1) may be tested in accordance with paragraph&#xA0;S6.3(b) of TSD&#xA0;301, except for the fuel spillage requirements, under the applicable conditions set out in sections&#xA0;3.2 to 3.4 of <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 301.2 &#x2014; CNG Fuel System Integrity</cite> (February 28, 2004) and paragraph&#xA0;S7.2(b) of TSD&#xA0;301.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(1.3)ID0EBHYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1.3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 26]</span>
</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(2)ID0EDGYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;When a vehicle is tested in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(1), (1.1) or (1.2),</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EBBGYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the fuel container shall remain attached to the vehicle at a minimum of one attachment point; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EDAGYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;when the pressure in the high-pressure portion of the fuel system is the greater of the maximum operating pressure and 20&#xA0;680&#xA0;kPa, this pressure shall not decrease during the 60-minute period after each impact by more than the greater of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBAGYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;1&#xA0;062&#xA0;kPa, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0ECAAGYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the product, expressed in kPa, obtained using the following formula:</p>
<div class="Subparagraph">
<p class="Formula">895 (T/V<sub>FS</sub>)</p>
<p class="FormulaGroup">where</p>
<dl class="FormulaDefinitionList">
<dt>
<dfn>T</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the ambient temperature of the test gas in degrees Kelvin, and</dd>
<dt>
<dfn>V<sub>FS</sub>
</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the volume of the high-pressure portion of the fuel system in litres.</dd>
</dl>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(3)ID0EDFYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Instead of complying with subsection&#xA0;(1), a vehicle, other than a school bus, that is equipped with a fuel system that uses CNG as a source of energy for its propulsion may comply with section&#xA0;4 of the version of Canadian Standards Association Standard CSA B109, <cite class="XRefExternal">Natural Gas for Vehicles Installation Code</cite>, that is in effect 24&#xA0;months before the date of the last manufacturing operation performed by the manufacturer who installed the fuel system, as shown on the manufacturer&#x2019;s information label, or the date of manufacture of the completed vehicle, as shown on the compliance label, or a more recent version of that Standard, except that the following requirements do not apply:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBBFYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;any requirement to obtain an approval from, or to act under the supervision of, an authority having jurisdiction or the boiler and pressure vessel inspection authority of a province or territory; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBAFYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;any requirement respecting inspection, service or repair after the main assembly of the vehicle has been completed.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(3.1)ID0EBEYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3.1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A three-wheeled vehicle that is equipped with a fuel system that uses CNG as a source of energy for its propulsion shall comply with the standard referred to in subsection&#xA0;(3).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(4)ID0EDDYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Only a CNG cylinder that is marked in accordance with the marking requirements in one of the following standards to indicate that the cylinder complies with that standard may be installed on a vehicle that is equipped with a fuel system that uses CNG as a source of energy for its propulsion:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EBBDYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the version of Canadian Standards Association Standard CSA B51, Part&#xA0;2, <cite class="XRefExternal">High-Pressure Cylinders for the Onboard Storage of Natural Gas as a Fuel for Automotive Vehicles</cite>, that is in effect 24&#xA0;months before the date of the last manufacturing operation performed by the manufacturer who installed the fuel system, as shown on the manufacturer&#x2019;s information label, or the date of manufacture of the completed vehicle, as shown on the compliance label, or a more recent version of that Standard; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EBADYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the version of American National Standard ANSI/AGA - NGV2, <cite class="XRefExternal">Basic Requirements for Compressed Natural Gas Vehicle (NGV) Fuel Containers</cite>, that is in effect 24&#xA0;months before the date of the last manufacturing operation performed by the manufacturer who installed the fuel system, as shown on the manufacturer&#x2019;s information label, or the date of manufacture of the completed vehicle, as shown on the compliance label, or a more recent version of that Standard.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(5)ID0EBCYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A manufacturer of a vehicle that is equipped with a fuel system that uses CNG as a source of energy for its propulsion shall provide to the Minister, on request, information respecting the version of the standards referred to in subsections&#xA0;(3) and (4) with which the vehicle complies.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.2ss-(6)ID0EBBYBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2004-89, s. 3]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">

<li> SOR/2001-152, s. 2;</li>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Fuel System Integrity for Three-wheeled Vehicles and Motorcycles (Standard&#xA0;301.3)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>301.3</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(1)ID0EBHWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A three-wheeled vehicle that is equipped with a fuel system that uses a fuel with a boiling point of 0&#xB0;C or higher as a source of energy for its propulsion shall meet the requirements of SAE Recommended Practice J288, <cite class="XRefExternal">Snowmobile Fuel Tanks</cite> (revised version of November 1983), except that section&#xA0;1 of that Practice does not apply.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(2)ID0EEGWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of this section,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EBCGWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the word &#x201C;should&#x201D; in sections&#xA0;3.2, 3.3 and 4.3 and in the footnote on page 5 of SAE Recommended Practice J288 shall be interpreted as expressing an obligation;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EBBGWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the words &#x201C;snowmobile fuel&#x201D; in sections&#xA0;3.2, 4.3 and 4.5 of SAE Recommended Practice J288 shall be read as &#x201C;unleaded gasoline&#x201D;; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(2)p-(c)ID0EBAGWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the word &#x201C;snowmobile&#x201D; in sections&#xA0;4.3 and 4.5 of SAE Recommended Practice J288 shall be read as &#x201C;vehicle&#x201D;.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(3)ID0EBFWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(5), a motorcycle that is equipped with a fuel system that uses a fuel with a boiling point of 0&#xB0;C or higher as a source of energy for its propulsion shall meet the requirements of SAE Recommended Practice J1241, <cite class="XRefExternal">Fuel and Lubricant Tanks for Motorcycles</cite> (revised version of November 1999), except that section&#xA0;1 of that Practice does not apply.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(4)ID0EDEWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of this section,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EBBEWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the words &#x201C;rated fuel capacity&#x201D; in SAE Recommended Practice J1241 shall have the same meaning as <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>vehicle fuel tank capacity</dfn>
</span> as defined in subsection&#xA0;2(1) of these Regulations; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EBAEWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the words &#x201C;significant effect&#x201D; in sections&#xA0;5.2.3 and 5.3.3 of SAE Recommended Practice J1241 shall be read as &#x201C;any effect resulting in the cracking or leaking of the tank&#x201D;.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(5)ID0EDDWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Instead of complying with subsection&#xA0;(3), a motorcycle that is equipped with a fuel system that uses a fuel with a boiling point of 0&#xB0;C or higher as a source of energy for its propulsion may meet the requirements of the following parts of Chapter&#xA0;6 of Directive 97/24/EC of the European Parliament and of the Council of June 17, 1997 on certain components and characteristics of two or three-wheel motor vehicles, as amended from time to time,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(5)p-(a)ID0EBBDWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Annex&#xA0;I, except that section&#xA0;1.0 does not apply; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(5)p-(b)ID0EBADWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Appendix&#xA0;1 to Annex&#xA0;I, except that sections&#xA0;2.2 and 4 of that Appendix do not apply.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(6)ID0EBCWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For the purposes of this section, the words &#x201C;rated capacity&#x201D; and &#x201C;nominal capacity&#x201D; in Annex&#xA0;I and Appendix&#xA0;1 to Annex&#xA0;I of Chapter&#xA0;6 of Directive 97/24/EC of the European Parliament and of the Council of June&#xA0;17, 1997 on certain components and characteristics of two or three-wheel motor vehicles shall have the same meaning as <span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>vehicle fuel tank capacity</dfn>
</span> as defined in subsection&#xA0;2(1) of these Regulations.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-301.3ss-(7)ID0EBBWBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Motorcycles that are manufactured before September&#xA0;1, 2004 need not comply with this section.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/2003-272, s. 31.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">

</h3>

<strong>302</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-302ss-(1)ID0EBCUBA">

</a>&#xA0;The interior materials of every passenger car, multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck, bus and three-wheeled vehicle shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;302, Flammability of Interior Materials</cite>, as amended from time to time.</p>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Electrolyte Spillage and Electrical Shock Protection (Standard&#xA0;305)</span>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>[SOR/2009-318, s. 13(F);</li>
<li> SOR/2011-238, s. 6]</li>
</ul>
</div>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>305</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-305ss-(1)ID0EBGSBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every passenger car and three-wheeled vehicle, and every multi-purpose passenger vehicle, truck and bus with a GVWR of 4&#xA0;536&#xA0;kg or less, that uses a nominal voltage of more than 60&#xA0;volts direct current (VDC) or more than 30&#xA0;volts alternating current (VAC) for its propulsion and that has an attainable speed of more than 40&#xA0;km/h over a distance of 1.6&#xA0;km on a paved level surface shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;305, Electrolyte Spillage and Electrical Shock Protection</cite> (TSD&#xA0;305), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-305ss-(2)ID0EBFSBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;S6.2, S6.3, S7.4 and S7.5 of TSD&#xA0;305 do not apply to a three-wheeled vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-305ss-(3)ID0EBESBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Instead of complying with S7.2.3 of TSD&#xA0;305, a three-wheeled vehicle, including test devices and instrumentation, shall be loaded to its unloaded vehicle weight, except that the vehicle fuel tank shall be filled to not less than 90&#xA0;per&#xA0;cent and not more than 95&#xA0;per&#xA0;cent of the vehicle fuel tank capacity.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-305ss-(4)ID0EBDSBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Instead of being tested in accordance with S6.2 of TSD&#xA0;305, a vehicle referred to in subsection&#xA0;(1), other than a three-wheeled vehicle, may be tested in accordance with the requirements of S6.2(b) of TSD&#xA0;301, except the fuel spillage requirements, under the applicable conditions set out in S7.3(b) of TSD&#xA0;301.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-305ss-(5)ID0EBCSBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;A vehicle tested in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(4) shall conform to the requirements of S5.1, S5.2 and S5.3 of TSD&#xA0;305.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-305ss-(6)ID0EBBSBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 28]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
