<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Low-speed Vehicles (Standard&#xA0;500)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>500</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-500ss-(1)ID0EBGOBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every low-speed vehicle shall conform to the requirements of <cite class="XRefExternal">Technical Standards Document No.&#xA0;500, Low-speed Vehicles</cite> (TSD&#xA0;500), as amended from time to time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-500ss-(2)ID0EBFOBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every low-speed vehicle shall be permanently marked with a slow-moving vehicle identification emblem (SMV emblem) that conforms to section&#xA0;6 of American National Standard <cite class="XRefExternal">Slow Moving Vehicle Identification Emblem (SMV Emblem)</cite>, ANSI/ASAE S276.6, published in January&#xA0;2005 by the American Society of Agricultural Engineers.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-500ss-(3)ID0EDEOBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;However, section&#xA0;6 of ANSI/ASAE S276.6 is modified as follows:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-500ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBBEOBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the dimensions of the SMV emblem may be greater than those specified in Figure&#xA0;1 as long as each dimension is increased so that it has the same relation to the other dimensions as the dimensions specified in the Figure have to each other; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-500ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBAEOBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the recommendation in paragraph&#xA0;6.2.6 is mandatory.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-500ss-(4)ID0EBDOBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The SMV emblem shall be mounted in accordance with paragraphs&#xA0;7.1.1 and 7.1.2 of ANSI/ASAE S276.6. It shall be mounted on the centreline or as near to the left of the centreline of the vehicle as practicable, not less than 500&#xA0;mm but not more than 1&#xA0;500&#xA0;mm above the surface of the roadway.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-500ss-(5)ID0EBCOBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The SMV emblem shall be affixed so that the view of the emblem is not obscured or obstructed by any part of the vehicle or any attachment designed for the vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-500ss-(6)ID0EBBOBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;<span class="Repealed">[Repealed, SOR/2014-307, s. 30]</span>
</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/2000-304, s. 6;</li>
<li> SOR/2005-42, ss. 11, 12;</li>
<li> SOR/2008-229, s. 3;</li>
<li> SOR/2011-238, s. 6;</li>
<li> SOR/2014-307, s. 30.</li>
</ul>

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Vehicle Stability</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>505</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-505ss-(1)ID0EBIMBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#xA0;(2), the height of the centre of mass, shown in Figure&#xA0;1, of a motor tricycle or a three-wheeled vehicle shall not exceed one and a half times the horizontal distance from the centre of mass to the nearest roll axis, shown in Figure&#xA0;2.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-505ss-(2)ID0EBHMBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Subsection&#xA0;(1) does not apply to a motor tricycle designed in such a way that it leans during a turning manoeuvre in the same direction as the turn.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-505ss-(3)ID0EBGMBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The total weight of a motor tricycle or three-wheeled vehicle on all its front wheels, as measured at the tire-ground interfaces, shall be not less than 25 per cent and not greater than 70 per cent of the loaded weight of that vehicle.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-505ss-(4)ID0EEFMBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The loaded weight of a motor tricycle or three-wheeled vehicle and the location of its centre of mass shall be determined under the following conditions:</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-505ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EBCFMBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the fuel tank is filled to any level from 90 to 95 per cent of the vehicle fuel tank capacity;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-505ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EBBFMBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a 50th percentile adult male anthropomorphic test device or an equivalent mass is located at every front outboard designated seating position but, if an equivalent mass is used, its centre of mass shall coincide, within 12&#xA0;mm in the vertical dimension and 12&#xA0;mm in the horizontal dimension, with a point 6&#xA0;mm below the position of the H-point as determined by using the equipment and procedures specified in SAE Standard J826, <cite class="XRefExternal">Devices for Use in Defining and Measuring Vehicle Seating Accommodation</cite> (July 1995), except that the length of the lower leg and thigh segments of the H-point machine shall be adjusted to 414&#xA0;mm and 401&#xA0;mm, respectively, instead of the 50th percentile values specified in Table 1 of that standard; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-505ss-(4)p-(c)ID0EBAFMBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;adjustable seats are placed in the adjustment position that is midway between the forward-most and rearmost positions and, if separately adjustable in a vertical direction, shall be at the lowest position but, if an adjustment position does not exist midway between the forward-most and rearmost positions, the closest adjustment position to the rear of the midpoint shall be used.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-505ss-(5)ID0ECEMBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For a motor tricycle or three-wheeled vehicle with one wheel at the front and two wheels at the rear, the horizontal distance from the centre of mass to the nearest roll axis, shown in Figure&#xA0;2, shall be determined using the equation</p>
<div class="Subsection">
<p class="Formula">d = L sin (arctan (t / 2W))</p>
<p class="FormulaGroup">where</p>
<dl class="FormulaDefinitionList">
<dt>
<dfn>d</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the horizontal distance from the centre of mass to the nearest roll axis;</dd>
<dt>
<dfn>L</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the longitudinal distance between the centre of mass and the centre of the front axle;</dd>
<dt>
<dfn>t</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the width of the wheel track of the rear axle; and</dd>
<dt>
<dfn>W</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the wheelbase.</dd>
</dl>
</div>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-505ss-(6)ID0ECDMBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;For a motor tricycle or three-wheeled vehicle with two wheels at the front and one wheel at the rear, the horizontal distance from the centre of mass to the nearest roll axis, shown in Figure&#xA0;2, shall be determined using the equation</p>
<div class="Subsection">
<p class="Formula">d = (W &#x2013; L) sin (arctan (t / 2W ))</p>
<p class="FormulaGroup">where</p>
<dl class="FormulaDefinitionList">
<dt>
<dfn>d</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the horizontal distance from the centre of mass to the nearest roll axis;</dd>
<dt>
<dfn>W</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the wheelbase;</dd>
<dt>
<dfn>L</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the longitudinal distance between the centre of mass and the centre of the front axle; and</dd>
<dt>
<dfn>t</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the width of the wheel track of the front axle.</dd>
</dl>
</div>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-505ss-(7)ID0EBCMBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Motor tricycles manufactured before September 1, 2004 need not comply with this section.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-505ss-ID0EDBMBA">
<span class="lawlabel">
</span>
</a>&#xA0;</p>
<table class="none">
<col class="width4">

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Axles</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>901</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(1)ID0EBDKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;No axle, axle assembly or wheel, tire, suspension or other hardware of an axle assembly commonly referred to as running gear that is designed and manufactured exclusively for use on a mobile home or other vehicle that is not of a class prescribed by the Regulations shall be fitted to a trailer.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(2)ID0EDCKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The gross axle weight rating for each axle with which a trailer is equipped shall not</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EGBCKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a vehicle equipped with demountable rims and spoke wheels, exceed the rated load carrying capacity of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(2)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBEBCKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the suspension springs,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(2)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBDBCKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the axle,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(2)p-(a)subp-(iii)ID0EBCBCKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the spoke wheels,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(2)p-(a)subp-(iv)ID0EBBBCKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iv)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the demountable rims, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(2)p-(a)subp-(v)ID0EBABCKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(v)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the tires; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EGACKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;in the case of a vehicle equipped with disc wheels and hubs, exceed the rated load-carrying capacity of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBEACKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the suspension springs,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBDACKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the axle,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(iii)ID0EBCACKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the hubs,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(iv)ID0EBBACKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iv)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the disc wheels, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(2)p-(b)subp-(v)ID0EBAACKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(v)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the tires.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(3)ID0EDBKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The rated load carrying capacity referred to in paragraphs&#xA0;2(<em>a</em>) and (<em>b</em>) for suspension springs, axles, hubs, disc wheels, spoke wheels, demountable rims or tires shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBBBKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be measured at the tire-ground interface; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-901ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBABKBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;except in the case of heavy hauler trailers, be the continuous service ratings supplied by the respective manufacturers of the suspension springs, axles, hubs, disc wheels, spoke wheels, demountable rims or tires.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/79-940, s. 10;</li>
<li> SOR/97-421, s. 14(E).</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="HistoricalNote">

<ul class="ProvisionList">

<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">C-dolly Specifications</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>903</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(1)ID0EFNGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every C-dolly shall be equipped with</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(1)p-(a)ID0EBDNGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;an automotive-type or a turntable-type self-steering mechanism;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(1)p-(b)ID0EBCNGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a means to return the wheels to within one degree of the straight-ahead position whenever any steering force applied to the wheels is removed;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(1)p-(c)ID0EBBNGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a device that automatically locks the steering mechanism in the straight-ahead position in the event of a failure of the means referred to in paragraph&#xA0;(<em>b</em>); and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(1)p-(d)ID0EEANGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a device</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(1)p-(d)subp-(i)ID0EBCANGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;that includes a switch by means of which the driver can, while seated in the normal driving position in the cab of the truck towing the C-dolly, lock the steering mechanism in the straight-ahead position, or unlock it,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(1)p-(d)subp-(ii)ID0EBBANGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;that locks the steering mechanism in the straight-ahead position in the event that the control for the device fails or the power supply to the device terminates, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(1)p-(d)subp-(iii)ID0EBAANGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;that includes, in both official languages, the information specified in subparagraphs&#xA0;(12)(<em>b</em>)(i) and (ii) on the switch referred in subparagraph&#xA0;(i) or on a label affixed near that switch.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(2)ID0EBMGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every C-dolly shall have a GAWR of 9&#xA0;100&#xA0;kg.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(3)ID0EBLGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The longitudinal distance on a C-dolly, measured on the longitudinal centre-line from a point aligned with the centre of the coupling to a point aligned with the centre of the axle, shall be no greater than 2 m.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(4)ID0EDKGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Where the coupling on a C-dolly consists of a single component, that coupling shall have</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(4)p-(a)ID0EDBKGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a static load rating of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(4)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBBBKGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;800&#xA0;kN in the longitudinal direction, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(4)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBABKGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;80&#xA0;kN in the lateral direction; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(4)p-(b)ID0EBAKGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a static moment rating of 76.2&#xA0;kN.m about the longitudinal axis of the C-dolly.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(5)ID0EFJGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(5)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Where the coupling on a C-dolly consists of two metal eyes, the two eyes shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(5)p-(a)ID0EBDJGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be separated laterally by a distance of 762&#xA0;mm &#xB1; 2&#xA0;mm;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(5)p-(b)ID0EBCJGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be equidistant from the longitudinal centre-line of the C-dolly;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(5)p-(c)ID0EBBJGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;have a mounting height of 900&#xA0;mm &#xB1; 10&#xA0;mm, when the C-dolly is not loaded; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(5)p-(d)ID0EEAJGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;each have a static load rating of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(5)p-(d)subp-(i)ID0EBCAJGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;400&#xA0;kN in the longitudinal direction,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(5)p-(d)subp-(ii)ID0EBBAJGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;100&#xA0;kN in the vertical direction, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(5)p-(d)subp-(iii)ID0EBAAJGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;40&#xA0;kN in the lateral direction.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(6)ID0EFIGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(6)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Where a C-dolly is tested in accordance with the <cite class="XRefExternal">Motor Vehicle Safety Test Methods, Section 903 - C-dolly</cite> (October&#xA0;1, 1992), published by the Department of Transport,</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(6)p-(a)ID0EBDIGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the axis of rotation of a turntable-type steering mechanism shall not deviate from the vertical by more than 0.5&#xA0;degree;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(6)p-(b)ID0EBCIGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the kingpin axes of an automotive-type steering mechanism shall not deviate from the vertical by more than 0.5&#xA0;degree;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(6)p-(c)ID0EDBIGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the steering mechanism shall keep the wheels within one degree of the straight-ahead position when the steering mechanism is subjected to</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(6)p-(c)subp-(i)ID0EBBBIGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a lateral force of 22&#xA0;320&#xA0;N that is applied to a point located 50&#xA0;mm behind the centre of the tire contact patch, or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(6)p-(c)subp-(ii)ID0EBABIGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a longitudinal force of 8&#xA0;930&#xA0;N that is applied through the centre of one of the tires in the case of a C-dolly that is equipped with one tire on each side, and through the centre of one of the dual tires and wheel assemblies in the case of a C-dolly that is equipped with two tires on each side; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(6)p-(d)ID0EBAIGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the steering mechanism shall not permit the wheels to move beyond one degree from the straight-ahead position unless the steering mechanism is subjected to a force exceeding the force referred to in subparagraph&#xA0;(<em>c</em>)(i) or (ii).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(7)ID0EEHGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(7)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Where a C-dolly is equipped with a pressurized hydraulic or pneumatic system that provides the means referred to in paragraph&#xA0;(1)(<em>b</em>), the system shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(7)p-(a)ID0EBCHGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be independent of the brake system of the C-dolly;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(7)p-(b)ID0EDBHGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be fitted with a pressure gauge that indicates</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(7)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBBHGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the minimum pressure required to meet the requirements of paragraphs&#xA0;(1)(<em>b</em>) and (6)(<em>c</em>) and (<em>d</em>), and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(7)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBABHGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;the amount of pressure in the system; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(7)p-(c)ID0EBAHGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;not permit any adjustment of the steering force.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(8)ID0EBGGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(8)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every C-dolly referred to in subsection&#xA0;(7) shall bear a label, in both official languages, that states the minimum pressure referred to in paragraph&#xA0;(7)(<em>b</em>).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(9)ID0EBFGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(9)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every pressure gauge referred to in subsection&#xA0;(7) and every manual valve and switch, if any, that forms part of a system referred to in that subsection, and every label referred to in subsection&#xA0;(8), shall be protected from adverse weather conditions.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(10)ID0EBEGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(10)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every C-dolly that is subjected to a torsion test conducted in accordance with the <cite class="XRefExternal">Motor Vehicle Safety Test Methods, Section 903 - C-dolly</cite> (October&#xA0;1, 1992), published by the Department of Transport, shall have a torsional stiffness of at least 3&#xA0;000&#xA0;N.m/degree with respect to the longitudinal direction, and shall be capable of sustaining a torque of at least 45&#xA0;000&#xA0;N.m in either direction without incurring a residual deformation that exceeds 0.5&#xA0;degree.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(11)ID0EDDGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(11)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Where a C-dolly is equipped with a device that is intended to lock the steering mechanism automatically according to the speed of the C-dolly, that device shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(11)p-(a)ID0EBBDGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;lock the steering mechanism in the straight-ahead position when the C-dolly is travelling at a speed of 60&#xA0;km/h and keep the steering mechanism locked when the C-dolly is travelling at a speed greater than 60&#xA0;km/h; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(11)p-(b)ID0EBADGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;unlock the steering mechanism when the C-dolly is travelling at a speed of 50&#xA0;km/h and keep the steering mechanism unlocked when the C-dolly is travelling at a speed less than 50&#xA0;km/h.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(12)ID0EDCGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(12)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every C-dolly shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(12)p-(a)ID0EBBCGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;have a flat surface that is horizontal when the C-dolly is not loaded and when the centre of the coupling on the C-dolly is held at the mounting height in accordance with the manufacturer&#x2019;s design; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(12)p-(b)ID0EDACGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;bear a label, in both official languages, that states</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(12)p-(b)subp-(i)ID0EBBACGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;that the steering mechanism should be locked when the C-dolly is travelling at a speed of 60&#xA0;km/h or more on any slippery or unpaved road, and that the steering mechanism should be unlocked when the C-dolly is travelling at a speed of 50&#xA0;km/h or less, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(12)p-(b)subp-(ii)ID0EBAACGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;that the C-dolly shall not be attached to a straight truck.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(13)ID0EFBGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(13)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The flat surface referred to in paragraph&#xA0;(12)(<em>a</em>) shall be</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(13)p-(a)ID0EBDBGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at least 30&#xA0;cm in length, measured longitudinally;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(13)p-(b)ID0EBCBGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;at least 5&#xA0;cm in width, measured laterally;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(13)p-(c)ID0EBBBGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;accessible from both sides of the C-dolly; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-903ss-(13)p-(d)ID0EBABGBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;within 50&#xA0;cm of the coupling of the C-dolly.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/93-146, s. 4;</li>
<li> SOR/2008-104, s. 22.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">C-dolly Hitch Requirements</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>904</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(1)ID0EBDEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every trailer that is designed to tow a C-dolly shall be equipped with a coupling to connect the trailer to the C-dolly.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(2)ID0EDCEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Where a coupling referred to in subsection&#xA0;(1) consists of a single component, the coupling shall have</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(2)p-(a)ID0EDBCEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a static load rating of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(2)p-(a)subp-(i)ID0EBBBCEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;800&#xA0;kN in the longitudinal direction, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(2)p-(a)subp-(ii)ID0EBABCEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;80&#xA0;kN in the lateral direction; and</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(2)p-(b)ID0EBACEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;a static moment rating of 76.2&#xA0;kN.m about the longitudinal axis of the C-dolly.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(3)ID0EFBEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Where a coupling referred to in subsection&#xA0;(1) consists of two separate hitches, the hitches shall</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(3)p-(a)ID0EBDBEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be separated laterally by a distance of 762&#xA0;mm &#xB1; 2&#xA0;mm;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(3)p-(b)ID0EBCBEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;be equidistant from the longitudinal centre-line of the trailer;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(3)p-(c)ID0EBBBEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(c)</span>
</a>&#xA0;have a mounting height of 900&#xA0;mm &#xB1; 10&#xA0;mm, when the trailer is not loaded; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(3)p-(d)ID0EEABEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(d)</span>
</a>&#xA0;each have a static load rating of</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(3)p-(d)subp-(i)ID0EBCABEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(i)</span>
</a>&#xA0;400&#xA0;kN in the longitudinal direction,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(3)p-(d)subp-(ii)ID0EBBABEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(ii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;100&#xA0;kN in the vertical direction, and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subparagraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-904ss-(3)p-(d)subp-(iii)ID0EBAABEBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(iii)</span>
</a>&#xA0;40&#xA0;kN in the lateral direction.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/93-146, s. 4;</li>
<li> SOR/2008-104, s. 23.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Trailer Cargo Anchoring Devices (Standard&#xA0;905)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<strong>905</strong>&#xA0;<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-905ss-(1)ID0EEECBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(1)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The definitions in this subsection apply in this section.</p>
<dl class="Definition">
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>bulkhead</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>bulkhead</dfn>
</span> means a fixed or removable structure installed across the width of a trailer to restrict the movement of cargo during transport. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">cloison</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>cargo anchoring device</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>cargo anchoring device</dfn>
</span> means a fitting or attachment point on a trailer, other than a bulkhead or rub rail, to which a tie-down assembly is attached. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">dispositif d&#x2019;ancrage des chargements</span>) </p>
</dd>
<dt>
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>rub rail</dfn>
</span>
</dt>
<dd>
<p class="Definition">
<span class="DefinedTerm">
<dfn>rub rail</dfn>
</span> means a protector strip extending horizontally along the sides of a trailer intended to provide protection from scuffing. (<span class="DefinedTermLink" lang="fr">bourrelet de protection</span>) </p>
</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-905ss-(2)ID0EBDCBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(2)</span>
</a>&#xA0;This section applies to every trailer that is designed to carry cargo, with a GVWR of 10&#xA0;000&#xA0;kg or more, a load-carrying mainframe and loading deck and no permanent sides or roof, such as a flatbed trailer, heavy hauler trailer, industrial trailer, lowbed trailer or drop-centre trailer.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-905ss-(3)ID0ECCCBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(3)</span>
</a>&#xA0;Every trailer shall, for the purpose of affixing cargo, be equipped with at least the number of cargo anchoring devices determined in accordance with the formula</p>
<div class="Subsection">
<p class="Formula">N = M / 2&#xA0;000&#xA0;kg</p>
<p class="FormulaGroup">where</p>
<dl class="FormulaDefinitionList">
<dt>
<dfn>N</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the minimum number of cargo anchoring devices, rounded up to the next even whole number; and</dd>
<dt>
<dfn>M</dfn>&#xA0;</dt>
<dd>is the cargo carrying capacity of the trailer, calculated as the difference between its gross vehicle weight rating and its curb mass, expressed in kilograms.</dd>
</dl>
</div>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Subsection">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-905ss-(4)ID0EBBCBA">
<span class="lawlabel">(4)</span>
</a>&#xA0;The minimum number of cargo anchoring devices determined in accordance with subsection&#xA0;(3) shall, when tested in accordance with <cite class="XRefExternal">Test Method 905-Trailer Cargo Anchoring Devices</cite> (August 1998), withstand a force of at least 67&#xA0;000&#xA0;N applied in an upward vertical direction.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/98-595, s. 2.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="SchedHeadL2">
<span class="HTitleText2">Snowmobile Trailers (Standard&#xA0;906)</span>
</h3>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Section">
<strong>906</strong>&#xA0;Every snowmobile trailer shall be equipped with</p>
<ul class="ProvisionList">
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-906p-(a)ID0EBCABA">
<span class="lawlabel">(a)</span>
</a>&#xA0;one or more tie-down cross bars located in such a manner as to be capable of clamping the skis of as many snowmobiles as the trailer is capable of carrying; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p class="Paragraph">
<a class="lawLabel" id="ScheduleRegulationPieces-906p-(b)ID0EBBABA">
<span class="lawlabel">(b)</span>
</a>&#xA0;tie-down points to which each snowmobile can be secured by ropes or straps and that are of sufficient strength to withstand a force of 2&#xA0;224.11&#xA0;N (500&#xA0;pounds) applied separately from any direction to each tie-down point.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="HistoricalNote">
<ul class="HistoricalNote">
<li>SOR/2003-359, s. 4.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
